## Deferred (tracked, non-blocking)

### Q-36-OQ1-BE12-TEMPLATE-AUTHORING
BE-12 is NOT in v1 — confirm EC-5a, do not build POST/PATCH/DELETE/clone. Grounding (not taste): `grep -c structure_template services/composition-service/app/mcp/server.py` = 0 — NO MCP tool authors a structure template either, so this is not a GG-1 gap (no capability is trapped behind the chat window); it is a NEW product capability, outside plan 30's tool↔GUI-parity charter. PO may veto this default at QC; if they do, the build contract is spelled out in the defer row.

CONCRETE BUILDER INSTRUCTION for M4a (Composition section, Story-structure control) — nothing here stalls:
1. Render the picker as a plain `<select>` fed by the EXISTING `listTemplates()` (`frontend/src/features/composition/api.ts:270` → `GET /templates`, `services/composition-service/app/routers/canon.py:192-199`). It lists the 6 System-tier built-ins (`owner_user_id IS NULL`, seeded `migrate.py:1790-1801`). On change → `PATCH /works/{project_id} {active_template_id}` with `If-Match` (EC-5 makes `active_template_id` the one home; spec 36 L389).
2. The "honest empty affordance" (EC-5a) is a STATIC NOTE, not a control: below the select render one line — i18n key `composition.settings.structure.customUnavailable` = "Custom story structures aren't supported yet — these 6 built-in structures are the full library." with `data-testid="structure-template-custom-note"`. Do NOT ship a disabled "Save as template" / "New template" button and do NOT ship a button that opens nothing — that is the repo's `silent-success-is-a-bug` / no-silent-no-op class. Zero write affordance, one honest sentence.
3. Do NOT modify `StructureTemplatesRepo`. Its `list_for_user` (structure_templates.py:32-40) and `get` (:43-51) already union `owner_user_id IS NULL OR owner_user_id = $1` and already 404-not-leak another user's row, so when BE-12 eventually lands the read + tenancy path needs zero change. The dead `= $1` branch is forward-compat, not a bug — leave it.
4. Test for M4a: assert the select renders exactly the 6 built-ins, that choosing one PATCHes `active_template_id` (and a stale same-key PATCH 412s), and that `structure-template-custom-note` is present while NO create/edit/delete control exists in the section.
5. Write the defer row below into `docs/deferred/DEFERRED.md` + SESSION_HANDOFF as part of M4a's DoD.

**Defer row:** **D-STRUCTURE-TEMPLATE-AUTHORING** | origin: Wave/M4a (spec 36 EC-5a / OQ-1) | **What:** user-authored `structure_template`s — `POST /templates`, `PATCH|DELETE /templates/{id}`, `POST /templates/{id}/clone`, plus the FE authoring surface. | **Gate reason: #5 conscious won't-fix** (scoped-out product capability, not a parity gap — verified: `structure_template` appears in **0** MCP tools, so no capability is agent-only and plan 30's GG-1 law does not require the surface; the 6 built-ins reachable = the whole library today). Secondary: #1 out-of-scope (plan 30 closes tool↔GUI gaps; this adds a new capability). **NOT deferred as "blocked"** — the routes are writable in this repo today; this is a deliberate scope call the PO may veto at QC. | **Target/trigger:** the first real request for a custom story structure, OR the moment any MCP tool gains a structure_template write (that would instantly make it a GG-1 violation and force the GUI). | **Build contract when it lands (binding, so it is never re-litigated):** (a) CLONE-TO-USER ONLY — `POST /templates/{id}/clone` inserts a new row with `owner_user_id = caller`, copying name/kind/beats; (b) `PATCH`/`DELETE` MUST return **403** (not 404) when the target row has `owner_user_id IS NULL` — a regular user never mutates a System-tier row (the `entity_kinds` bug; CLAUDE.md User Boundaries); (c) every write filters `WHERE id=$1 AND owner_user_id=$2`; (d) uniqueness, if any, is `UNIQUE(owner_user_id, name)` — never `UNIQUE(name)`; (e) required test: user A cannot PATCH/DELETE a built-in (403) and cannot see/mutate user B's custom template (404); (f) the slice carries its own tenancy review + `/review-impl`.

### Q-36-DEFERRED-BE12-TEMPLATE-AUTHORING
BE-12 (structure_template authoring) is OUT of v1 — DEFER, adopting spec 36's own EC-5a/OQ-1 recommendation. This is NOT the "missing infrastructure = blocked" lazy tell: the code proves no writer exists on EITHER side of the loop — no REST write route (canon.py:192-199 is the only route, a GET), no MCP write tool (composition mcp/server.py has only composition_arc_extract_template/composition_arc_template_drift, unrelated to structure_template), no FE writer (api.ts:270 is a read). Therefore template authoring is not an agent-only capability hidden from the human (which GG-1 would force us to surface) — it is a capability that does not exist at all. GG-1 obligates a human surface for capabilities the user ALREADY owns; there is nothing to surface. It is net-new feature scope, and the honest cost is not "3 routes" — it is a beats-array authoring editor (add/rename/reorder beat objects in the `beats` JSONB, migrate.py:183) plus a clone-to-user tenancy tier with its own tenancy review.

CONCRETE BUILDER INSTRUCTION for this run (do exactly this, nothing more):
1. BACKEND — change nothing. Do NOT add POST/PATCH/DELETE/clone routes. `StructureTemplatesRepo` stays two methods. Edit its module docstring (services/composition-service/app/db/repositories/structure_templates.py:4-5) to replace the vague "Read-only in V0 (custom-template authoring is a later surface)" with the tracked ID and the tenancy law that any future writer MUST obey: "Read-only — user-authored templates are DEFERRED (D-STRUCTURE-TEMPLATE-AUTHORING). When BE-12 is built it MUST be CLONE-TO-USER: a write sets owner_user_id = caller; it must NEVER UPDATE/DELETE a row WHERE owner_user_id IS NULL (System tier — the entity_kinds bug, CLAUDE.md User Boundaries)."
2. FRONTEND (M4a picker) — the picker consumes GET /v1/composition/templates (frontend/src/features/composition/api.ts:270 via hooks/usePlanner.ts:11) and renders the 6 System built-ins; the list is already correctly ordered built-ins-first (`ORDER BY owner_user_id NULLS FIRST, name`, structure_templates.py:36-37). Where a "save my own structure" control would go, render an HONEST STATIC HINT — plain text, e.g. "Custom structures aren't available yet — pick a built-in." NO disabled button, NO create/save control of any kind. A dead or no-op affordance would be this repo's own `silent-success-is-a-bug` class shipped into the picker; a truthful sentence is not.
3. TEST (this is the DoD, not a checkbox) — one FE test on the picker: (a) asserts all 6 built-ins render; (b) asserts the hint string renders; (c) asserts the picker exposes NO enabled or disabled create/save/clone control (query by role button and assert none matches a create/save affordance). Per the run policy, `/review-impl` runs at wave close and any bug it finds is fixed before the wave closes.
4. Do NOT drop the nullable `owner_user_id` column or the owner index — the tier stays advertised because BE-12 will land there; the defer row is what keeps it honest.

PO VETO NOTE: the sane default I picked is "6 built-ins reachable = 90% of the value; nobody has asked to author their own." If the PO wants authoring in v1, the veto is cheap and localized — it adds one slice (repo create/update/delete/clone + 4 routes on canon.py + a beats editor + a tenancy test asserting a regular user gets 403/404 on an owner_user_id IS NULL row). Nothing in this run's plan is built in a way that would have to be undone.

**Defer row:** | `D-STRUCTURE-TEMPLATE-AUTHORING` | origin: spec 36 (editor craft ports) / M4a structure picker slice | **What:** `structure_template` has an advertised user-custom tier (`owner_user_id` nullable, migrate.py:179-187) and zero write paths — no REST route (canon.py:192-199 is a lone GET), no MCP tool, no FE writer. Every user sees only the 6 System-tier built-ins, forever. BE-12 = `POST /templates` · `PATCH|DELETE /templates/{id}` · `POST /templates/{id}/clone`, plus a beats-array authoring editor, plus a clone-to-user tenancy tier. | **Gate: #1 (out of scope) + #2 (large/structural).** #1 — spec 36 ports EXISTING craft GUIs; there is no existing capability here to surface, so GG-1 is not violated (nothing is agent-only; nothing exists). #2 — the real work is a beats-JSONB authoring editor + a clone-to-user tenancy design needing its own tenancy review, not 3 CRUD routes. Explicitly NOT gate #4: this is buildable in-repo, it is scoped out, not blocked. | **Target: a future authoring wave, triggered by an actual user request to author a custom structure.** Hard constraint for whoever builds it: CLONE-TO-USER ONLY — set `owner_user_id` = caller; NEVER UPDATE/DELETE a row `WHERE owner_user_id IS NULL` (System tier; the `entity_kinds` bug, CLAUDE.md User Boundaries). v1 mitigation already shipped: the M4a picker renders an honest static "custom structures aren't available yet" hint — no dead/no-op control. |

## Decisions

### Q-36-SPEC-APPROVAL-GATE
APPROVED IN FULL — answer (a), no scope cuts. The plan-30 PO-4 hold is a phase gate whose exit condition ("once every spec and draft is on disk") is SATISFIED: specs 31–38 all exist on disk (dated 2026-07-12/13, several adversarially reviewed) and all 24 HTML drafts exist under design-drafts/screens/studio/, including spec 36's two (screen-style-voice-references.html, screen-divergence.html). This QC adjudication IS the gate the PO named ("after this QC gate, implementation proceeds autonomously with no further design checkpoints"), so no further approval exists to wait for.

BUILDER INSTRUCTION (do exactly this):
1. First commit of Wave 6: edit docs/specs/2026-07-01-writing-studio/36_editor_craft_ports.md line 3 — replace "📐 SPEC (written 2026-07-13, PO-approval pending) — buildable. **No implementation this phase** (plan 30 PO-4)." with "✅ APPROVED 2026-07-13 (QC gate) — BUILDABLE. Wave 6 of plan 30. PO-4's specs-first hold is SATISFIED (31–38 + all drafts on disk) and LIFTED. Approved in FULL — no scope cuts; M4b/BE-20 is IN."
2. Build all of M1→M5 as written in §Milestones (spec 36:562-573). M4b is NOT cut — per the spec's own OQ-3, "Build BE-20; porting a known cost-gate hole onto a new surface is self-refuting." Dropping it would ship a Decompose button that spends the user's tokens with no 402 precheck — the paid-action-defect class this run treats as a critical blocker.
3. Hard prerequisite, unchanged: Wave 0 (X-1 AddModelCta · X-2 CATEGORY_ORDER · X-3 guideBodyKey · X-4 Lane-B handlers · X-5 ui_show_panel retirement, per plan 30 PO-3) lands BEFORE M1. Spec 36:11 declares it.
4. Carried constraints (NOT re-litigated): M5 ships the parity contract test ONLY — do NOT delete ChapterEditorPage in this wave (spec 36 §10 recommendation + OQ-2 + plan 30 GG-4). Its retirement is a separate PO call after M6 (mobile).
5. Per run policy, /review-impl runs at the close of Wave 6 and any bug it finds is fixed before the wave closes.

DEFAULT NOTED FOR PO VETO: I chose (a)-full over (c)-with-cuts. If the PO wants M4b (the cost-gated Decompose action, BE-20 = MCP composition_decompose + descriptor + _claim_or_replay/_precheck_or_402) pushed to a later wave, that is a one-line cut — M4 is already split precisely so M4b is severable and nothing else in the wave depends on it.

### Q-36-OQ2-CHAPTEREDITORPAGE-DELETE
KEEP `ChapterEditorPage` — answer (a). It stays as the deprecated, URL-only fallback, exactly as spec 16 Phase 4b sealed it on 2026-07-05. The build proceeds on that assumption; no re-authorization is needed because nothing was ever de-authorized. Deletion is NOT in this wave and is NOT queued for a later one — it is a closed decision that only a fresh PO call may reopen, and the code gives that call a hard prerequisite (M6/mobile) it does not yet have.

CONCRETE BUILDER INSTRUCTIONS (no further thought required):

1. DO NOT delete `frontend/src/pages/ChapterEditorPage.tsx`. DO NOT remove the route at `frontend/src/App.tsx:134` (`/books/:bookId/chapters/:chapterId/edit`). DO NOT add a redirect. DO NOT touch the deprecation banner at `ChapterEditorPage.tsx:1-18` (it is the standing decision's record).

2. DO NOT write `frontend/src/__tests__/legacyEditorRouteRetired.test.tsx` (spec 36 §GG-4's second test). Spec 36 itself says it "lands WITH the deletion, not before." There is no deletion. Skip it entirely.

3. DO NOT touch `editorBridge` / `registerEditorTarget` / `getEditorTarget`. It has 12 referencing files and its death is coupled to the page's death. Keeping the page keeps the singleton — that is the accepted, recorded cost. Do not open a "while we're here" refactor.

4. M5 (the GG-4 gate) SHIPS, and ships in its GREEN-with-UNPORTED-rows form. Write `frontend/src/features/studio/panels/__tests__/legacyParityContract.test.ts` exactly as spec 36 §GG-4 sketches: map all 25 `CompositionPanel` sub-tabs to a Studio panel id, or to `{ retired: '<reason >20 chars>' }`. Its purpose is now a machine-checked INVENTORY of what is still legacy-only, not a pre-deletion gate. Rows for capabilities this wave ports assert `OPENABLE_STUDIO_PANEL_IDS` contains the id; rows not yet ported may carry an `{ unported: '<reason>' }` variant — the test must PASS while listing them, never red-list the build. The hygiene grep for `ChapterEditorPage` imports (the second `it()` in the sketch) is DROPPED with item 2 — do not write it (and note it would false-positive on prose anyway, per the repo's own `hygiene-grep-literal-token-in-comment-false-positive` lesson).

5. EC-3c's legacy-4 `candidates[0]` fixes ARE IN SCOPE — all twelve sites, not seven. Because the page is not deleted, leaving the legacy 4 on `candidates[0]` ships the wrong-Work bug on a surface we are refusing to delete. Replace `candidates[0]` with the shared `selectCanonicalWork(candidates)` / `selectDerivatives(candidates)` helper (`frontend/src/features/composition/workSelect.ts`, predicate `!w.source_work_id`) at the 7 studio sites AND at the legacy 4: `features/composition/components/CompositionPanel.tsx:156`, `features/composition/components/OutlineTree.tsx:118`, `features/composition/hooks/usePublishGate.ts:51`, `pages/ChapterEditorPage.tsx:218` — plus the server-side predicate at `services/composition-service/app/routers/internal_model_settings.py:85`. This is the ONE place the "keep" decision makes MORE work, and it is non-negotiable: item 1 is why item 5 exists.

6. When the wave closes, file the standing constraint (do not silently drop it): "Deleting `ChapterEditorPage` requires an M6/mobile answer FIRST, because `ChapterEditorPage.tsx:844` is the only non-test consumer of `MobileEditorShell` and Studio has no mobile editing surface." Record it as a defer row (gate #4 — genuinely blocked on a PO product decision, not on unbuilt infrastructure), target trigger = "M6 mobile shell decided."

DEFAULT NOTED FOR PO VETO: I am treating "keep" as already-sealed rather than reopened. If the PO actually wants deletion, that is a separate effort whose first slice is building a Studio mobile editing shell — not a line item in this wave.

*Evidence:* frontend/src/pages/ChapterEditorPage.tsx:1-18 — banner: "a decision to keep it around, not a decision pending removal (spec 16 Phase 4b, 2026-07-05: kept indefinitely, not deleted)." · frontend/src/pages/ChapterEditorPage.tsx:844 — the ONLY non-test consumer of MobileEditorShell (verified: `grep -rn "MobileEditorShell" frontend/src` returns just this line + its own test file), so deletion removes the product's only mobile chapter-editing surface while Studio has none (features/studio/hooks/useStudioChrome.ts only collapses the sidebar on mobile). · frontend/src/App.tsx:134 — route still mounted. · `grep -rln editorBridge frontend/src` → 12 files, all coupled to the page's lifetime. · docs/specs/2026-07-01-writing-studio/16_chapter_editor_parity_and_retirement.md:133-135 (Phase 4b, "kept indefinitely") and 30_TOOL_GUI_GAP_AUDIT_AND_PLAN.md GG-4 ("do NOT retire ChapterEditorPage before the ports land") — both agree with the code.

### Q-36-OQ5-BOOK-TIER-CASCADE-UNEXERCISED
DECIDED — keep the live-smoke, but the spec's version of it is wrong on three counts and would have burned the builder. Also DOWNGRADE the premise: the Book tier is NOT unexercised.

**(a) The premise is half-false — say so in the spec.** The Book-tier transport (chat-service -> composition /internal -> grant check -> resolve_by_book -> resolver) is ALREADY LIVE in production. `_model_roles_from_settings` DUAL-READS the legacy scalar `settings.default_model_ref` into role `chat` (internal_model_settings.py:59-61), and `default_model_ref` HAS a real GUI writer today: CompositionSettingsView.tsx:47 `patch({ default_model_ref: e.target.value })` -> `compositionApi.patchWork` (useWork.ts:135). A book with a default drafter model already resolves `models.chat.source_tier === 'book'`. M4a is NOT the first writer of the Book tier — it is the first writer of the `model_roles` KEY and of the `composer`/`planner`/`critic` roles. This is therefore a *partially* new contract, not a virgin one. Rewrite OQ-5 in spec 36 to say this (a stale in-code/in-spec claim is how the next agent re-derives the wrong thing).

**(b) FIX THE SMOKE COMMAND — the spec names a route that does not exist.** Spec says `GET /v1/chat/ai-settings/effective`. The real route is `GET /v1/chat/effective-settings?book_id=<uuid>` (chat-service/app/routers/ai_settings.py:34, mounted main.py:175). Copied verbatim it 404s and the builder "fixes" a resolver that was never broken. Correct it in the spec text.

**(c) The smoke is a TWO-LEG smoke. Leg A alone ships the headline bug.** Write it as a repeatable script (`services/chat-service/scripts/smoke_book_tier_cascade.py`, following the composition-service/scripts/eval_*.py pattern), run it as the CLAUDE.md test account, and paste its stdout into M4a's VERIFY evidence as `live smoke: book-tier cascade <one-liner>`:
  - LEG A (the resolver): resolve a REAL active model — `SELECT user_model_id FROM user_models WHERE owner_user_id='019d5e3c-7cc5-7e6a-8b27-1344e148bf7c' AND is_active` — then PATCH the book's canonical Work settings with `model_roles.critic = {"model_ref": "<that uuid>", "model_source": "user_model"}` (whole-blob merge: `patchWork` spreads `{...currentSettings, ...patch}`, so a partial PATCH CLOBBERS — spread current settings). Then `GET /v1/chat/effective-settings?book_id=<uuid>` and assert ALL THREE: `models.critic.source_tier === "book"`, `models.critic.effective_value.model_ref === <that uuid>`, and `"book" NOT IN models.critic.skipped`.
  - LEG B (the consumer that actually matters — this is what makes M4a true rather than a write-only editor): run the critique on that book with a drafter `model_ref` DIFFERENT from the critic ref, and assert the response body does NOT contain `"critique skipped: no distinct critic model configured"` and `critic` is populated. **Leg B is red until BE-21 lands**, because composition-service's engine reads `model_roles` NOWHERE — the critic gate reads the legacy scalar `settings_dict.get("critic_model_ref")` at engine.py:1643-1649 (and 6 sibling sites). Leg A green + Leg B red IS the `silent-success-is-a-bug` / stored-but-unread shape, shipped by the spec that cites the rule. Treat Leg B as the pass condition of M4a's DoD, not a bonus.

**(d) Two traps to write into the smoke script's docstring so a 3am builder does not misread a correct result as a bug:**
  1. Liveness is OWNER-SCOPED and it silently demotes. `resolve_model_role` liveness-checks EVERY tier; `ProviderRegistryClient.is_live` -> `resolve(model_source, model_ref, user_id)` -> a 404 raises ValueError -> `False` -> the book tier is SKIPPED (recorded in `skipped[]`) and resolution falls through to Account (provider_client.py:47-62). So a placeholder/fake ref — exactly what the existing unit test injects, the literal string `"book-model"` at test_ai_settings_router.py:170 — produces `source_tier: "account"`, `skipped: ["book"]`. That is the resolver working CORRECTLY, not a broken cascade. The ref MUST be a `user_model_id` that the CALLING user owns and that is active. (Note `is_live` fails OPEN on any non-404 exception, so a flaky provider-registry will not demote — only a genuine 404 will.)
  2. `book_id` MUST be a well-formed UUID: the composition route signature is `book_id: UUID` (internal_model_settings.py:71), and `CompositionClient.get_book_model_roles` swallows EVERYTHING into `{}` (composition_client.py:44-47) — so a non-UUID book_id yields a silent no-book-override, indistinguishable from "no model set". The existing test at test_ai_settings_router.py:79 passes `book_id=abc` and relies on exactly this.

**(e) Why the unit suite cannot substitute (quote in the wave DoD):** the only existing Book-tier test monkeypatches a `_FakeComposition` client (test_ai_settings_router.py:161-178). That mock encodes the author's assumption of the contract — it cannot catch the wrong route path, the owner-scoped liveness demotion, or the fact that the engine never reads what the panel writes. `new-cross-service-contract-needs-consumer-live-smoke` + `mocked-client-hides-server-side-default-filters`.

Default I am picking (veto-able): the smoke lands as a committed script, not a hand-run curl, so it is re-runnable at every later wave that touches the cascade. Per PO policy 2, `/review-impl` runs at M4a's wave close and any bug it finds is fixed before the wave closes.

*Evidence:* services/chat-service/app/routers/ai_settings.py:34 — `effective_router = APIRouter(prefix="/v1/chat/effective-settings")` (the spec's `/v1/chat/ai-settings/effective` does NOT exist; mounted at main.py:175). services/composition-service/app/routers/internal_model_settings.py:59-63 — dual-read: `dmr = settings.get("default_model_ref")` -> `roles["chat"]`, so the Book tier already has a live writer. frontend/src/features/composition/components/CompositionSettingsView.tsx:47 — `onChange={(e) => patch({ default_model_ref: e.target.value })}` = that live writer (via useWork.ts:135 `patchWork` whole-blob merge). services/chat-service/app/client/provider_client.py:47-62 — `is_live` -> `resolve(model_source, model_ref, user_id)`; ValueError (404) => False => tier skipped (owner-scoped demotion trap); non-404 => True (fails open). services/chat-service/app/services/settings_resolution.py:161-196 — `resolve_model_role` liveness-validates EVERY tier and records `skipped`. services/composition-service/app/routers/engine.py:1643-1655 — `critic_ref = settings_dict.get("critic_model_ref")` -> `"critique skipped: no distinct critic model configured"`: the engine reads the LEGACY scalar, never `model_roles` (F-EC4b — Leg B of the smoke is red until BE-21). services/chat-service/tests/test_ai_settings_router.py:161-178 — the only Book-tier test injects `_FakeComposition` with the fake ref `"book-model"`.

### Q-36-OQ4-REFERENCE-COUNT-N
MEASURED: N = 0. The dev DB has ZERO references (`reference_source`: 0 rows, 0 works, 0 books) across 12 `composition_work` rows, and ZERO works have `reference_embed_model_ref` set in `settings`. The reference-shelf has never been used, so there is no "typical N" — and therefore NO CONSTANT IS HONEST. Baking any number into EC-2a's copy ("re-embeds all ~50") would fabricate the very figure the clause exists to make truthful.

BUILDER INSTRUCTION (M2, `reference-shelf`) — make N LIVE, not literal. The data is already there: `ReferencesRepo.list()` has no LIMIT (references.py:99-108) and LIST returns the full `references[]` array + `embed_model_set` (references.py:88-94), so `references.length` IS the exact N for that Work at render time. Do all three:

1. `frontend/src/features/studio/panels/ReferenceShelfPanel.tsx` — the embed-model header row branches on `embed_model_set`, and the count comes from `refs.data.references.length`. NEVER hardcode a number, and NEVER render "re-embed all 0 references" (the true state for every Work today — it reads as a bug):
   - `embed_model_set === false` → `panels.reference-shelf.embedModelUnset`: "No embedding model yet — the first reference you add sets it for this work, permanently."
   - `embed_model_set === true` → `panels.reference-shelf.embedModelLocked` with `{{count}}` = `references.length`, i18n plural (`_one` / `_other`): "{{count}} reference in this work is embedded with {{model}}; changing the model would re-embed it." / "All {{count}} references in this work are embedded with {{model}}; changing the model would re-embed all {{count}}."
2. `frontend/src/i18n/locales/en/studio.json` — add those two keys under `panels.reference-shelf.*` (spec 36 §"i18n" row 3 already reserves that namespace). Use i18next `count` pluralization; do not concatenate a bare number into an English sentence.
3. TEST (M2 DoD): a vitest on `ReferenceShelfPanel` asserting (a) with `embed_model_set:false, references:[]` the panel renders `embedModelUnset` and the string "0" appears nowhere in the header row; (b) with `embed_model_set:true` and 3 refs, the header interpolates "3". That test is what makes the copy honest-by-construction instead of honest-by-a-number-someone-measured-once.

BE-17 (deferred to v2, D-REF-UPDATE-AND-MODEL-SURFACE) is likewise UNBLOCKED by this: its re-embed cost estimate does not need a global N either — it computes cost per-Work from the actual row count at call time, bounded by the existing `content` cap of 20,000 chars/reference (references.py:50). Nothing about BE-17 was waiting on this measurement.

DEFAULT I PICKED (veto-able): I chose live interpolation over "measure once and hardcode" because the measurement returned 0, which makes hardcoding impossible to do honestly. If the PO would rather ship a static sentence with no number at all ("changing the model would re-embed every reference in this work"), that is also honest and is a strictly smaller change — but it hides the cost the clause was written to reveal, so live count is the better default. Either way, OQ-4 is CLOSED: the spec can drop its UNVERIFIED tag.

*Evidence:* MEASUREMENT (docker exec infra-postgres-1 psql -U loreweave -d loreweave_composition):
  SELECT count(*), count(DISTINCT project_id), count(DISTINCT book_id) FROM reference_source; → 0 | 0 | 0
  SELECT count(*), count(*) FILTER (WHERE settings ? 'reference_embed_model_ref') FROM composition_work; → 12 | 0

GROUNDING CODE:
  services/composition-service/app/db/repositories/references.py:99-108 — `list()` is `SELECT ... WHERE project_id=$1 ORDER BY created_at DESC` with NO LIMIT → the FE receives every row, so `references.length` is the exact N.
  services/composition-service/app/routers/references.py:88-94 — LIST returns `{"references": [...], "embed_model_set": reference_embed_model(work.settings) is not None}` → both the count AND the branch condition are already on the wire; no new route needed.
  services/composition-service/app/routers/references.py:50 — `content: max_length=20000` → the per-reference upper bound BE-17's cost estimate multiplies by the live count.
  services/composition-service/app/routers/references.py:54-57,134-137 — the model is set on first add and thereafter immutable ("a differing value here is ignored") → confirms the one-way door EC-2a's sentence must disclose.
  frontend/src/features/composition/components/ReferencesPanel.tsx:76 — existing `references-no-embed-model` warning div, the element the new header row sits beside.
  docs/specs/2026-07-01-writing-studio/36_editor_craft_ports.md:693 — OQ-4 ("Measure on the dev DB before writing the copy. Owner: builder") — measured; now closed.

### Q-36-OQ6-SHELF-VS-GROUNDING-SPLIT
THE SPLIT STANDS — confirmed by code, and it is stronger than the spec's framing. The question's premise ("the pinned references that GroundingPanel shows") is false: GroundingPanel does NOT show reference items at all. It hard-filters them (GroundingPanel.tsx:13 `ADDRESSABLE = ['present','canon','lore']`; :17 `ITEM_GROUPS` excludes 'reference'; :14-15 comment says exactly why), even though the backend DOES emit `type:"reference"` rows into `grounding_items` (pack.py:702). The shelf is the ONLY surface that authors reference pin/exclude (ReferencesPanel.tsx:161-172 -> useReferences.ts:50-64, PUT grounding-pin with item_type='reference'), and the packer still honors them (pack.py:688-703 pinned_reference_ids / excludes). So there is nothing to "surface again" — do not merge the panels.

BUILDER INSTRUCTIONS for Wave M2 (spec 36 §M2, `reference-shelf` port):

1. PORT AS-IS, DO NOT MERGE. `studio/panels/ReferenceShelfPanel.tsx` keeps the add-form / per-scene retrieval (with pin+exclude) / library exactly as `ReferencesPanel.tsx` has them. DO NOT add `'reference'` to `GroundingPanel.tsx`'s `ADDRESSABLE` (:13) or `ITEM_GROUPS` (:17), and DO NOT copy the grounding item rows into the shelf. One concept, one home.

2. FIX-NOW (this is a real bug the split created — it must land inside M2, it is a 1-line change): in `frontend/src/features/composition/hooks/useReferences.ts`, the `pin` mutation's `onSettled` (currently ~:61-63) invalidates ONLY `['composition','references','search',projectId,sceneId]`. It must ALSO invalidate `['composition','grounding', projectId, sceneId]` — the key `useGrounding` feeds GroundingPanel. Today: pin a reference in the shelf -> the BE will pack it (pack.py:688-703) -> but the grounding preview keeps rendering a stale `token_count` / `blocks` / `grounding_available`. Shared pin store, unshared cache. Mirror `useGroundingPins.ts:30`'s own `onSettled` re-pack.
   TEST (mandatory): `frontend/src/features/composition/hooks/__tests__/useReferences.test.tsx` — render the hook with a real QueryClient, spy on `queryClient.invalidateQueries`, call `setPin(hit,'pin')`, assert it was called with BOTH `['composition','references','search',pid,sid]` AND `['composition','grounding',pid,sid]`.
   Do NOT add the symmetric invalidation to `useGroundingPins` — GroundingPanel never renders a reference row, so it cannot flip a reference's pin state; adding it would be cargo-cult.

3. DEEP-LINK BOTH WAYS (this is what the spec's "both panels deep-link to each other" cashes out to):
   a. In `ReferenceShelfPanel.tsx`, in the "For this scene" retrieval header (the row at ReferencesPanel.tsx:93-102), add a text button `data-testid="reference-shelf-open-grounding"`, label "What this scene actually uses ->", onClick `host.openPanel('scene-inspector', { focus: true })`.
      ⚠ The target id is `scene-inspector`, NOT `grounding`: there is no `grounding` panel in the catalog — GroundingPanel is a Section INSIDE SceneInspectorPanel (`catalog.ts:185`; `SceneInspectorPanel.tsx:188-192`). Passing a non-catalog id is exactly the closed-set silent-no-op class.
   b. In `SceneInspectorPanel.tsx`, on the Grounding `<Section>` header (:188), add a text button `data-testid="grounding-open-reference-shelf"`, label "Reference shelf ->", onClick `host.openPanel('reference-shelf', { focus: true })`.
      ⚠ Put this link in SceneInspectorPanel, NOT inside `GroundingPanel.tsx` — GroundingPanel is ALSO mounted by the legacy non-Studio `CompositionPanel.tsx:795`, which has no StudioHost; calling `useStudioHost()` inside it would crash/no-op there.
   Test: one vitest per direction asserting `host.openPanel` was called with `'scene-inspector'` / `'reference-shelf'` respectively (a string-literal assertion, so a typo reds).

DEFAULT NOTED FOR PO VETO: the shelf shows the corpus + this scene's retrieved hits (with their pin state on the hit rows, which the panel already renders at ReferencesPanel.tsx:162-172); it does NOT get a separate "pinned references" list. A pinned reference that is not in the current scene's top-k hits is therefore invisible in the shelf. Judged acceptable for v1 — pinning is only reachable FROM a hit row, so a pin implies the reference was a hit at pin time. If the PO wants pinned-but-not-retrieved references always visible, that is a BE change (widen `GET /references/search` to force-include pinned ids) and should be its own slice, not a v1 blocker.

### Q-36-OQ7-ACTIVE-WORK-HOME
PREFERENCES — confirm the v1 default, with two code-grounded corrections the builder MUST apply.

**1. Home: `/v1/me/preferences`. Build no new table.** The infra is already shipped end-to-end: auth-service `GET/PATCH /v1/me/preferences` (handlers.go:812/:835), gateway-allowlisted (gateway-setup.ts:69,578), and three FE helpers (`syncPrefsToServer` / `savePrefToServer` / `loadPrefFromServer`, frontend/src/lib/syncPrefs.ts). A `composition_work`-side "last opened by user X" table buys zero extra capability and costs a migration + its own tenancy review. `work.settings` is CONFIRMED shared, not per-user: it hangs off the shared `CompositionWork` row (models.py:70) whose `created_by` is annotated "stored, never a scope key / filter (PM-5)" (models.py:56) — writing there re-ships the `entity_kinds` bug exactly as the spec feared.

**2. Key shape MUST be a FLAT dotted top-level key — `lw_active_work.<book_id>` — NOT a nested object.** This is the load-bearing correction. The server merge is SHALLOW: `prefs = user_preferences.prefs || $2` (handlers.go:860) is a top-level JSONB merge. So PATCHing `{"lw_active_work": {"<book_id>": "..."}}` REPLACES the whole `lw_active_work` object and silently wipes every other book's active Work on each switch. PATCH `{"lw_active_work.<book_id>": "<work_id>"}` instead — one top-level key per book, merged independently. Precedent to mirror verbatim: `modelPicker.recents.<capability>` (frontend/src/components/model-picker/recents.ts:13-15), dotted-flat for exactly this reason.

**3. Store the Work's surrogate `id`, NOT `project_id`. EC-3d's name `activeWorkProjectId` is a misnomer and would ship a NULL.** models.py:52-59: `project_id` is NULLABLE — a lazy greenfield Work whose knowledge project could not be created yet carries `project_id = NULL` pending backfill; `id` is the surrogate PK (repositories/works.py:247 keeps them distinct: `work_id=row["id"], project_id=row["project_id"]`). Persisting `project_id` therefore stores NULL for precisely the Works a user just created — Switch-to would silently fail to restore them. Rename the concept to `activeWorkId` and store `work.id`.

**Builder instruction (M3, Switch-to persistence):**
- New file `frontend/src/features/studio/activeWork.ts`, mirroring recents.ts: export `activeWorkPrefKey(bookId: string) => \`lw_active_work.${bookId}\``; `loadActiveWork(bookId, token)` → `loadPrefFromServer<string>(activeWorkPrefKey(bookId), token)`; `saveActiveWork(bookId, workId, token)` → `syncPrefsToServer(activeWorkPrefKey(bookId), workId, token)` (fire-and-forget; use `savePrefToServer` if a navigation must be ordered after the durable write).
- localStorage is CACHE-ONLY and MUST be user-scoped — copy recents.ts:21-23's `cacheKey(..., userId)` guard verbatim (an unscoped cache key leaks user A's active Work into user B's server prefs across a logout/login on a shared browser; that exact bug was already caught once in review-impl W5 #1).
- On Switch-to: call `saveActiveWork`. On Editor mount for a book: `loadActiveWork` → if the id no longer resolves to a live Work (deleted/archived), fall back to the book's default Work and clear the stale key.
- Tests: (a) a vitest asserting PATCH body is `{prefs: {"lw_active_work.<bookId>": workId}}` — a FLAT key, and that switching Work on book B leaves book A's key intact (this is the shallow-merge regression guard); (b) a test asserting a lazy-greenfield Work (project_id NULL) round-trips — i.e. the stored value is `work.id`, never `project_id`.

Default noted for PO veto: this is the spec's own v1 answer, so it contradicts nothing sealed in plan 30 §0; corrections 2 and 3 are bug fixes to the v1 shape, not a change of home.

*Evidence:* services/auth-service/internal/api/handlers.go:860 — `prefs = user_preferences.prefs || $2` (SHALLOW top-level JSONB merge ⇒ nested key would clobber sibling books); handlers.go:812/:835 (GET/PATCH exist). services/composition-service/app/db/models.py:70 (`settings` on shared Work row) + :56 (`created_by` "stored, never a scope key / filter (PM-5)") ⇒ work.settings is shared, tenancy hazard real. models.py:52-59 (`project_id: UUID | None` — nullable for lazy greenfield; `id` = surrogate PK) + services/composition-service/app/db/repositories/works.py:247 (`work_id=row["id"], project_id=row["project_id"]` kept distinct) ⇒ store `id`, not `project_id`. frontend/src/components/model-picker/recents.ts:13-15 (flat dotted key precedent `modelPicker.recents.<capability>`) + :21-23 (user-scoped localStorage cache guard). frontend/src/lib/syncPrefs.ts:8/24/41 (three helpers already shipped). services/api-gateway-bff/src/gateway-setup.ts:69,578 (/v1/me/preferences already allowlisted).

### Q-36-BE18-SETTINGS-FULL-BLOB-REPLACE
BUILD IT — exactly as EC-4b seals it (spec 36 line 274; the blanket-If-Match half is struck). The bug is real and confirmed in code: `services/composition-service/app/db/repositories/works.py:311-313` emits `settings = $n::jsonb` (full REPLACE), and three FE hooks hand-merge the whole blob before PATCHing, so two panels writing two different keys blind-clobber each other. Concrete build (XS):

1) BE repo — ONE `settings` SET clause, composed (Postgres forbids two assignments to the same column). In `works.py` `update()` (line ~296-316):
   - Before the `_UPDATABLE_COLUMNS` unknown-field loop, POP the pseudo-field: `unset = patch.pop("settings_unset", None)` (it is not a column — leaving it in the loop raises `ValueError: field not updatable`). Treat `unset` (non-empty list) as an effective update so the `if not updates: return await self.get(project_id)` no-op guard does NOT swallow an unset-only patch.
   - Build the expression incrementally: start `expr = "COALESCE(settings, '{}'::jsonb)"`; if `settings` in updates → `params.append(json.dumps(value)); expr = f"({expr} || ${len(params)}::jsonb)"`; if `unset` → `params.append(list(unset)); expr = f"({expr} - ${len(params)}::text[])"`; then `set_clauses.append(f"settings = {expr}")`. Keep the existing `updated_at = now()`, the `expected_version` WHERE-gate + `version = version + 1`, and the 404-vs-412 follow-up GET untouched.
   - Merge is SHALLOW by design: `useWorldMap`'s whole-`world_map`-key write still replaces that key wholesale (sub-key deletes inside it keep working).

2) BE router — `services/composition-service/app/routers/works.py:59-72` `WorkPatch`: add `settings_unset: list[str] | None = None`; validate it in a `field_validator` (each key a non-empty str, list length ≤ 32) — a 422 at the boundary, same discipline as the existing `assembly_mode` enum validator. `patch.model_dump(exclude_unset=True)` at line 598 already carries it through to the repo.

3) FE — `frontend/src/features/composition/api.ts:443`: `patchWork(projectId, patch: { settings?: Record<string, unknown>; settings_unset?: string[]; status?: string }, token, opts?: { ifMatch?: number })`, adding `...(opts?.ifMatch != null ? { headers: { 'If-Match': String(opts.ifMatch) } } : {})` — the exact pattern already used at api.ts:237. Fix the now-false comment above it ("the server REPLACES the whole settings blob") and the two copies of that comment in `hooks/useWork.ts:124-127` and `hooks/useProgress.ts:66-68`.

4) FE — If-Match is PER CALL SITE, never blanket (EC-4b): thread an optional `ifMatch?: number` through `useSetWorkSettings`'s mutation VARIABLES (`useWork.ts:131-137`), and pass it ONLY from the Composition-settings save (`CompositionSettingsView.tsx:26`) and the divergence archive. `useWorldMap.ts:95` and `SceneGraphCanvas.tsx:47` (drag writers, one PATCH per drag) pass nothing — a 412 mid-drag is worse than the lost update the merge already closes. Any call site that DOES send `ifMatch` must chain its writes and re-seed `version` from the response.

5) Keep the FE hand-merge (`{...currentSettings, ...patch}`) as-is — behaviour-preserving with `||`. `useSetDailyGoal`'s clear stays `daily_goal: null` (readers already treat null as cleared); `settings_unset` is for genuine key removal, not for it.

6) Tests (Definition of Done): composition repo/router pytest — (a) two sequential PATCHes of two DIFFERENT keys ⇒ both keys survive; (b) `settings_unset: ["k"]` removes only k; (c) unset-only patch is not a no-op and bumps version under If-Match; (d) a stale same-key PATCH with If-Match still 412s. FE vitest — `patchWork` sends `If-Match` only when `opts.ifMatch` is given, and a world-map drag through `useSetWorkSettings` sends NO If-Match header (the EC-4b regression guard).

*Evidence:* services/composition-service/app/db/repositories/works.py:311-313 (`if field == "settings": params.append(json.dumps(value)); set_clauses.append(f"settings = ${len(params)}::jsonb")` — full-blob REPLACE) · services/composition-service/app/routers/works.py:59-72 (WorkPatch, no settings_unset), :581-601 (patch_work, `_parse_if_match` + `model_dump(exclude_unset=True)`) · frontend/src/features/composition/api.ts:443 (`patchWork`, no ifMatch; comment says "the server REPLACES the whole settings blob") · 3 blind hand-merge call sites: hooks/useWork.ts:135 (useSetWorkSettings), hooks/useChapterAssembly.ts:33, hooks/useProgress.ts:77 · the drag writers that must NOT get If-Match: hooks/useWorldMap.ts:95 and components/SceneGraphCanvas.tsx:47, both routing through useSetWorkSettings → patchWork · existing header pattern to copy: frontend/src/features/composition/api.ts:237 · sealed decision: docs/specs/2026-07-01-writing-studio/36_editor_craft_ports.md:274 (EC-4b) and :436 (BE-18 MUST-BUILD), scheduled in M4a at :571.

### Q-36-OQ8-BE21-SCOPE-CRITIC-ONLY
BE-21 changes ONLY `critic` behaviour. Ship the helper GENERIC, re-point ONLY the 7 critic sites — the spec's candidate answer is right, and the code makes it tighter (composer/planner are not merely "wider blast radius"; they are NOT read from `work.settings` by composition-service AT ALL, so there is literally nothing else to re-point in this service).

BUILD IT EXACTLY LIKE THIS:

1) NEW FILE `services/composition-service/app/services/model_roles.py` — pure, total, no I/O (mirror the proven precedent `services/knowledge-service/app/extraction/model_roles.py:1-60`):
```python
ROLES = ("chat", "composer", "planner", "critic")   # == chat-service ModelRole app-roles
_LEGACY = {"chat": ("default_model_ref", "default_model_source"),
           "critic": ("critic_model_ref", "critic_model_source")}   # composer/planner have NO legacy scalar
class RoleModel(NamedTuple):
    model_source: str | None
    model_ref: str | None
def resolve_model_role(settings: Mapping | None, role: str) -> RoleModel: ...
```
Precedence: (1) `settings["model_roles"][role]` when it is a dict with a truthy `model_ref` (`model_source` defaults to `"user_model"`), (2) the legacy scalar pair for that role — chat/critic only, (3) `RoleModel(None, None)`. NOTE the tuple order is (source, ref) to match the existing `c_src, c_ref` call sites.

2) LIFT the dual-read: rewrite `_model_roles_from_settings` in `services/composition-service/app/routers/internal_model_settings.py:46-65` to loop `for role in ROLES: rm = resolve_model_role(settings, role)` and emit only roles with a ref. Do NOT keep a second copy of the precedence logic (SET-8, one home). `tests/unit/test_internal_model_settings.py` must stay green UNCHANGED — that is the regression proof of the lift.

3) RE-POINT the 7 critic sites in `services/composition-service/app/routers/engine.py`: lines 465, 529, 1029, 1099, 1261, 1345 become `c_src, c_ref = resolve_model_role(sdict, "critic")`; line 1644-1645 becomes `critic_src, critic_ref = resolve_model_role(settings_dict, "critic")`. Nothing else in engine.py changes (the `distinct = bool(c_ref and c_src and str(c_ref) != str(body.model_ref))` anti-self-reinforcement logic is untouched).

4) TOUCH NOTHING ELSE. Explicitly out of scope for BE-21:
   - composer — the engine takes it per-call as `body.model_ref`; the FE reads `work.settings.default_model_ref` at `frontend/src/features/composition/components/CompositionPanel.tsx:310`, `frontend/src/features/studio/panels/EditorPanel.tsx:199`, `frontend/src/pages/ChapterEditorPage.tsx:243`. Re-pointing those 3 FE reads at `model_roles.composer` = D-WORK-MODEL-ROLES-DEFAULT-REF (already on the register).
   - planner — resolves from the user's pinned provider-registry `planner` default (`app/services/plan_forge_service.py:127`, `app/clients/llm_client.py:165`), never from `work.settings`. Nothing to re-point, ever.
   - the 8 `scripts/eval_*.py` + `scripts/diag_s1_regurgitation.py` — they WRITE `critic_model_ref` (`scripts/eval_a1_diverge.py:93`, `eval_a2_canon.py:213`, `eval_a3_decompose.py:107`, `eval_a_fair.py:45`, `eval_a_grounded.py:251`, `eval_a_validate.py:123`, `eval_narrative_thread.py:137`, `diag_s1_regurgitation.py:109`). ### Q-36-EC4B-BLANKET-IFMATCH-IS-WRONG
EC-4b is CORRECT and is confirmed by the code — build it exactly as written; do NOT put If-Match on patchWork itself.

(1) FE signature — `frontend/src/features/composition/api.ts:443`, change to:
`patchWork(projectId: string, patch: { settings?: Record<string,unknown>; settings_unset?: string[]; status?: string; active_template_id?: string|null }, token: string, opts?: { ifMatch?: number }): Promise<Work>` with body
`return apiJson(`${BASE}/works/${projectId}`, { method:'PATCH', body: JSON.stringify(patch), token, ...(opts?.ifMatch != null ? { headers: { 'If-Match': String(opts.ifMatch) } } : {}) });`
Copy the exact conditional-header idiom already used at `frontend/src/features/chat-ai-settings/api.ts:30-35` and `composition/api.ts:237`. A 4th OPTIONAL arg means the 4 existing call sites compile and behave unchanged (unconditional PATCH). Also update the stale comment above it (it still says "the server REPLACES the whole settings blob") once BE-18 lands.

(2) BE — NO new concurrency code is needed: `services/composition-service/app/routers/works.py:588` already accepts the optional `If-Match` header, parses it (`_parse_if_match`, :122) and 412s with `{code:'WORK_VERSION_CONFLICT', current:<work>}` (:605); `expected_version=None` ⇒ unconditional UPDATE. The ONLY BE change is BE-18's merge: `services/composition-service/app/db/repositories/works.py:311-313` → `settings = COALESCE(settings,'{}'::jsonb) || $n::jsonb`, plus a `settings_unset: list[str]` field on `WorkPatch` (`routers/works.py:59`) handled as a special SET branch `settings = settings - $n::text[]` in `WorksRepo.update()` (add it to `_UPDATABLE_COLUMNS` at works.py:41 AND special-case it in the per-field loop at :310-316, since it is not a real column). Order matters: apply `-` (unset) BEFORE `||` (merge) in the same UPDATE.

(3) Adopt `ifMatch` at EXACTLY TWO call sites, both human-paced:
  - M4a Composition-section save — pass `{ ifMatch: work.version }`.
  - M3 divergence archive — pass `{ ifMatch: work.version }`.
Both MUST (a) chain their writes (single in-flight; queue the next save behind the previous promise — no parallel saves) and (b) RE-SEED version from the response: `onSuccess: (updated) => qc.setQueryData(['composition','work',bookId], updated)`, mirroring `frontend/src/features/composition/motif/hooks/useArcTimeline.ts:85` ("adopt the server's new version as the next If-Match"). On 412, surface WORK_VERSION_CONFLICT + refetch the work (mirror `OutlineTree.tsx:140`).

(4) NEVER pass `ifMatch` from `useWorldMap`, `useChapterAssembly` (`useChapterAssembly.ts:33`) or `useProgress` (`useProgress.ts:77`). `useSetWorkSettings` (`useWork.ts:131-135`) is the drag path (useWorldMap `persistPositions` → `setSettings.mutate`) and STAYS unconditional. DEFAULT I am setting (veto-able): if the M4a section reuses `useSetWorkSettings`, extend its mutate VARIABLES with an optional `ifMatch?: number` that is passed straight to `patchWork(..., { ifMatch: v.ifMatch })` — undefined ⇒ unconditional. One writer, opt-in per CALL. Do not add If-Match to the hook unconditionally.

(5) Tests (the M4a DoD regression guard, literally): in `frontend/src/features/composition/hooks/__tests__/useWorldMap.test.tsx` assert a drag → `patchWorkMock` is called with `undefined` (or no) 4th arg ⇒ NO If-Match header, and a second drag with a stale `work.version` still succeeds (does NOT 412). Add an api.ts unit test: no opts ⇒ no If-Match header; `{ifMatch:7}` ⇒ `If-Match: '7'`. BE pytest on PATCH /works/{pid}: two PATCHes to two DIFFERENT settings keys both survive (merge); `settings_unset:['k']` removes the key; a stale same-key PATCH with If-Match ⇒ 412 WORK_VERSION_CONFLICT; a PATCH with NO If-Match never 412s.

*Evidence:* frontend/src/features/composition/api.ts:443 (patchWork — 3 args, no headers, comment still says server REPLACES settings) · frontend/src/features/composition/hooks/useWork.ts:131-135 (useSetWorkSettings → patchWork) · frontend/src/features/composition/hooks/useWorldMap.ts persistPositions/persistWorldMap → setSettings.mutate (one PATCH per drag-end, read-modify-write from a possibly stale `work` prop) · services/composition-service/app/routers/works.py:588 + :122 + :605 (If-Match header ALREADY optional; expected_version=None ⇒ unconditional; 412 WORK_VERSION_CONFLICT) · services/composition-service/app/db/repositories/works.py:311-313 (`settings = $n::jsonb` — full blob REPLACE, the real lost-update window) · frontend/src/features/composition/types.ts:10 (Work.version exists FE-side) · frontend/src/features/chat-ai-settings/api.ts:30-35 + composition/api.ts:237 (the conditional-If-Match idiom to copy) · frontend/src/features/composition/motif/hooks/useArcTimeline.ts:85 (re-seed version from the response)

### Q-36-BE21-MODEL-ROLES-HAS-NO-READER
CONFIRMED BY CODE — BE-21 is real, is a hard prereq of M4a, and is size S. BUILD IT AS FOLLOWS (no further design input needed).

**1. NEW FILE `services/composition-service/app/services/model_roles.py`** — mirror the existing precedent `services/knowledge-service/app/extraction/model_roles.py` (RoleModel NamedTuple + a pure/total resolver with documented rungs). Pure, no I/O:

```python
ROLES = ("chat", "composer", "planner", "critic", "embedding", "rerank")
_DEFAULT_SOURCE = "user_model"
_LEGACY_SCALARS = {  # role -> (ref_key, source_key) — the compat rung, chat+critic ONLY
    "chat":   ("default_model_ref", "default_model_source"),
    "critic": ("critic_model_ref",  "critic_model_source"),
}

class RoleModel(NamedTuple):
    model_source: str
    model_ref: str

def resolve_model_role(settings: Mapping[str, Any] | None, role: str) -> RoleModel | None:
    """settings.model_roles.<role> WINS; the legacy scalar is the fallback rung. ONE home."""
    s = settings or {}
    roles = s.get("model_roles")
    if isinstance(roles, Mapping):
        e = roles.get(role)
        if isinstance(e, Mapping) and e.get("model_ref"):
            return RoleModel(str(e.get("model_source") or _DEFAULT_SOURCE), str(e["model_ref"]))
    keys = _LEGACY_SCALARS.get(role)
    if keys and s.get(keys[0]):
        return RoleModel(str(s.get(keys[1]) or _DEFAULT_SOURCE), str(s[keys[0]]))
    return None
```

**2. REWRITE `internal_model_settings._model_roles_from_settings` (internal_model_settings.py:46-65) to call the helper** (loop over ROLES, keep the same return shape). Do NOT leave a second copy of the dual-read — the spec's "lift it OUT of the router, do not write a second copy" is the whole point (SET-8). Its test `tests/unit/test_internal_model_settings.py:80` must stay green unchanged.

**3. REPLACE the read at all 7 engine.py sites. Keep each site's `distinct` predicate EXACTLY as-is** — the sites diverge downstream (529 falls back to the drafter as judge; 1345 passes None) and that behaviour must not change.
- Six sites (465, 529, 1029, 1099, 1261, 1345), identical 2-line idiom →
  `_c = resolve_model_role(sdict, "critic")`
  `c_src, c_ref = (_c.model_source, _c.model_ref) if _c else (None, None)`
  (leave the following `distinct = bool(c_ref and c_src and str(c_ref) != str(body.model_ref))` line untouched)
- Site 7 (1643-1644, the "critique skipped" gate) →
  `_c = resolve_model_role(settings_dict, "critic")`
  `critic_src = _c.model_source if _c else None`
  `critic_ref = _c.model_ref if _c else None`
  Leave the gate at 1649 byte-identical (the `not critic_src` arm becomes dead-but-harmless since the helper defaults source to "user_model" — keep it defensively; do not "simplify" the gate).

**4. DO NOT touch the worker.** `worker/operations.py:291,349-350,471-472` reads `input["critic_source"/"critic_ref"]`, which the ROUTER writes into `job_input` at sites 465/1029/1261 — the 7-site fix propagates to every worker path for free. (The spec did not state this; it means the blast radius is engine.py only.)

**5. DO NOT touch `authoring_run_service.py:574`.** It reads `params.get("critic_model_ref")` — the caller-supplied RUN-PARAMS tier (fed by `routers/authoring_runs.py:145` and `mcp/server.py:3619`), NOT `work.settings`. It is a different tier, not a `model_roles` reader. It is NOT an 8th site.

**6. TESTS (this is M4a's DoD behaviour test — it must exist or the wave ships write-only):**
- New `tests/unit/test_model_roles.py`: map wins over scalar · scalar-only → fallback fires · neither → None · malformed entry (dict with no `model_ref`) → falls through to the scalar, not a crash (the nil-tolerant-wrapper lesson: a dropped rung must RED a test).

This is the exact test that REDs today.

**Follow-up, NOT this slice:** existing defer row `D-WORK-MODEL-ROLES-DEFAULT-REF` (spec 36 line 710) stands unchanged — the `default_model_ref`/role-`chat` READ sites (incl. 8 `scripts/eval_*.py`) still read the legacy scalar. The helper already handles `chat`, so that row is a mechanical sweep of read sites, not new logic. Gate reason #2 (large/structural — wider blast radius, its own slice).

### Q-36-EC3C-NULLISH-NOT-STRICT-NULL
CONFIRMED — the predicate is NULLISH everywhere. Build it exactly as follows.

FE — new file `frontend/src/features/composition/workSelect.ts` (the single home; no consumer re-implements the predicate):
```ts
import type { Work } from './types';
// `source_work_id` is OPTIONAL (types.ts:18) — pre-C23 rows and most fixtures carry
// `undefined`, not `null`. A `=== null` test silently returns NO canonical Work for
// them. Nullish only. (A UUID is never '', so falsy === absent is safe here.)
export const isCanonicalWork = (w: Work): boolean => !w.source_work_id;
export const isDerivativeWork = (w: Work): boolean => !!w.source_work_id;
export function selectCanonicalWork(candidates: readonly Work[]): Work | null {
  // Last-resort: a book whose canonical Work was archived leaves only derivatives —
  // fall back to the earliest row (list is created_at asc) rather than "no Work".
  // Spelled `.at(0)` on purpose: M3's hygiene test bans the literal `candidates[0]`.
  return candidates.find(isCanonicalWork) ?? candidates.at(0) ?? null;
}
export function selectDerivatives(candidates: readonly Work[]): Work[] {
  return candidates.filter(isDerivativeWork);
}
```
Replace `candidates[0]` with `selectCanonicalWork(...)` at all 12 sites (7 studio + 4 legacy + the deep-link fallback), incl. `frontend/src/features/studio/panels/EditorPanel.tsx:189`, `useQualityWork.ts:49`, `useSceneInspector.ts:31`, `manuscript/useManuscriptTree.ts:55`, `useManuscriptJump.ts:48`, `ManuscriptUnitProvider.tsx:138`, `composition/components/CompositionPanel.tsx:156`, `OutlineTree.tsx:118`, `hooks/usePublishGate.ts:51`, `features/books/hooks/useChapterBrowserGroups.ts:89`, `pages/ChapterEditorPage.tsx:218`. Leave `useDerivativeContext.ts:66` as-is (it is already `!!work?.source_work_id`) but re-express it as `isDerivativeWork(work)` so there is ONE predicate.

BE — `services/composition-service/app/routers/internal_model_settings.py:85`: replace `rows[0]` with the same predicate, mirroring the existing in-repo picker at `engine/scene_decompile.py:132`:
```python
canon = next((r for r in rows if getattr(r, "source_work_id", None) is None), None) or (rows[0] if rows else None)
settings = (canon.settings if canon else {}) or {}
```
(Python side is genuinely `None` — `db/models.py:68` declares `source_work_id: UUID | None = None` — so `is None` is correct there; do NOT copy the FE falsy form, and do NOT copy `=== null` to the FE.)

Tests (M3 DoD, literal): in `frontend/src/features/composition/__tests__/workSelect.test.ts` — (a) `selectCanonicalWork([{...w, source_work_id: undefined}])` returns that Work (the `=== null` trap: this test MUST red if the predicate is changed to `=== null`); (b) a fixture with the derivative sorted FIRST still resolves the canonical one; (c) `selectDerivatives` excludes a `source_work_id: undefined` row; (d) empty list → `null`. Plus the hygiene test asserting the literal `candidates[0]` appears nowhere under `frontend/src` or `services/` outside `__tests__`/`tests`.

*Evidence:* frontend/src/features/composition/types.ts:18 (`source_work_id?: string | null` — optional ⇒ `undefined` at runtime); frontend/src/features/composition/hooks/useDerivativeContext.ts:66 (`const isDerivative = !!work?.source_work_id;` — shipped nullish precedent); frontend/src/features/world/lib/livingWorldTree.ts:109 (`const src = work.source_work_id ?? null;`); services/composition-service/app/db/models.py:68 (`source_work_id: UUID | None = None` — BE row always has the attr); services/composition-service/app/engine/scene_decompile.py:132 (`if getattr(w, "source_work_id", None) is None:` — the BE canonical picker to mirror); services/composition-service/app/routers/internal_model_settings.py:85 (`settings = (rows[0].settings if rows else {}) or {}` — the position-as-identity site EC-3c names)

### Q-36-BE10-STYLE-VOICE-MCP-TOOLS
BUILD IT — it is a work item, fully buildable today (no DDL, no new REST). The REST + repo layer already exists; BE-10 is a thin MCP facade cloned from the canon_rule tools. Three ambiguities the spec text leaves open are settled below (each is a 3am stall if left vague).

**A. H13 does NOT mean "no project_id arg".** In this repo H13 = the uniform `not_accessible()` (no enumeration oracle) — server.py:24, plan-30:643. `project_id` IS the scoping tool arg, exactly as in all 30+ existing composition tools; what is DERIVED-never-a-body-arg is `book_id` (from `composition_work` inside the INSERT, style_voice.py repo:59-61) and `created_by` (from `tc.user_id`, the envelope — never an arg; `ForbidExtra` blocks smuggling). BE-7c's "drop the un-knowable project_id" applies ONLY to `composition_get_mine_job` (a job id whose project the agent cannot know); style/voice rows are project-keyed and the agent must name the Work. Do not invent a project-less signature.

**B. Tier: the two `_list` tools are Tier R, not A.** Spec 36:493 blanket-labels the group "Tier-A"; tier A = auto-write + undo_hint (server.py:25). Reads get `require_meta("R","book")` + GrantLevel.VIEW; the four writes get `require_meta("A","book")` + GrantLevel.EDIT + `_meta.undo_hint`.

**C. undo of an upsert-that-created = the DELETE tool, not `None`.** Spec 36:434 says "None if it was unset" — refine to the `composition_canon_rule_create`/`outline_node_create` precedent (server.py:1106): a verified reverse op EXISTS here (unlike canon_rule_delete's archive-with-no-unarchive, server.py:1199-1201), so emit `_undo("composition_style_delete", ...)`. Emitting None would leave every agent-created profile un-undoable. PO may veto; flagged.

### Q-36-F-EC1-DELETE-ROUTE-UNREACHABLE
CONFIRMED as stated — and it is a pure-FE wire-up: ZERO backend work. Build it in M1 as slice EC-1a exactly as follows.

DEFAULT I AM PICKING (veto-able): the cascade is resolved CLIENT-SIDE from the rows `GET /style-profiles` already returns — do NOT add a BE `/style-profile/resolve` route. `StyleProfileRepo.list_all()` (style_voice.py:75) returns EVERY row for the Work, so the FE has all the input `resolve()` (style_voice.py:86) uses. Adding a BE resolve route would be a second implementation of the same precedence rule = the cross-service-normalization bug class.

STEP 1 — `frontend/src/features/chat-ai-settings/components/TierChip.tsx:13-38`. Add 4 rows to ALL THREE maps (CLS, LABEL, TITLE): `scene`, `chapter`, `work`, `neutral`. `neutral` LABEL = "unset", TITLE = "No row at any scope — the packer adds no density/pace directive." Pick any consistent CLS colors (e.g. scene=sky, chapter=violet, work=teal, neutral=muted). Extend the ONE chip; forking a second is the defect. This is the only prerequisite and it is shared with EC-1's cascade requirement.

STEP 2 — `frontend/src/features/composition/components/StyleVoicePanel.tsx` (and its studio-dock port). Add a pure helper (export it so it is unit-testable):

  type Ctx = { projectId: string; chapterId?: string; sceneId?: string };
  // MIRROR of StyleProfileRepo.resolve() (style_voice.py:86-104): most-specific-wins,
  // restricted to scopes AT OR ABOVE the selected tab's specificity.
  export function resolveStyle(rows: StyleProfile[], ctx: Ctx, scope: StyleScope, excludeExactScope = false) {
    const order: {t: StyleScope; id?: string}[] =
      scope === 'scene'   ? [{t:'scene',   id: ctx.sceneId},   {t:'chapter', id: ctx.chapterId}, {t:'work', id: ctx.projectId}]
    : scope === 'chapter' ? [{t:'chapter', id: ctx.chapterId}, {t:'work',    id: ctx.projectId}]
    :                       [{t:'work',    id: ctx.projectId}];
    const cands = excludeExactScope ? order.slice(1) : order;
    for (const c of cands) {
      if (!c.id) continue;
      const hit = rows.find(r => r.scope_type === c.t && r.scope_id === c.id);
      if (hit) return { tier: c.t as string, density: hit.density, pace: hit.pace };
    }
    return { tier: 'neutral', density: null as number | null, pace: null as number | null };
  }

STEP 3 — in the panel body, replace the lying line `StyleSliders key={scope} density={row?.density ?? 50} pace={row?.pace ?? 50}` (StyleVoicePanel.tsx:131) with:
  const own = styleQ.data?.find(r => r.scope_type === scope && r.scope_id === scopeId);   // exact-scope row (already computed as `row`)
  const eff = resolveStyle(styleQ.data ?? [], {projectId, chapterId, sceneId}, scope);
  const fallback = resolveStyle(styleQ.data ?? [], {projectId, chapterId, sceneId}, scope, true); // what a DELETE would leave
Render `<TierChip tier={eff.tier} />` next to the scope tabs. Sliders show `eff.density ?? 50` / `eff.pace ?? 50`, and when `eff.tier !== scope` (inherited) or `eff.tier === 'neutral'` the slider block gets `opacity-60` + a `<p>` reading "inherited from {tier}" / "unset — the packer adds no directive". Keep `key={scope}` so local slider state remounts on tab switch.

STEP 4 — THE ACTUAL ASK. Import `useDeleteStyleProfile` (useStyleVoice.ts:30) and `ClearOverride` (TierChip.tsx:60), and render:
  const delStyle = useDeleteStyleProfile(projectId, token);
  <ClearOverride
    show={!!own}                                    // ROW EXISTENCE ONLY — never value-equality (TierChip.tsx:8-11)
    inherited={fallback.density === null ? null : `${fallback.density}/${fallback.pace} (from ${fallback.tier})`}
    testId="style-clear-override"
    onClear={() => scopeId && delStyle.mutate({ scopeType: scope, scopeId })}
  />
`show={!!own}` IS the spec's "only when a row exists at that exact scope". `inherited={null}` makes ClearOverride print "clear · inherit the default" — acceptable; if you want it explicit, pass the literal string "neutral (no directive)". The hook already hits `DELETE /v1/composition/works/{pid}/style-profile?scope_type&scope_id` (api.ts:333 → style_voice.py:89) and already invalidates the style + grounding query keys — nothing else to wire.

STEP 5 — i18n: add `styleVoice.inheritedFrom`, `styleVoice.unset`, `styleVoice.clearOverride` to `frontend/src/i18n/locales/*/composition.json` (ALL locales — the repo has ~13).

STEP 6 — TESTS (extend `frontend/src/features/composition/components/__tests__/StyleVoicePanel.test.tsx`; the panel already has one). Five assertions, all mandatory:
  (a) no row anywhere ⇒ `tier-chip-neutral` rendered AND `style-clear-override` ABSENT.
  (b) row at `chapter` only, `scene` tab selected ⇒ sliders read the CHAPTER numbers, `tier-chip-chapter` rendered, `style-clear-override` ABSENT (no scene row).
  (c) row at the exact selected scope ⇒ `style-clear-override` PRESENT, its text names the fallback ("clear · inherit 80/20 (from chapter)").
  (d) clicking it calls `compositionApi.deleteStyleProfile` with the exact `scope_type` + `scope_id` of the selected tab (spy the api module).
  (e) THE ANTI-REGRESSION: a scene row whose density/pace EQUAL the inherited chapter values still renders `style-clear-override` and `tier-chip-scene` — proves the chip/clear key on row existence, not value equality (TierChip.tsx:8-11).
  Plus one pure unit test of `resolveStyle` asserting scene>chapter>work and the `neutral` fall-through, so the FE mirror of `StyleProfileRepo.resolve()` is pinned.

Route is live: services/composition-service/app/routers/style_voice.py:89 `@router.delete("/works/{project_id}/style-profile")` with scope_type+scope_id Query params, EDIT-gated; client exists at frontend/src/features/composition/api.ts:333. ### Q-36-STYLE-VOICE-NO-OCC-CHAIN-WRITES
CONFIRMED BY CODE, and it is a build instruction, not an open question. The tables genuinely have NO `version` column (migrate.py:513-524 style_profile, :531-540 voice_profile) and the PUT is a true upsert (`ON CONFLICT (project_id, scope_type, scope_id) DO UPDATE` / `ON CONFLICT (project_id, entity_id) DO UPDATE`, style_voice.py repo). So: NO OCC, NO `If-Match`, NO version echo on these two routes — last-writer-wins by design, and `instant-commit-control-over-occ-entity` does NOT apply (nothing to self-412 against). Do not "fix" this by adding a version column — that is out of scope and would break the shared-package upsert semantics (DA-11).

BUT the FE today WILL race: `useSetStyleProfile` / `useSetVoiceProfile` are plain `useMutation`s (useStyleVoice.ts:18-28, 51-60) — N rapid `mutate()` calls fire N parallel PUTs and the DB commits whichever lands last, so a fast slider drag can persist 62 after the user released at 80. Build this, in M1:

1) COMMIT TRIGGER — keep what already exists, do not regress it: the range inputs commit ONLY on `onPointerUp` / `onKeyUp` (StyleVoicePanel.tsx:33-34 and :44-45); `onChange` updates LOCAL state only. Voice-tag rows commit on Enter / chip-remove. Never per-keystroke, never on `onChange`.

2) SERIAL WRITER — add to `frontend/src/features/composition/hooks/useStyleVoice.ts` a new exported hook `useStyleVoiceWriter(projectId, token)` used by the new `studio/panels/StyleVoicePanel.tsx`. Shape (no external lib; there is no shared debounce util in this repo — roll it local):
   - `const chain = useRef<Promise<unknown>>(Promise.resolve())` — ONE FIFO chain for the whole panel ⇒ at most one PUT in flight, strict order.
   - `const pending = useRef(new Map<string, Body>())` — LATEST-WINS COALESCE, keyed `style:${scope_type}:${scope_id}` / `voice:${entity_id}` so a chapter commit never clobbers a scene commit; a superseded intermediate value is DROPPED, not queued.
   - `const timer = useRef<number>()` — 250 ms trailing debounce; `commitStyle(body)` / `commitVoice(body)` write into `pending` and (re)arm the timer.
   - flush: `chain.current = chain.current.catch(() => {}).then(async () => { for (const [k, b] of drain(pending)) await putFor(k, b); })` — the `.catch` is load-bearing: one 4xx/5xx must not wedge the chain forever.
   - INVALIDATE ONLY WHEN THE CHAIN DRAINS. Move the `invalidateQueries(['composition','style-profiles',pid])` + `['composition','grounding',pid]` calls (useStyleVoice.ts:23-25, 36-37, 56-57, 68-69) out of per-mutation `onSuccess` and into the flush tail (`if (pending.size === 0)`), otherwise a mid-drag refetch snaps the slider back to a stale server value.
   - `StyleSliders` local state stays authoritative while `dirty` (a write is pending); re-sync from server props only after the chain drains — EXCEPT on error, where it reverts to the server value and shows the spec's inline row-level error (36 §1 state table).

3) TESTS (M1 DoD, vitest, `frontend/src/features/studio/panels/__tests__/StyleVoicePanel.write.test.tsx`): (a) deferred-promise mock of `compositionApi.putStyleProfile`; fire pointer-up at 60, 70, 80 inside the debounce window ⇒ exactly ONE PUT, body `density: 80`; (b) three commits SPACED past the debounce ⇒ PUTs are strictly serial (call #2's mock is not invoked until #1's promise resolves) and never >1 in flight; (c) 100 `onChange` events with no pointer-up ⇒ ZERO PUTs; (d) a rejecting PUT followed by a fresh commit ⇒ the second PUT still fires (chain not wedged) and the slider reverted on the failure.

DEFAULT THE PO CAN VETO: 250 ms trailing debounce and a single panel-wide chain (not one chain per scope key) — global ordering is simpler and the coalesce map already prevents cross-scope clobbering. The agent path (BE-10 `composition_style_upsert`) bypasses this chain by design — it is a discrete human/agent action, last-writer-wins is correct there, and the Lane-B effect handler's invalidation covers the re-render.

*Evidence:* services/composition-service/app/db/migrate.py:513-524 (style_profile: created_by/project_id/book_id/scope_type/scope_id/density/pace/updated_at — NO version col; PK (project_id,scope_type,scope_id)) and :531-540 (voice_profile — same, PK (project_id,entity_id)) · services/composition-service/app/db/repositories/style_voice.py StyleProfileRepo.upsert `ON CONFLICT (project_id, scope_type, scope_id) DO UPDATE SET density=EXCLUDED.density, pace=EXCLUDED.pace` (last-writer-wins, no version guard) · services/composition-service/app/routers/style_voice.py:71-85 put_style_profile (no If-Match, no 412 path) · frontend/src/features/composition/hooks/useStyleVoice.ts:18-28 + 51-60 (plain useMutation — THE RACE: parallel PUTs, no chain, no debounce; invalidates on every success) · frontend/src/features/composition/components/StyleVoicePanel.tsx:33-34,44-45 (onPointerUp/onKeyUp commit already correct — preserve on port) · docs/specs/2026-07-01-writing-studio/36_editor_craft_ports.md:323-327 and :542-544 (the spec's own statement of the constraint)

### Q-36-F-EC1-GUI-LIES-ABOUT-EFFECTIVE-VALUE
CONFIRMED — the spec is right, and the defect is WORSE than it states. Build the cascade renderer. NO new backend route is needed (see §C) — this is one FE file.

=== A · WHAT THE CODE PROVES ===
1. resolve() (style_voice.py:86-104) orders by _SCOPE_RANK (:32 — scene=0 > chapter=1 > work=2) LIMIT 1; returns None when nothing is set.
2. None is NOT 50. profile.py:32-33 `density_level: int | None = None`; style_directive() emits a directive ONLY on the OUTER bands (d<34 / d>66) — 34-66 is "balanced → no instruction". So the packer's neutral is "no directive at all".
3. StyleVoicePanel.tsx:104 finds `row` by EXACT scope match (scope_type===scope && scope_id===scopeId), then :131 renders `density={row?.density ?? 50} pace={row?.pace ?? 50}`. A scene inheriting chapter 80/20 renders 50/50. THE LIE IS REAL.

=== B · THE DEFECT THE SPEC MISSED (this is the dangerous one) ===
The sliders commit on pointer/key release — StyleVoicePanel.tsx:34 `onPointerUp={() => onCommit(d, p)}` and :44 (same for pace) → commitStyle (:105-107) → PUT upsert. So: a user opens a scene that INHERITS chapter 80/20, the panel shows the phantom "50/50", the user merely TOUCHES a slider → an explicit scene row is written at ~50/50, which SHADOWS the chapter's 80/20 permanently (resolve is LIMIT 1 by rank). Because 50 lands in the balanced band, the lush/slow directive silently vanishes from every future draft with no feedback. The GUI does not just lie about the effective value — it CONVERTS THE LIE INTO PERSISTED TRUTH and destroys the user's chapter setting. Any fix that only changes the readout and leaves the commit-on-touch path is INCOMPLETE.

=== C · WHY NO BACKEND WORK ===
GET /works/{project_id}/style-profiles (routers/style_voice.py:60) already returns ALL rows for the project (repo list_all, :75-84), and useStyleVoice.ts:14 (`select: (d) => d.items`) already hands the FE every row. The cascade is therefore computable CLIENT-SIDE by mirroring _SCOPE_RANK. Do NOT add a /resolve or /effective endpoint — the data is already on the client.
BONUS: useDeleteStyleProfile (useStyleVoice.ts:30) already exists, already calls the live DELETE (routers/style_voice.py:89-101), and has ZERO consumers (grep: only its own definition). The "clear override" affordance is already-built dead code — CONSUME it, don't write it.

=== D · BUILD THIS (file: frontend/src/features/composition/components/StyleVoicePanel.tsx) ===
D1. DELETE the `?? 50` defaults at :131. There is no default. Unset is a distinct third state.
D2. Add a pure exported helper (same file or a sibling `styleCascade.ts`) — mirror the backend precedence exactly:
    resolveStyle(rows, {projectId, chapterId, sceneId}) -> { density, pace, tier } | { tier: 'unset' }
    Try in order: scene row (scope_type==='scene' && scope_id===sceneId), then chapter, then work (scope_id===projectId). First hit wins. None → tier:'unset'.
    Guard: skip a tier whose id is undefined (the panel is often opened with no sceneId — scopes[] :100-102 already models this).
D3. EFFECTIVE READOUT (the SET-1 fix) — render ALWAYS, above the sliders, independent of which scope TAB is selected, computed for the CURRENT SCENE (the thing the packer will actually pack):
    data-testid="style-effective"; text: `Effective: Density {d} · Pace {p} — from {Scene|Chapter|Work}` and, when tier==='unset': `Effective: not set — the drafter gets no style directive.`
    Also show the BAND, because it is load-bearing and invisible today: a value in 34-66 emits NO directive. Render e.g. `Density 50 (balanced — no directive)`. This is the honest surface of profile.py's band logic.
D4. PER-SCOPE EDITOR — the tabs still edit ONE scope, but must distinguish set-here from inherited:
    - If the SELECTED scope has an explicit row → sliders live, plus a "Clear override" button wired to the existing useDeleteStyleProfile (useStyleVoice.ts:30); data-testid="style-clear-override".
    - If the SELECTED scope has NO row → render the sliders in an INHERITED state: seed them from the effective value (so the user starts from what is actually in force, not from a phantom 50), visually marked as inherited (muted + a `Inherited from {tier}` label, data-testid="style-inherited"), and DISABLE THE WRITE until the user explicitly opts in via an "Override here" button (data-testid="style-set-override"). This is what kills §B.
D5. Remove the write-on-touch hazard: `onCommit` must not fire for a scope that has no row and no explicit override opt-in. Keep commit-on-release for an already-overridden scope (that behavior is fine); gate it behind the override state otherwise.
D6. i18n: add the new keys under the existing `composition:styleVoice.*` namespace (siblings of styleVoice.scopeHint at :132). No raw strings.

=== E · TESTS (extend frontend/src/features/composition/components/__tests__/StyleVoicePanel.test.tsx) ===
E1. Cascade truth: rows = [work 20/20, chapter 80/20], scene selected with NO scene row → the readout MUST show 80/20 "from Chapter". Assert it does NOT show 50. (This test RED-s on today's code — it is the regression proof.)
E2. Unset ≠ 50: rows = [] → readout says "not set / no directive"; assert no "50" is rendered as an effective value.
E3. Explicit-50 ≠ unset: a scene row at 50/50 renders tier 'Scene' + "balanced — no directive", visibly distinct from E2's unset. (Same prompt, DIFFERENT cascade — this is the distinction the old GUI collapsed.)
E4. ANTI-CLOBBER (guards §B): scene inherits chapter 80/20; fire pointerUp on the density slider WITHOUT clicking "Override here" → assert the PUT mutation was NOT called. Today this writes 50/50 and destroys the 80/20.
E5. Clear override: a scene with its own row → click "Clear override" → useDeleteStyleProfile called with (scene, sceneId); readout falls back to the chapter tier.
E6. Unit-test resolveStyle directly against the backend precedence (scene>chapter>work>unset), including the undefined-id skip.

=== F · DEFAULT I AM PICKING (PO may veto) ===
When a scope is unset, the sliders are SEEDED FROM THE INHERITED VALUE (not from 50, not from zero). Rationale: the user's mental model is "I am nudging what is currently in force"; starting them at 50 is exactly the phantom that caused this bug. The inherited seed is visually marked and writes nothing until "Override here" is pressed, so no value is invented and nothing is silently persisted.

=== G · SCOPE NOTE ===
Nothing here contradicts plan 30 §0 (PO-1..4 concern AN-12/Wave 7, G-WORKFLOWS/Track C, ui_show_panel retirement, and spec-before-build sequencing — none touch style/voice). GG-3 classifies most legacy surfaces as verbatim PORTs; EC-1 is the explicit exception — this one is a re-design, and §B is the receipt for why porting it verbatim would ship a data-corruption path into the Studio.

*Evidence:* frontend/src/features/composition/components/StyleVoicePanel.tsx:131 — `<StyleSliders key={scope} density={row?.density ?? 50} pace={row?.pace ?? 50} onCommit={commitStyle} />` (the lie); :104 — `const row = styleQ.data?.find((r) => r.scope_type === scope && r.scope_id === scopeId)` (EXACT match, no cascade); :34 + :44 — `onPointerUp={() => onCommit(d, p)}` / `onKeyUp={() => onCommit(d, p)}` (the lie becomes a WRITE that shadows the inherited row). services/composition-service/app/db/repositories/style_voice.py:86-104 — `resolve()` ... `ORDER BY {_SCOPE_RANK} LIMIT 1` → `return _row_to_style(row) if row else None`; :32 — `_SCOPE_RANK = "CASE scope_type WHEN 'scene' THEN 0 WHEN 'chapter' THEN 1 ELSE 2 END"`. services/composition-service/app/packer/profile.py:32-33 — `density_level: int | None = None` / `pace_level: int | None = None` (None ≠ 50); style_directive() emits only on `d < 34` / `d > 66` (34-66 = balanced = NO directive). services/composition-service/app/packer/pack.py:269-275 — `sp = await style_profile_repo.resolve(...)`; `if sp is not None: profile = _replace(profile, density_level=sp.density, pace_level=sp.pace)`.
