### Q-36-EC3D-USEACTIVEWORK-CONTRADICTION
EC-3d's locked resolution is CORRECT and fully buildable today with ZERO backend work. Build it exactly as follows (M3, one slice, before any of the 7 studio sites are touched).

1) `frontend/src/features/composition/workSelect.ts` (NEW — pure, no hooks):
   - `export function workList(res): Work[]` — normalizes the resolution: `status:'found'` → `[res.work]` (drop null), `status:'candidates'` → `res.candidates`, else `[]`.
   - `export function selectCanonicalWork(works: Work[]): Work | null` → `works.find(w => !w.source_work_id) ?? null`. NULLISH, never `=== null` (`composition/types.ts:19` types it `source_work_id?: string | null`).
   - `export function selectDerivatives(works: Work[]): Work[]` → `works.filter(w => !!w.source_work_id)`.

2) Bus (`frontend/src/features/studio/host/types.ts`):
   - `StudioBusSnapshot` gains `activeWorkProjectId?: string`.
   - `StudioBusEvent` gains `| { type: 'work:switch'; projectId: string | null }` (null = "back to canon").
   - `applyBusEvent` case `'work:switch'`: `if (e.projectId === s.activeWorkProjectId) return base;` otherwise return `{...base, activeWorkProjectId: e.projectId ?? undefined, activeChapterId: undefined, activeSceneId: undefined, selectionRange: undefined, qualityIssueRef: undefined}` — a chapter/scene id belongs to ONE Work's partition; carrying it across a switch opens a chapter that does not exist in the target Work. (Same clearing discipline the `'chapter'` case already applies to `activeSceneId`, types.ts:98.)

3) Hydration (`StudioHostProvider.tsx`, in the existing bookId effect at :112-128): on mount `loadPrefFromServer<string>('lw_active_work.' + bookId, token)` (`frontend/src/lib/syncPrefs.ts:37`) → if truthy, `busStore.set(applyBusEvent(..., {type:'work:switch', projectId}))`. Guard against a book switch racing (the effect is already keyed on bookId; check bookId is still current before setting).

4) `frontend/src/features/composition/hooks/useActiveWork.ts` (NEW — THE resolver; the ONLY thing panels call):
   ```ts
   export function useActiveWork(bookId: string | undefined) {
     const { token } = useAuth();
     const res = useWorkResolution(bookId ?? '', token);           // useWork.ts:7
     const host = useOptionalStudioHost();                          // StudioHostProvider.tsx:143 — null on the legacy page
     const activeId = useSyncExternalStore(
       host ? host._busStore.subscribe : NOOP_SUBSCRIBE,
       () => (host ? host._busStore.get().activeWorkProjectId : undefined),
       () => undefined,
     );
     const works = useMemo(() => workList(res.data), [res.data]);
     const canonical = selectCanonicalWork(works);
     const work = works.find(w => w.project_id === activeId) ?? canonical;   // STALE/ARCHIVED id → canon
     return { work, projectId: work?.project_id ?? null, isDerivative: !!work?.source_work_id,
              canonical, derivatives: selectDerivatives(works), works, loading: res.isLoading };
   }
   ```
   Note the two guards that make this correct and that a naive impl misses: (a) `useOptionalStudioHost` — so the SAME hook is safe on the legacy page (no host ⇒ no bus ⇒ canon), which is strictly better than EC-3c's "legacy 4 call selectCanonicalWork directly"; use `useActiveWork` at ALL 11 FE sites. (b) validate the persisted id against `works` — an archived/deleted derivative must not strand the studio on a dead project_id.

5) `useSwitchWork()` (same file): `async (projectId: string | null) => { host.publish({type:'work:switch', projectId}); await savePrefToServer('lw_active_work.' + bookId, projectId, token); }` — publish FIRST (instant UI), then the awaitable write-through (`syncPrefs.ts:24`). The divergence panel's "Switch to" and the banner's "back to canon" both call this. NO write to `work.settings` (per-book blob, shared across collaborators — that is the `entity_kinds` tenancy bug re-shipped).

6) Replace `candidates[0]` at the 11 FE sites with `useActiveWork(bookId).projectId`: ManuscriptUnitProvider.tsx:138, useManuscriptJump.ts:48, useManuscriptTree.ts:55, EditorPanel.tsx:189, useQualityWork.ts:49, useSceneInspector.ts:31, useChapterBrowserGroups.ts:89, CompositionPanel.tsx:156, OutlineTree.tsx:118, usePublishGate.ts:51, ChapterEditorPage.tsx:218. BE site 12 (`internal_model_settings.py:85`): `row = next((r for r in rows if not r.source_work_id), None); settings = (row.settings if row else {}) or {}` — and delete the now-false "rows[0] is the canonical manifest" comment.

TESTS (the DoD): (a) `workSelect.test.ts` — derivative sorted first still resolves canonical; a `source_work_id: undefined` fixture still resolves. (b) `useActiveWork.test.tsx` — bus set to derivative ⇒ derivative; no host ⇒ canonical; persisted id NOT in candidates ⇒ canonical (archived-derivative case). (c) hydration test — pref `lw_active_work.<bookId>` present at mount ⇒ EditorPanel + useQualityWork + useSceneInspector + useManuscriptTree ALL report the derivative's project_id (this is the reload test that a bus-only impl fails). (d) `work:switch` reducer clears activeChapterId/activeSceneId.

⚠ ONE CORRECTION to M3's stated DoD (spec line 570): the hygiene test must NOT assert the literal string `candidates[0]` appears nowhere in `frontend/src`/`services/` — 5 legitimate, unrelated hits exist (glossary `resolveDisplayValue.ts:35`, model-picker `PlannerPanel.tsx:77`, `SceneAnchor.ts:112`, `prose_doc.py:77`, `pass2_writer.py:218/541/543`) and the test would red on day one. Scope the grep to the work-resolution shape: `/\.candidates\[0\]/` in files that import `useWorkResolution`/`resolve_by_book`, i.e. assert no file importing the work resolution touches `.candidates[0]` (and that `rows[0]` is gone from internal_model_settings.py).

DEFAULT the PO may veto: `useActiveWork` (not `selectCanonicalWork`) is used at the 4 legacy sites too, via the optional-host fallback. It is behaviour-identical to EC-3c there (no host ⇒ canon) but removes the "which lane am I in" judgment call from the builder, which is precisely the mistake EC-3d exists to prevent.

*Evidence:* frontend/src/features/studio/host/types.ts:36-37,73-74 (bus has NO active-Work concept; StudioContextSlice/StudioBusSnapshot carry only chapter/scene/selection/quality) · types.ts:91-110 (applyBusEvent — the 'chapter' case already clears activeSceneId, the pattern 'work:switch' must follow) · frontend/src/features/studio/host/StudioHostProvider.tsx:143 (useOptionalStudioHost — the seam that lets ONE hook serve studio + legacy) and :112-128 (the bookId mount effect where hydration lands) · frontend/src/lib/syncPrefs.ts:24 (savePrefToServer) and :37 (loadPrefFromServer) · services/auth-service/internal/api/server.go:180-181 (GET/PATCH /v1/me/preferences, JSON-merge — EC-3d needs ZERO backend work) · the 12 position-as-identity sites confirmed at HEAD by grep: ManuscriptUnitProvider.tsx:138, useManuscriptJump.ts:48, useManuscriptTree.ts:55, EditorPanel.tsx:189, useQualityWork.ts:49, useSceneInspector.ts:31, useChapterBrowserGroups.ts:89, CompositionPanel.tsx:156, OutlineTree.tsx:118, usePublishGate.ts:51, ChapterEditorPage.tsx:218, services/composition-service/app/routers/internal_model_settings.py:85 (`settings = (rows[0].settings if rows else {}) or {}`, with the comment that documents the false assumption) · frontend/src/features/composition/types.ts:19 (`source_work_id?: string | null` — why the predicate must be `!w.source_work_id`) · unrelated candidates[0] hits that break a naive hygiene grep: frontend/src/features/glossary/lib/resolveDisplayValue.ts:35, frontend/src/features/plan-forge/components/PlannerPanel.tsx:77, frontend/src/components/editor/SceneAnchor.ts:112, services/composition-service/app/engine/prose_doc.py:77, services/knowledge-service/app/extraction/pass2_writer.py:218

### Q-36-EC3C-CANDIDATES0-12-SITES
CONFIRMED: all 12 sites exist at the named lines, and the fix is real (not a no-op). BUILD IT AS FOLLOWS — one slice, shipped WITH the divergence panel.

**Why the predicate is law, not a heuristic:** `migrate.py:121` creates `UNIQUE ON composition_work(book_id) WHERE source_work_id IS NULL AND status='active'` — the DB guarantees EXACTLY ONE canonical Work per book. So `!w.source_work_id` selects exactly one row, and a `candidates` list of len>1 is definitionally `1 canon + N derivatives`. Verified the field reaches the wire: `models.py:68` (`source_work_id: UUID | None`) -> `works.py:34` (`_SELECT_COLS` includes it) -> `routers/works.py:79` (`candidates=[w.model_dump(mode="json") for w in res.works]` — a FULL dump). If the response model had dropped it, `!w.source_work_id` would be true for every work and the fix would silently still return candidates[0] (the repo's REST-mirror-drops-fields bug class). It does not. Ship it.

**NEW FILE `frontend/src/features/composition/workSelect.ts`** — three exports (the spec named two; add the third, see below):
```ts
import type { Work, WorkResolution } from './types';
// DB law: migrate.py:121 partial-unique index => at most ONE active canonical
// Work per book. The `?? candidates[0]` tail is NOT dead: returning null would
// make CompositionPanel loop on "set up co-writer" forever (see CompositionPanel:150).
export function selectCanonicalWork(candidates: Work[]): Work | null {
  return candidates.find((w) => !w.source_work_id) ?? candidates[0] ?? null;
}
export function selectDerivatives(candidates: Work[]): Work[] {
  return candidates.filter((w) => !!w.source_work_id);
}
// Collapses the ternary that is copy-pasted at ALL 11 FE sites.
export function resolveActiveWork(res: WorkResolution | undefined): Work | null {
  if (res?.status === 'found') return res.work ?? null;
  if (res?.status === 'candidates') return selectCanonicalWork(res.candidates ?? []);
  return null; // unmarked_single/unmarked_candidates/none/unavailable — UNCHANGED
}
```
**THE THIRD EXPORT IS THE POINT (spec correction #1).** The spec's `selectCanonicalWork(candidates)` alone leaves the SAME ternary (`status==='found' ? res.work : status==='candidates' ? candidates[0] : null`) copy-pasted at 11 sites — the actual duplication — and lets site #12 re-grow the bug. Every FE site calls `resolveActiveWork`, not the raw array helper.

**11 FE EDITS** — replace the whole ternary, do not just swap the index:
- 6 project_id sites -> `resolveActiveWork(d)?.project_id ?? null`: ManuscriptUnitProvider.tsx:138, useManuscriptJump.ts:48, useManuscriptTree.ts:55, useQualityWork.ts:49, useSceneInspector.ts:31, useChapterBrowserGroups.ts:89.
- 3 Work-object sites -> `resolveActiveWork(workResolution.data)`: EditorPanel.tsx:189, ChapterEditorPage.tsx:218, OutlineTree.tsx:118 (`resolveActiveWork(res)`).
- usePublishGate.ts:51 -> `resolveActiveWork(res)`.
- CompositionPanel.tsx:156 -> `activeWorkOverride ?? deepLinkWork ?? resolveActiveWork(res)`. **PRESERVE the `activeWorkOverride`/`deepLinkWork` precedence above it** (CompositionPanel:147-156) — the `?work=` deep-link must still win over the canon; that is D-04, already shipped.

**1 BE EDIT — `services/composition-service/app/routers/internal_model_settings.py:83-86`.** Replace:
```python
rows = await works.resolve_by_book(book_id)
settings = (rows[0].settings if rows else {}) or {}
```
with:
```python
rows = await works.resolve_by_book(book_id)
# PM-4: the canonical manifest is the row with source_work_id IS NULL (migrate.py:121
# partial-unique index guarantees at most one active). NOT rows[0] — resolve_by_book
# is ORDER BY created_at, project_id, which only accidentally puts the canon first.
canonical = next((r for r in rows if r.source_work_id is None), None) or (rows[0] if rows else None)
settings = (canonical.settings if canonical else {}) or {}
```
Also REWRITE the :83 comment — it currently *documents the wrong assumption* ("rows[0] is the canonical manifest"), which is how a future agent reverts this. Fix the comment at its source (the file's own PM-14 anti-revert rule, :14-16).

**TESTS (each must FAIL before the fix):**
- `frontend/src/features/composition/__tests__/workSelect.test.ts` (new): candidates ordered **DERIVATIVE FIRST** -> `selectCanonicalWork` returns the canon; `selectDerivatives` returns only the derivative; `resolveActiveWork` returns canon for 'candidates', `res.work` for 'found', null for 'unmarked_candidates'; all-derivatives edge -> falls back to `candidates[0]` (NOT null).
- Per-site: at minimum EditorPanel + useQualityWork + useManuscriptTree — mock `useWorkResolution` with `status:'candidates'`, derivative first -> assert the CANON's project_id. A fixture with the canon first passes either way and proves nothing.
- `services/composition-service/tests/unit/test_internal_model_settings.py` (exists): add a case where `resolve_by_book` returns `[derivative, canonical]` -> assert the response carries the CANONICAL work's `model_roles`.
- ⚠ `CompositionPanelDeepLink.test.tsx:84,89` ("falls back to candidates[0]") stays green only because its fixture puts the canon first. Rename those to "...falls back to the CANONICAL work" and flip the fixture order so they actually assert the new behavior.

### Q-36-PANEL-COUNT-NEVER-A-LITERAL
CONFIRMED BY CODE — the drift-lock is already relational; the builder must add ZERO count assertions. Binding instruction:

(1) NO LITERAL COUNT, ANYWHERE. Do not write `57`, `60`, `66`, `69` (or any absolute number) into a test, a DoD line, or a review note for spec 36. The three-way lock (py enum == contract enum == openable) is ALREADY enforced as a set-equality by shipped tests and needs no change:
  - `frontend/src/features/studio/panels/__tests__/panelCatalogContract.test.ts:28` — every advertised `panel_id` is a buildable dock component; `:33-34` — sorted contract enum `toEqual` sorted `OPENABLE_STUDIO_PANELS.map(p=>p.id)`; `:40-42` — every openable panel has a `category`. No `.length`, no number.
  - `services/chat-service/tests/test_frontend_tools.py:168-172` — enum non-empty / all-strings / no-dupes. Its comment at `:153-156` records that a hand-copied literal list WAS there and "drifted stale at least twice" — it was deliberately deleted. Do not resurrect it in any form (count or list).
  So the correct behavior when a wave adds a panel is: the set-equality tests go red until all three sources are updated. That IS the lock. A count assertion adds nothing and creates the phantom-regression trap.

(2) REGISTRATION = EXACTLY 3 EDITS per new panel, in this order:
  a. `frontend/src/features/studio/panels/catalog.ts` — add a `STUDIO_PANELS` row: `{ id, component, titleKey, descKey, category, guideBodyKey }`. `category` is MANDATORY (omit it → `panelCatalogContract.test.ts:40` reds). `STUDIO_PANEL_COMPONENTS` (`:275`) and `OPENABLE_STUDIO_PANELS` (`:279`) are DERIVED — never hand-edit them.
  b. `services/chat-service/app/services/frontend_tools.py:402` — append the id to `UI_OPEN_STUDIO_PANEL_TOOL`'s `panel_id.enum`, and append its clause to the description block (`:404-478`).
  c. Regenerate the contract: from `services/chat-service`, `WRITE_FRONTEND_CONTRACT=1 pytest tests/test_frontend_tools_contract.py` (the writer branch is `test_frontend_tools_contract.py:135`), and COMMIT `contracts/frontend-tools.contract.json`.

(3) IF a wave wants an explicit delta check, it is an EVIDENCE-STRING check at VERIFY time, never a committed test. Measure N_before at the START of the milestone (not the start of the wave), then re-measure after:
    `python -c "import json;print(len(json.load(open('contracts/frontend-tools.contract.json'))['ui_open_studio_panel']['args']['panel_id']['enum']))"`
  and paste `N_before=<x> N_after=<y> delta=+1` into the milestone's VERIFY evidence. Re-measuring per-milestone (rather than per-wave) also DISSOLVES the ordering coupling the question flags: M1/M2/M3's `N+1` / `N+2` / `N+3` are only cumulative-from-wave-start; expressed as "this milestone's own N_before + 1" they hold regardless of whether M1→M2→M3 land in order or a milestone slips. Builder: read M1/M2/M3's `N+1` / `N+2` / `N+3` as "+1 panel each, delta re-measured at that milestone", NOT as absolute cumulative targets.

(4) The spec text is already correct — no edit needed: `36_editor_craft_ports.md:451-457` ("the drift-lock is an equality, not a number… Assert `N_before + 3 == N_after` … never a literal") and `:579` (which explicitly strikes the wrong `60 == 60 == 60` cut). Baseline verified today at HEAD 9262ed53e: contract `panel_id.enum` = 57 members — recorded here as PROVENANCE ONLY. Waves 1–5 land 9 panels upstream, so the wave-6 baseline will be ~66; any builder who sees 66 instead of 57 must treat that as EXPECTED, not a regression, and must not go hunting.

  - `chapterId`/`sceneId` come from the studio host / `ManuscriptUnitProvider` (as ComposePanel does via `useManuscriptUnitMeta`), never from `CompositionPanel` state.

### Q-36-EC3D-STUDIO-BUS-HAS-NO-ACTIVE-WORK
BUILD IT IN M3 — and it is FE-ONLY. Reclassify the item from BE_PREREQ to FE: the "hydrate from /v1/me/preferences" dependency ALREADY EXISTS end-to-end (route: auth-service/internal/api/server.go:180-181; FE wrapper: frontend/src/lib/syncPrefs.ts loadPrefFromServer/savePrefToServer). No route to write. M3's only BE dep stays BE-13a (name).

Do exactly this, in one commit, in M3:

(1) BUS — frontend/src/features/studio/host/types.ts. Add ONE field to StudioBusSnapshot: `activeWorkId?: string` — the surrogate `Work.id`, NOT `project_id`. [DELIBERATE REFINEMENT of EC-3d's `activeWorkProjectId` name; PO may veto. Reason from code: Work carries BOTH `project_id` (types.ts:4, NULLABLE for a lazy greenfield Work, :11-13) AND surrogate `id` (:13), and the EXISTING deep-link already matches on the surrogate — `(w.id ?? w.project_id) === deepLinkWorkId`, CompositionPanel.tsx:148. `source_work_id` also self-refs the surrogate. Storing a surrogate into a field named/read as a project_id = a comparison that silently never matches → falls back to canon → the "survives reload" DoD fails invisibly. ONE identity on the wire = the surrogate.] Add event `| { type: 'work:switch'; workId: string }` to StudioBusEvent and a reducer case in applyBusEvent: `return { ...base, activeWorkId: e.workId }`.

(2) RESOLVER — new frontend/src/features/composition/hooks/useActiveWork.ts, exporting `useActiveWork(bookId): Work | null`. It owns the ONE precedence ladder (this is the thing EC-3d leaves undecided and the build would stall on):
    `?work=` deep-link (explicit, this navigation)  >  bus `activeWorkId` (switch-to / hydrated pref)  >  `selectCanonicalWork(candidates)` (fallback).
    Match a candidate by surrogate: `(w.id ?? w.project_id) === id` (reuse CompositionPanel.tsx:148's expression verbatim — do not re-derive it). Consumers that need the API key read `.project_id` OFF the returned Work; they never re-resolve.
    A resolved deep-link ALSO writes through (publish `work:switch` + persist), so URL and pref converge instead of fighting on the next reload.

(3) HYDRATION — in StudioHostProvider. The busStore is created inside `useMemo([bookId])` with a literal initial value (StudioHostProvider.tsx:63-71), so an async pref CANNOT seed it there. Add a small effect in the provider, keyed on `[bookId, token]`, that calls `loadPrefFromServer<string>('lw_active_work.' + bookId, token)` and, on a hit, `publish({type:'work:switch', workId})`. This is synchronization, not event-handling — it is the allowed useEffect shape per CLAUDE.md. GUARD: skip hydration entirely when `searchParams.get('work')` is present, or the late publish CLOBBERS the deep-link (silent C28 regression — the Living World Tree's openWork navigates to `/books/{bookId}?work={node.id}`, LivingWorldTree.tsx:56-58).

(4) PERSIST — the `Switch to` handler (and (2)'s write-through) calls `savePrefToServer('lw_active_work.' + bookId, workId, token)`. The key MUST be that FLAT dotted string, NOT a nested `{lw_active_work: {[bookId]: …}}` object: the server merge is Postgres jsonb `||`, which is SHALLOW (`prefs = user_preferences.prefs || $2`, handlers.go:860) — a nested object would CLOBBER every other book's active Work on each switch. Per-user (not work.settings) is already correct per EC-3d and is the tenancy rule.

(5) DELETE the old source of truth — `const [activeWorkOverride, setActiveWorkOverride] = useState<Work|null>(null)` (CompositionPanel.tsx:134) and its use at :154. This local useState IS the reload-drops-you-to-canon bug EC-3d exists to kill; leaving it in place = two sources of truth. `onDerivedWork` now publishes `work:switch` + persists instead of setting local state. CompositionPanel then reads `useActiveWork(bookId)` like every other site.

(6) CONSUMERS — every site currently reaching for `candidates[0]` reads `useActiveWork()` instead, never `selectCanonicalWork` directly. The real FE surface (grep-verified, 12 files, matching EC-3c's "all 12 sites"): CompositionPanel.tsx, EditorPanel.tsx, useQualityWork.ts, useSceneInspector.ts, useManuscriptTree.ts, useManuscriptJump.ts, ManuscriptUnitProvider.tsx, OutlineTree.tsx, usePublishGate.ts, PlannerPanel.tsx, useChapterBrowserGroups.ts, ChapterEditorPage.tsx, SceneAnchor.ts. NOTE: `selectCanonicalWork` does NOT exist in the tree today (0 hits) — it is net-new in M3 alongside this, per EC-3c.

TESTS (the DoD, all vitest):
  a. reducer: `applyBusEvent(snap, {type:'work:switch', workId:'w2'})` sets activeWorkId AND bumps revision.
  b. THE test that proves EC-3d and that a bus-only impl fails: mount studio → switch to a derivative → REMOUNT with a fresh bus (no in-memory state) with the prefs GET stubbed to return `{'lw_active_work.<bid>': 'w2'}` → Editor, navigator, scene-inspector and quality panels are ALL still on the derivative.
  c. precedence: with pref='w2' AND `?work=w3`, the resolved Work is w3 (deep-link wins) — the anti-clobber guard.
  d. identifier: a Work with `project_id: null` + surrogate `id` still resolves (the nullable-project_id trap).
  e. hygiene: `candidates[0]` appears nowhere in frontend/src outside tests (grep the pattern, not a count).

*Evidence:* BE dep already exists (kills the BE_PREREQ label): services/auth-service/internal/api/server.go:180-181 (GET+PATCH /v1/me/preferences) + frontend/src/lib/syncPrefs.ts (loadPrefFromServer/savePrefToServer). SHALLOW merge forces the flat dotted key: services/auth-service/internal/api/handlers.go:860 `prefs = user_preferences.prefs || $2`. ### Q-36-EFFECTREGISTRY-MUST-BE-REGEXP
CONFIRMED trap — use a RegExp, and drop the id segment. Build it as follows (M1, BE-10 Lane-B leg):

**1. Add `styleVoiceEffect` to `frontend/src/features/studio/agent/handlers/bookEffects.ts`** (composition effects already live in this file alongside `outlineEffect`; `registerDefaultEffectHandlers` is the single registration chokepoint):

```ts
/** M1 / BE-10 — after an agent style/voice write: refresh the panel + the grounding preview.
 * Keys are ['composition','<kind>',projectId] but EffectContext only carries bookId (project_id
 * is a field ON the Work, useWork.ts:56) — so prefix-invalidate WITHOUT the id, exactly as
 * outlineEffect does. Grounding is keyed [...,projectId,nodeId,guide]; the prefix covers it. */
export function styleVoiceEffect(ctx: EffectContext): void {
  ctx.queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['composition', 'style-profiles'] });
  ctx.queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['composition', 'voice-profiles'] });
  ctx.queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['composition', 'grounding'] });
}
```

**2. Register it inside `registerDefaultEffectHandlers()`** (bookEffects.ts:55-63), as a **RegExp**, writes-only:

```ts
registerEffectHandler(/^composition_(style|voice)_(upsert|delete)$/, styleVoiceEffect);
```

NOT the bare string `'composition_(style|voice)_'` — `effectRegistry.ts:42`'s string branch is `tool === p || tool.startsWith(p)`, so that string matches NOTHING and the handler is a silent no-op. Exclude `_list` (BE-10's six tools are `composition_{style,voice}_{list,upsert,delete}`); effects fire after writes only.

**3. Tests (`handlers/__tests__/bookEffects.test.ts`) — must exercise the REAL registration, not a fake.** The whole point is that a test which registers its own pattern and calls it cannot see this bug. So:
- `registerDefaultEffectHandlers(); expect(matchEffectHandlers('composition_style_upsert')).toHaveLength(1)` — and the same for `composition_voice_upsert`, `composition_style_delete`, `composition_voice_delete`. This single assertion reds if anyone swaps the RegExp for a string.
- `expect(matchEffectHandlers('composition_style_list')).toHaveLength(0)`.
- Run `styleVoiceEffect` with a spied `queryClient` and assert `invalidateQueries` was called with each of the three **3-segment** keys — assert the key has NO 4th element, which pins the bookId≠projectId fix (a test asserting `[...,'style-profiles', bookId]` would enshrine the second silent no-op).
- Note `registerDefaultEffectHandlers` is guarded by a module-level `registered` flag (bookEffects.ts:8,56) — call `clearEffectHandlers()` in `beforeEach` and reset that flag, or the second test in the file registers nothing.

Sane default I am picking (veto-able): writes-only matching, and prefix-invalidate-without-projectId rather than plumbing a new `projectId` into `EffectContext`. Over-invalidating another work's cached profiles is free (one Work is open at a time); widening `EffectContext` is a cross-cutting change M1 does not need.

*Evidence:* frontend/src/features/studio/agent/effectRegistry.ts:42 — `return typeof pattern === 'string' ? tool === pattern || tool.startsWith(pattern) : pattern.test(tool);` (string branch is exact-or-prefix, NOT a pattern match → `'composition_(style|voice)_'` matches nothing). Correct precedent already in the target file: frontend/src/features/studio/agent/handlers/bookEffects.ts:62 — `registerEffectHandler(/^composition_(outline_node|scene_link)_/, outlineEffect);`. The bookId≠projectId trap + its fix: bookEffects.ts:48-49 (`// Outline queries are keyed ['composition','outline',projectId] — prefix-invalidate them all.` → `invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['composition','outline'] })`), EffectContext carries only `bookId` (effectRegistry.ts:12), and project_id is a field on the Work (frontend/src/features/composition/hooks/useWork.ts:56 `if (w.project_id)`). The three keys: frontend/src/features/composition/hooks/useStyleVoice.ts:6-7 (`['composition','style-profiles',projectId]` / `['composition','voice-profiles',projectId]`) + :23-25,36-37,56-57,67-68 (each write also invalidates `['composition','grounding',projectId]`, commented "the resolved style surfaces in the grounding preview profile"); grounding's full key is 5 segments — useWork.ts:145 `['composition','grounding',projectId,nodeId,guide]` — so prefix invalidation is required, not incidental. Tool names from BE-10: docs/specs/2026-07-01-writing-studio/36_editor_craft_ports.md:434 (`composition_style_upsert · _style_delete · _style_list · composition_voice_upsert · _voice_delete · _voice_list`).

### Q-36-BE20-DECOMPOSE-COST-GATE
BUILD IT, exactly as BE-20 scopes it, and DO NOT touch the REST route's spend behavior. Four slices:

(a) MCP propose tool `composition_decompose` — services/composition-service/app/mcp/server.py, insert directly after `composition_conformance_run` (ends :3186). Copy that tool verbatim in shape. Args class `_DecomposeArgs(ForbidExtra)`: `project_id: str`, `structure_template_id: str`, `premise: str`, `model_ref: str`, `model_source: str`, `pipeline: bool = False`, `motifs_enabled: bool = False`, `thread_state: bool = False` (mirrors DecomposeRequest, plan.py:70-87). Body: `tc = _ctx(ctx)`; `meta = await _book_or_deny(WorksRepo(get_pool()), tc, pid, GrantLevel.EDIT)`; verify the template exists via `StructureTemplatesRepo(get_pool()).get(tc.user_id, UUID(args.structure_template_id))` → `raise uniform_not_accessible()` on None (H13); mint a service bearer (`mint_service_bearer(tc.user_id, settings.jwt_secret)`, as server.py:485 already does) and call `_book_chapter_ids(book_client, meta.book_id, bearer)` (import from app.routers.plan) ONLY to COUNT chapters for the estimate; then mint the confirm token with `mint_confirm_token(settings.confirm_token_signing_secret, tc.user_id, pid, _DECOMPOSE_DESCRIPTOR, payload)`. Payload carries ONLY the small scalars — {project_id, structure_template_id, premise, model_ref, model_source, pipeline, motifs_enabled, thread_state, estimate_usd}. LOAD-BEARING: do NOT resolve chapters/cast/beats into the payload — the payload is embedded in the signed token and a 40-chapter roster + cast would blow the token size; the effect re-resolves them at confirm time (see (c)). meta = `require_meta("W", "book", async_job=True, tool_name="composition_decompose", synonyms=["decompose the outline","plan scenes","break chapters into scenes","run the planner","scene plan"])`. Return {confirm_token, descriptor, title: "Decompose the outline into scenes", domain: "composition", requires: "human confirmation — this spends LLM tokens", estimate}. Estimate helper (new, next to `_mine_estimate` at server.py:271) — **default I am picking, veto if you disagree**: `_decompose_estimate(*, chapter_count: int, pipeline: bool)` → `usd = max(0.25, round(0.02 * chapter_count, 2))`, `× 3.0 if pipeline` (the multi-step pipeline is ~6 LLM stages vs one); returns `{"estimated_usd": usd, "currency": "USD", "basis": f"{chapter_count} chapters"}`. Rationale: `_mine_estimate`'s flat $0.50 under-reserves a per-chapter pass on a long book, and the precheck is explicitly coarse ("gates the obvious over-quota case", server.py:272-276).

(b) Descriptor — actions.py: add `_DECOMPOSE_DESCRIPTOR = "composition.decompose"` beside `_CONFORMANCE_RUN_DESCRIPTOR` (:75) and add it to `_ALL_DESCRIPTORS` (:96-101). It is WORK-scoped (payload has project_id) → it needs NO new branch in the confirm dispatch's book/user-scoped prefix; it falls through to the shared Work re-resolve + `authorize_book(..., EDIT)` at :313-330. Change the dispatch tail (:344-346) from an unconditional `return await _execute_conformance_run(...)` to an explicit `if claims.descriptor == _CONFORMANCE_RUN_DESCRIPTOR: return await _execute_conformance_run(...)` followed by `return await _execute_decompose(...)` — leaving the bare fallthrough would route a decompose token into conformance.

(c) `_execute_decompose` — actions.py, immediately after `_execute_conformance_run` (:714-750). Signature mirrors it: `(payload, project_id, work, envelope_user, *, token, claims)`. Body, in order: `await _claim_or_replay(token, claims)` → `await _precheck_or_402(owner_user_id=envelope_user, job_id=_billing_job_id(token), estimate_usd=float(payload.get("estimate_usd") or 0.0))` → resolve the job input → `job_id = await _enqueue_motif_job(envelope_user=envelope_user, project_id=project_id, operation=("plan_pipeline" if payload.get("pipeline") else "decompose_preview"), spec=job_input)` → return `{"outcome": "action_accepted", "descriptor": _DECOMPOSE_DESCRIPTOR, "job_id": job_id, "poll": "composition_get_generation_job"}`. (Poll tool is `composition_get_generation_job`, server.py:524 — NOT `composition_get_mine_job`; both read GenerationJobsRepo with the same project_id IDOR check, but the mine poller is documented as motif-only.) `_enqueue_motif_job` (:533) already stamps `input={"worker_op": operation, **spec}`, which is exactly what `_worker_op` (job_consumer.py:285) and `SUPPORTED_OPERATIONS` (worker/constants.py:37) expect — `decompose_preview` and `plan_pipeline` are ALREADY in the supported set and already dispatch to `run_decompose` / `run_plan_pipeline` (job_consumer.py:302-308). No worker change at all.
   To resolve `job_input` WITHOUT duplicating the route: EXTRACT the arg-resolution block from plan.py's `decompose_preview` (:508-610 — the `_require_work`/template-404/`_book_chapter_ids`+NO_CHAPTERS/TOO_MANY_CHAPTERS guards/`_cast_roster`/`from_settings`/`ChapterPlan` build/`motif_genres`+`motif_applied_counts`, ending in the `job_input` and `pipe_input` dicts) into ONE new module-level coroutine in plan.py:
   `async def build_decompose_job_input(*, work, project_id, user_id, bearer, body, book, kal, templates) -> tuple[str, dict]` returning `(operation, job_input)`. Rewrite BOTH the REST route (call it, then `jobs.create(..., operation=op, mode="auto", ...)` + `enqueue_job` exactly as today) AND `_execute_decompose` (which mints its own bearer via `mint_service_bearer(envelope_user, settings.jwt_secret)` — the MCP path has no JWT, same trick `_execute_generate` uses at :388-397 — and rebuilds a `DecomposeRequest` from the payload scalars) to call it. The NO_CHAPTERS/TOO_MANY_CHAPTERS 400s then also protect the agent path for free. Do NOT copy-paste those 100 lines into actions.py.

(d) ALSO ADD `composition_decompose_commit` (Tier-A MCP write, no confirm token, no cost gate — it is a pure DB persist, zero LLM spend). Without it BE-20 half-closes its own inverse gap: the agent can propose a tree and read the job result but has no way to persist it except ~N calls to `composition_outline_node_create`. Wrap `POST /works/{pid}/outline/decompose/commit` (plan.py:647) — `_book_or_deny(..., EDIT)`, then `OutlineRepo.commit_decomposed_tree(...)`, reusing the route's existing idempotency_key + already-planned guards verbatim. `meta=require_meta("A", "book", tool_name="composition_decompose_commit")`.

WHAT NOT TO DO — the REST route `POST /works/{pid}/outline/decompose` keeps its current behavior (no precheck, no 402). Grounding: `grep -rn precheck app/` in composition-service returns call sites ONLY inside actions.py; ZERO composition REST routes precheck, and the engine's `/generate` route doesn't either. A human clicking "Decompose" in the Studio IS the consent that the confirm token exists to obtain from the agent (GG-1: the GUI is the deterministic human door). Adding a 402 to the GUI path would be an unprecedented behavior change to a shipped human surface and is out of BE-20's scope. Also note for the builder: the question's premise that `generate` prechecks is WRONG — `_execute_generate` (actions.py:388) has NO `_precheck_or_402`; the precheck belongs strictly to the async worker-enqueue family (motif_mine :642, arc_import :692, conformance_run :722), which is exactly the family `decompose` joins, so `_execute_decompose` DOES precheck.

TESTS (per the "checklist ⇒ test the effect" law):
- tests/unit/test_mcp_actions.py — (1) `composition_decompose` returns a confirm_token whose decoded descriptor == "composition.decompose" and whose payload has NO `chapters`/`cast` key (asserts the small-payload invariant); (2) confirming it enqueues a generation_job with `operation`/`input["worker_op"] == "decompose_preview"` (and `"plan_pipeline"` when `pipeline=True`) and returns `outcome == "action_accepted"`; (3) with billing precheck stubbed False → 402 `quota_exhausted` AND **assert no generation_job row was created** (the fail-closed gate is the whole point); (4) replaying the same token → 409 `already_consumed`; (5) a token minted for user A confirmed as user B → 400 (H13 uniform).
- tests/unit/test_plan.py — `build_decompose_job_input` produces a byte-identical `job_input` dict to the pre-refactor route (pin the key set), so the extraction cannot silently drop `thread_state` / `motifs_enabled` / `motif_genre_tags` / `book_id`.
- Add the new tool to the MCP catalog/enum contract test if `tests/contracts/` pins the tool list (check `tests/contracts/` before finishing — a new tool that isn't registered there reds the contract).

### Q-36-WORKLESS-STATE-FIRST-CLASS
CONFIRMED as a build constraint, with two corrections the builder MUST apply. The gate already exists and is correct; the CTA does not. Retrofit, don't re-derive.

CORRECTION 1 — the spec's status list is INCOMPLETE. `work_resolution.py:94-109` has SIX statuses; FOUR are Work-less (`none`, `unmarked_single`, `unmarked_candidates`, and — separately — `unavailable` which is "we could not look"). The spec omits `unmarked_candidates`. RULE: map to `ready` ONLY when a projectId actually resolves; NEVER by enumerating the Work-less statuses. (`if (status==='none'||status==='unmarked_single')` lets `unmarked_candidates` reach `ready` with an undefined projectId — the exact crash this constraint forbids.) The shipped gate already does it by exclusion (useQualityWork.ts:45-52); keep that shape.

CORRECTION 2 — `useQualityWork.ts:15-17`'s comment is FALSE and must be fixed in the same slice: it claims "`candidates` / `unmarked_*` — the book HAS Works." Per work_resolution.py:107, `unmarked_*` = 0 marked Works. Only `candidates` (>1 marked) means Works exist. The code is right; the prose will mislead the next reader into treating `unmarked_single` as `ready`.

BUILD:
1. `git mv frontend/src/features/studio/panels/useQualityWork.ts → useWorkGate.ts`; rename export `useQualityWork`→`useWorkGate`, `QualityWorkState`→`WorkGateState`. Update the 5 quality call sites. Per EC-3c/EC-3d, `ready.projectId` must come from `useActiveWork(bookId)`, NOT `candidates[0]` (useQualityWork.ts:49 is 🔴 site #5 in spec 36's own table, line 148).
2. NEW `frontend/src/features/composition/components/WorkSetupCta.tsx` — the ONE Work-less CTA ("Set up the co-writer for this book") → `useCreateWork(bookId, token)`. It MUST carry the `usePendingWorkResolver` handoff (useWork.ts D-C16): onSuccess, if `!created.project_id` → `pendingResolver.start(created.id)` and render its `resolving` ("Finishing setup…") / `failed` (+Retry) states. WITHOUT this, a create during a knowledge outage returns a pending Work that the resolution query EXCLUDES → refetch says `none` → the button looks like it did nothing (silent-success bug). Take an optional `onCreated?: (w: Work) => void` so CompositionPanel.tsx:262-292 passes its guided-first-scene logic and its inline copy is DELETED — one name, one concept. Do NOT copy the guided-scene auto-create into the shared component (it needs a chapterId the new panels don't have).
3. `QualityNoWorkState.tsx` → `WorkGate.tsx`. `loading`→Skeleton; `unavailable`→ keep `WorkUnavailableState` as-is (an ERROR, NEVER a CTA — offering "create" while composition is down invites a DUPLICATE Work; the file already argues this at :29-30); `no-work`→ replace the dead-end sentence at :21-23 ("start composing a chapter first") with `<WorkSetupCta bookId={...} />`.
4. All three spec-36 panels (`style-voice`, `reference-shelf`, `divergence`) render `<WorkGate state={useWorkGate(bookId, token)} testIdPrefix="…" />` and use `work.projectId` unconditionally after it. No spinner, no crash, no empty list.
5. plan-hub Decompose (spec 36 §414): gate the button on the SAME `useWorkGate(bookId)`. `no-work` → `disabled` + visible reason ("Decompose needs a co-writer Work — set one up first") AND an inline `<WorkSetupCta>` (PH7 visible-fallback means the user can ACT, not just read a reason). `unavailable` → disabled + "Could not reach the co-writer service." `loading` → disabled. Never a dead button.

TESTS (each is a literal DoD line):
- `useWorkGate` unit: all 6 statuses → the 4 kinds; explicitly assert `unmarked_single` AND `unmarked_candidates` → `no-work` (not `ready`, not `unavailable`).
- `WorkSetupCta` unit: create resolves `{project_id: null}` → asserts `pendingResolver.start` was called and "Finishing setup…" renders (the silent-success guard).
- Per-panel (×3 + plan-hub): `status:'none'` → setup-button testid present, NO skeleton, NO empty-list copy; plan-hub asserts decompose `disabled` AND a non-empty reason string.

DEFAULT THE PO MAY VETO: `unavailable` deliberately gets NO create CTA (error state, retry only). If they'd rather offer create-anyway there, that's a one-line change in WorkGate.

### Q-36-CRITIC-SKIPPED-UNLESS-DISTINCT
Build it in THREE parts. The question asks only for copy; the code shows copy alone is insufficient — the skip is currently invisible AND actively misleading.

(A) CONFIG-TIME — the Critic row in the Composition section (EC-4). ModelPicker writes `settings.model_roles.critic` (NOT `critic_model_ref` — EC-4/SET-8). Two pieces of copy:
  1. Always-on hint under the row (the honest warning, verbatim per spec 36 line 391): "The critic is skipped unless it is a different model from the drafter."
  2. A LIVE predictive warning: when the selected critic `model_ref` === the effective composer `model_ref`, render an inline amber note, `data-testid="composition-critic-same-as-composer"`, text: "Same model as the drafter — critiques will be SKIPPED. Pick a different model." Do NOT block the write (the user may intend a per-session drafter override); warn only.

(B) RUN-TIME — CriticPanel is the AUTHORITATIVE surface, and this is the load-bearing fix. The gate compares against `job.input.model_ref` (engine.py:1645) — the model the JOB ran with — NOT the composer setting. So (A) is only a prediction; the BE `warning` string is the truth. Today it is dropped on the floor: `api.ts:557` types `warning?` and no consumer reads it, so a skipped critique resolves `verdict → null` (CriticPanel.tsx:42-49) and falls into the `critic-empty` branch (CriticPanel.tsx:82-87) rendering "No verdict yet — generate a scene (or re-check the current draft)…" — i.e. the user clicks "Re-check current draft", it runs, and the panel tells them to re-check the current draft. FIX: in CriticPanel, when `critique.data?.warning` is present (or a refetched job carries no critic and no distinct critic is configured), render a distinct state `data-testid="critic-skipped"` INSTEAD of `critic-empty`: "Critique skipped — the critic model is not set, or is the same model as the drafter. Set a different Critic model in Book settings → Composition." Include a deep-link to that section. This state must win over `critic-empty`.

(C) BE-21 TRAP — `resolve_model_role(settings, role)` must default `model_source` to "user_model" when the map entry omits it, mirroring internal_model_settings.py:56. The gate at engine.py:1649 fails on a missing `critic_src` just as hard as a missing ref, and the existing drafter picker (CompositionSettingsView.tsx:47) already writes a bare ref with no `_source` — so a ModelPicker that writes only `model_ref` would silently re-trigger "critique skipped" and look like BE-21 never landed.

DoD/test guidance (this is what the question means by "will look broken"): M4a's behaviour test "critic model set ⇒ the critique is no longer skipped" MUST set the critic to a model DIFFERENT from the job's `input.model_ref`. Setting it equal to the composer still yields "critique skipped" — that is correct behaviour, not a BE-21 regression. Add the paired negative test: critic == drafter ⇒ response carries the warning AND the panel renders `critic-skipped` (not `critic-empty`).

Default I am picking (PO may veto): warn, do not block. A user with one BYOK model can still save a critic == drafter and gets an honest "skipped" everywhere, rather than being locked out of the control.

*Evidence:* services/composition-service/app/routers/engine.py:1645 (`drafter_ref = (job.input or {}).get("model_ref")` — the gate compares against the JOB's model, not the composer setting); :1649 (`if not critic_ref or not critic_src or str(critic_ref) == str(drafter_ref)`); :1656 (the warning string). frontend/src/features/composition/api.ts:557 (`critique(): Promise<{critic; warning?}>` — `warning` typed but zero consumers: `grep -rn "critique.data" frontend/src` shows CriticPanel reads only `.critic`). frontend/src/features/composition/components/CriticPanel.tsx:42-49 (verdict resolves to null on a skip) → :82-87 (misleading `critic-empty` copy: "No verdict yet — generate a scene (or re-check the current draft)"). frontend/src/features/composition/components/CompositionSettingsView.tsx:47 (`patch({ default_model_ref: e.target.value })` — the only model writer; no `_source`, no critic). services/composition-service/app/routers/internal_model_settings.py:56,62-64 (the dual-read + the `model_source or "user_model"` default BE-21 must mirror). ### Q-36-CAPTURE-CORRECTION-PROSE-GATES-WAVE1
**Wave 1 is NOT blocked. Ship BE-9 unchanged. The toggle is M4a's, it is ~15 lines of FE JSX, and the entire BE half already exists and is already tested.**

**(a) What Wave 1's BE-9 builder must know — and must NOT do.**
The structural signal is captured **unconditionally**: `kind`, `changed_blocks`, `chosen_candidate_index`, `winner_index`, `candidate_count` are all computed and stored regardless of the flag (`engine.py:1740-1758`, `:1776-1786`). ONLY `raw_before`/`raw_after` are gated (`engine.py:1766`). So the flywheel *works* on day one — it just learns from structure, not prose. Wave 1's builder therefore: **does NOT build a toggle** (it is M4a's, SET-8 one-home), **does NOT block or defer**, and **MUST treat `raw_before`/`raw_after = NULL` as the NORMAL case in the learning consumer** — not an error, not a degraded path, not a skipped row. A consumer that requires prose to mine a correction is a bug, because default-OFF is the permanent majority case.

**(b) M4a's slice — build it exactly as spec 36 already specifies it (§4 row "Capture correction prose", line 395).**
Add ONE row to `<CompositionSettingsSection>` (the migrated `CompositionSettingsView`), cloning the existing `narrative_thread_enabled` checkbox verbatim — it is a working template 50 lines up in the same file:
- `frontend/src/features/composition/components/CompositionSettingsView.tsx` — after the narrative-thread block (`:76-92`), add: `const captureProse = settings.capture_correction_prose === true;` (the `=== true` **is** the defaults-OFF guarantee — `undefined` → `false`), and a checkbox with `data-testid="composition-settings-capture-correction-prose"`, `checked={captureProse}`, `disabled={setSettings.isPending}`, `onChange={(e) => patch({ capture_correction_prose: e.target.checked })}`. It goes through the existing `patch()` → `useSetWorkSettings` (`useWork.ts:131-138`), which merges `{...currentSettings, ...patch}` — so no other settings key is dropped.
- **Label copy is the spec's, verbatim (the "must say what it does" requirement):** *"Store the verbatim before/after prose of each correction so the model can learn your taste. Off = structural signal only."* Source-tier chip: **book**.
- **Forward-only — say so in the hint, and do NOT build a backfill.** Flipping ON cannot recover prose for corrections already stored; those rows are NULL by construction (`models.py:206`, `migrate.py:315`) because the prose was never written. This is by design (the no-raw-text privacy default), not a gap.

**(c) The BE needs ZERO new work — verify before writing any.** The route (`works.py:581` `PATCH /v1/composition/works/{project_id}`, accepts `settings`), the gate (`engine.py:1766`), and **both** unit tests already exist: default-OFF asserts `raw_before is None and raw_after is None` (`test_correction_router.py:195`) and ON asserts the prose is stored (`:200`). M4a's DoD line *"`capture_correction_prose` on ⇒ `raw_before/raw_after` are stored"* is **already green on the BE**. The only red is that no human can flip it.

**(d) The one test M4a adds.** Mirror `CompositionSettingsView.test.tsx`'s existing *"toggling narrative_thread MERGES the patch (never drops the other keys)"* case: assert `patchWork` is called with `{...currentSettings, capture_correction_prose: true}`, and that turning it **OFF sends `capture_correction_prose: false`** — a key **drop** would silently revert to the default and read as a phantom success.

**Default I am picking (PO may veto):** the toggle is **per-book** (on the Work's `settings`), not per-user, exactly as spec 36 states — a user may reasonably want prose capture on for their own draft novel and off for a client's manuscript, and the book is where that line is drawn. Nothing in plan 30 §0 (PO-1..4) touches this.

*Evidence:* GATE (the only thing the flag controls): `services/composition-service/app/routers/engine.py:1766` — `if bool(work.settings.get("capture_correction_prose", False)):` → sets `raw_before`/`raw_after`. STRUCTURAL CAPTURE IS UNCONDITIONAL (proves Wave 1 is not blocked): `engine.py:1740-1758` (changed_blocks/chosen_index) + `:1776-1786` (`corrections.create` always runs). WRITE PATH ALREADY EXISTS: `services/composition-service/app/routers/works.py:581` (`PATCH /works/{project_id}`, accepts `settings`). FE MERGE HOOK ALREADY EXISTS: `frontend/src/features/composition/hooks/useWork.ts:131-138` (`useSetWorkSettings` spreads `{...currentSettings, ...patch}`). THE TEMPLATE TO CLONE: `frontend/src/features/composition/components/CompositionSettingsView.tsx:28` (`const ntEnabled = settings.narrative_thread_enabled === true;`) + `:76-92` (the checkbox), mounted at `frontend/src/features/composition/components/CompositionPanel.tsx:891`. BE ALREADY TESTED BOTH WAYS: `services/composition-service/tests/unit/test_correction_router.py:195` (default OFF ⇒ both NULL) and `:200` (ON ⇒ prose stored). NULL-BY-DEFAULT IS BY DESIGN: `services/composition-service/app/db/models.py:206`, `services/composition-service/app/db/migrate.py:315`. No conflict with plan 30 §0 PO-1..4.

### Q-36-GG4-MOBILE-BLOCKER
**DECIDED — and it does not block this build. Two parts: (a) OQ-2 is answered by the code: KEEP. (b) The mobile hole is real but it is NOT "deletion deletes the mobile surface" — it is "the nav already stranded mobile users in the dock". Fix (b) with a 20-line redirect in M5.**

**(a) OQ-2 = KEEP — answer it now, do not escalate it.** `ChapterEditorPage.tsx:1-18` already states the sealed outcome: *"a decision to keep it around, not a decision pending removal (spec 16 Phase 4b, 2026-07-05: kept indefinitely, not deleted)."* The retirement was **CANCELLED**, so "M9 gates deletion on M6" gates a deletion nobody has authorized. **Builder instruction: `ChapterEditorPage.tsx` and its route (`App.tsx:134`) are NOT deleted in wave 36 or any wave of plan 30. Nothing in M1–M5 depends on deleting it.** Its new, positive job: it is the **mobile chapter-editing surface** (deprecated on desktop, supported on mobile). Rewrite the banner at `ChapterEditorPage.tsx:1-18`: keep the "do not port new capabilities here / do not edit" clauses, strike *"never linked to from the app UI"* (no longer true — see (b)), and add: *"KEEP — this page is ALSO the ONLY mobile chapter-editing surface (MobileEditorShell, line 844). WritingStudioPage redirects mobile viewports here. It may not be deleted until a Studio mobile shell exists — D-STUDIO-MOBILE-SHELL."*

**(b) The concern MIS-STATES the bug — and the true bug is live today, not hypothetical.** Deletion is not what strands mobile users; **the nav already did.** Every in-app door to a chapter goes to the Studio: `BooksPage.tsx:143`, `BookDetailPage.tsx:113`, `book-tabs/ChaptersTab.tsx:153` (`/books/${bookId}/studio?chapter=${ch.chapter_id}`). And `WritingStudioPage.tsx:11-19` has **no mobile branch whatsoever** — it mounts `StudioFrame` unconditionally, whose entire mobile concession is a collapsed sidebar (`useStudioChrome.ts:13-16`). So a phone user tapping a chapter row gets a 68-panel dockview on a 390px screen, and `MobileEditorShell` — which is built, mounted at `ChapterEditorPage.tsx:844`, and tested (`__tests__/MobileEditorShell.test.tsx`) — is reachable only by hand-typing a URL. This is the repo's `built-mounted-unreachable` class, shipped.

**BUILD THIS in wave 36 M5 (slice M5c — ~20 LOC + 1 test, in scope because M5 IS the GG-4 gate):**
1. `frontend/src/pages/WritingStudioPage.tsx` — add `import { Navigate } from 'react-router-dom'` + `import { useIsMobile } from '@/hooks/useIsMobile'`. Call `const isMobile = useIsMobile();` **after** `useParams`/`useSearchParams` and **before** any return (no conditional hooks). Then, before `return <StudioFrame .../>`:
   `if (isMobile && bookId) return <Navigate replace to={initialChapterId ? \`/books/${bookId}/chapters/${initialChapterId}/edit\` : \`/books/${bookId}\`} />;`
   (no `?chapter` ⇒ send them to the book's Chapters tab, whose rows link back through `/studio?chapter=…` and therefore re-enter this same redirect — the loop composes, it does not cycle.)
2. **Test** `frontend/src/pages/__tests__/WritingStudioPage.mobile.test.tsx`: mock `window.matchMedia` to `(max-width: 767px) => matches:true`, mock `StudioFrame`, render at `/books/B1/studio?chapter=C9` inside a `MemoryRouter` with a catch-all route echoing the location → assert the landed path is `/books/B1/chapters/C9/edit`; assert `StudioFrame` was NOT rendered. Desktop case (`matches:false`) → assert `StudioFrame` IS rendered with `initialChapterId="C9"`.
3. **Machine-check the gate** (spec 36 §10's parity contract test, same file): add
   `it('the Studio has no mobile shell → the legacy editor route must stay mounted', () => { expect(readFileSync('src/App.tsx','utf8')).toContain('/books/:bookId/chapters/:chapterId/edit'); });`
   with a comment naming D-STUDIO-MOBILE-SHELL. Whoever deletes the route reds this test and is forced to confront the mobile hole instead of discovering it in production. That is exactly the "gate = a test, not a comment" discipline §10 already asks for.
4. Spec edits: in `36_editor_craft_ports.md`, rewrite §10 item 2 (line 624-629) and **OQ-2 (line 691)** to *"ANSWERED 2026-07-13 (Q-36-GG4): KEEP. The page is retained as the mobile surface + deprecated desktop fallback. It is not deleted in plan 30. Deletion is re-considered only after D-STUDIO-MOBILE-SHELL ships."* OQ-2 leaves the open-questions table.

**Reclassify the defer row** (line 708): `D-STUDIO-MOBILE-SHELL` is **NOT** gate #4 (product decision) — nothing is waiting on the PO. It is **gate #2 (large/structural)**: a Studio mobile shell is a real, buildable, multi-slice track (a mobile group-bar over the dock: Editor / Studio panel switcher / History, mirroring `MobileEditorShell`'s three-group pattern, driven by `useIsMobile()` at `StudioFrame`). It is unbuilt work, not a blocker.

**PO default I am picking (veto if you disagree):** mobile users get the legacy editor, not a broken dock, and the legacy page lives on indefinitely as that surface. The alternative — building a Studio mobile shell inside wave 36 — is a wave of its own and would delay every editor-craft port for a surface that already works.

*Evidence:* frontend/src/pages/ChapterEditorPage.tsx:1-18 (banner: "kept indefinitely, not deleted" — the retirement was already CANCELLED, so there is no deletion for M6 to block) · frontend/src/pages/ChapterEditorPage.tsx:844 (MobileEditorShell mounted — the working mobile surface) · frontend/src/pages/WritingStudioPage.tsx:11-19 (mounts StudioFrame unconditionally — ZERO mobile branch) · frontend/src/features/studio/hooks/useStudioChrome.ts:13-16 (the entire Studio mobile concession) · frontend/src/pages/book-tabs/ChaptersTab.tsx:153 + frontend/src/pages/BookDetailPage.tsx:113 + frontend/src/pages/BooksPage.tsx:143 (every in-app chapter door → /books/:bookId/studio — mobile is ALREADY stranded, today) · frontend/src/App.tsx:134 (the legacy route that must stay) · docs/specs/2026-07-01-writing-studio/36_editor_craft_ports.md:624-629, :691 (OQ-2), :708 (the defer row)

### Q-36-GG4-EDITORBRIDGE-SINGLETON
KEEP `editorBridge`, and FIX THE FALSE PREMISE IN THE ROW — it does not "die with the page." The code says there are TWO registrants and one is the STUDIO: `frontend/src/features/studio/panels/EditorPanel.tsx:100` registers `{bookId, chapterId, handleRef, applyProposedEdit}` (the checkpoint-wrapped hoist action), and `frontend/src/pages/ChapterEditorPage.tsx:284` registers the legacy one. The consumer is `frontend/src/features/chat/components/ProposeEditCard.tsx` at lines 55 (selection snapshot), 70 (chapter guard) and 100 (apply). Deleting ChapterEditorPage removes ONE of TWO registrants; deleting `editorBridge.ts` with the page breaks Studio propose_edit Apply on every AI edit (getEditorTarget() -> null -> "no editor"). The row as written instructs a future builder to do exactly that.

BUILDER INSTRUCTION — 3 concrete edits, all in spec 36's M5 (the wave that ships the GG-4 mechanical gate). Do NOT touch runtime behavior.

(1) `docs/specs/2026-07-01-writing-studio/36_editor_craft_ports.md`, "The GG-4 gate" item 3 (lines ~630-633): replace the paragraph with the corrected fact — "`editorBridge` is NOT legacy-only and does NOT die with the page. `features/studio/panels/EditorPanel.tsx:100` is a live registrant (it hands over the checkpoint-wrapped `applyProposedEdit`); `pages/ChapterEditorPage.tsx:284` is the second. Deleting the page removes one registrant, not the module. Killing the singleton is a REPLACEMENT REFACTOR — point `ProposeEditCard`'s three `getEditorTarget()` reads at `ManuscriptUnitProvider` context (reachable: `StudioFrame.tsx:137` hoists the provider ABOVE `StudioDock`, so the chat panel is inside it) — not a delete, and it cannot land while the legacy page (which has no Tier-4 hoist) still consumes the bridge."

(2) Rewrite the defer row (spec 36 line 709 + the same row in SESSION_HANDOFF): keep ID `D-EDITORBRIDGE-SINGLETON`; change gate #3 (naturally-next-phase / "dies with the page") to **gate #2 (large/structural — a replacement refactor across 3 surfaces)**; change the trigger to: "AFTER ChapterEditorPage is deleted (OQ-2, still open) AND ProposeEditCard is migrated to read the target from ManuscriptUnitProvider context. Scope: ProposeEditCard.tsx:55,70,100 (3 reads) + EditorPanel.tsx:100-101 (registrant) + delete editorBridge.ts + editorBridge.test.ts. The popout relay path (`popoutRelayContext` / `StudioPopoutHost`) is unaffected — a popout is a separate JS realm and already has neither the singleton nor the context."

(3) MECHANIZE IT so the false premise cannot be re-acted-on (a comment is the weakest guard — `built-mounted-unreachable-duplicated-nav-list`). Add to `frontend/src/features/chat/__tests__/editorBridge.test.ts` a hygiene test in the pattern spec 36 already sanctions for the retirement grep: read the `frontend/src` tree, collect files IMPORTING `registerEditorTarget` (match the import, not the literal token — `hygiene-grep-literal-token-in-comment-false-positive`), and assert at least one is OUTSIDE `src/pages/`, with the failure message "editorBridge has a non-legacy registrant (Studio EditorPanel) — do NOT delete it with ChapterEditorPage; migrate ProposeEditCard to ManuscriptUnitProvider context first (D-EDITORBRIDGE-SINGLETON)."

DEFAULT TAKEN (PO may veto): do NOT do the context migration in this wave. It is a pure refactor with zero user-visible gain, it touches the shared chat message chain that serves three surfaces (Studio dock, legacy page, popout), and it is BLOCKED anyway while the legacy page lives — GG-4/OQ-2 keep the page. The wave's deliverable here is the corrected row + the mechanical guard, which is what actually prevents the bug.

*Evidence:* frontend/src/features/studio/panels/EditorPanel.tsx:100 — `registerEditorTarget({ bookId, chapterId, handleRef: editorRef, applyProposedEdit })` (Studio registrant, NOT legacy) with cleanup `return () => registerEditorTarget(null)` at :101. Second registrant: frontend/src/pages/ChapterEditorPage.tsx:284. Consumer: frontend/src/features/chat/components/ProposeEditCard.tsx:55, :70, :100 (three getEditorTarget() calls). Context path exists: frontend/src/features/studio/components/StudioFrame.tsx:137 mounts ManuscriptUnitProvider above StudioDock (closes :171). Contradicted claim: docs/specs/2026-07-01-writing-studio/36_editor_craft_ports.md:630-633 and the defer row at :709.

### Q-36-EC4-NO-BESPOKE-CRITIC-PICKER
AFFIRMED, and extended with the one thing the concern missed (an FE read-site gap). The Composition section is the Book-tier writer of the model cascade. Build it exactly as follows.

The section writes ONLY `work.settings.model_roles.<role> = {model_ref, model_source}` for role in {composer, critic, planner} — the closed set already frozen at `services/chat-service/app/services/settings_resolution.py:28-40` (chat|composer|planner|critic|embedding|rerank). NO `critic_model_ref` picker is added. NO dual-write of the legacy scalar (dual-write = two homes = the SET-8 violation wearing a hat). Each row renders effective value + source tier (book / inherited-from-account), per SET-2.

(2) BE-21 IS A HARD PREREQUISITE — build it in the same slice, before the GUI. LIFT this logic out of `internal_model_settings.py:46-65` — do not write a second copy: `_model_roles_from_settings` must then be re-expressed in terms of the new helper (import it) so the shim has exactly one implementation. Repoint ALL SEVEN engine read sites — `services/composition-service/app/routers/engine.py:465, 529, 1029, 1099, 1261, 1345, 1644` — from `sdict.get("critic_model_source"), sdict.get("critic_model_ref")` to `resolve_model_role(sdict, "critic")`. Scope per OQ-8: only the 7 `critic` sites are re-pointed this wave; the `default_model_ref` (role `chat`) BE readers stay on the shim (row D-WORK-MODEL-ROLES-DEFAULT-REF).

(3) THE FE READ SITES — NEW, and non-optional (this is what the concern did not catch). The legacy scalar has a live FE writer AND two live FE readers today: writer `frontend/src/features/composition/components/CompositionSettingsView.tsx:47` (`patch({ default_model_ref: e.target.value })`, labelled "Default drafter model"), readers `frontend/src/features/studio/panels/EditorPanel.tsx:199` and `frontend/src/pages/ChapterEditorPage.tsx:243` (`work.settings?.default_model_ref` → `persistedDefaultModel` → the model_ref the compose/continue call posts). So: add `frontend/src/features/composition/modelRoles.ts` exporting `resolveModelRole(settings, role): {model_ref, model_source} | null` — the FE mirror of BE-21 (`settings.model_roles?.[role]?.model_ref` first, then the legacy scalar for `composer`←`default_model_ref` / `critic`←`critic_model_ref`). Replace the CompositionSettingsView "Default drafter model" select's `onChange` so it patches `{ model_roles: { ...settings.model_roles, composer: { model_ref: v, model_source: 'user_model' } } }` (a nested merge inside the FE-hand-merged blob; BE-18's shallow `||` merge is at the TOP-level key `model_roles`, so send the whole `model_roles` sub-object). It no longer writes `default_model_ref` at all.

    model = reference_embed_model(work.settings)
    return {
      "references": [r.model_dump(mode="json") for r in rows],

   `async def update_meta(self, project_id: UUID, reference_id: UUID, *, fields: dict[str, str]) -> ReferenceSource | None`
   with a HARDCODED column allowlist {"title","author","source_url"} (build the SET clause from the allowlist, never from caller keys); `WHERE project_id = $1 AND id = $2 RETURNING {_SELECT_COLS}`; row None → return None. Empty `fields` → return `await self.get(project_id, reference_id)` (idempotent no-op, still 200). NEVER writes content/embedding/embedding_model/embedding_dim — a content edit would strand the vector, which is exactly why this route is metadata-only.

   Body: `class ReferenceUpdate(BaseModel)` with `model_config = ConfigDict(extra="forbid")` and `title/author/source_url: Annotated[str, StringConstraints(max_length=500)] | None = None`. `extra="forbid"` is load-bearing: a caller sending `content` must get a 422, not a silently-dropped field that looks like it re-embedded (the rest-write-mirror-drops-fields bug class).
   Update the module docstring route list (references.py:1-18) — it enumerates the routes.
3) Tests (test_references_router.py): PATCH updates title only, leaves author/source_url/embedding_model untouched; PATCH with `content` → 422; PATCH on another user's/another project's reference → 404/403 per the delete tests; assert the EmbeddingClient spy is NEVER called during PATCH (that assertion IS the "no re-embed" contract).
No gateway change: gateway-setup.ts:354 forwards all `/v1/composition/*` generically, all methods.

Mark BE-17 (36:440) and plan 30's BE-17 row (30:311) as IN M2, not deferred; delete the D-REF-UPDATE-AND-MODEL-SURFACE defer row (36:703). OQ-4 (measure real N for the "re-embeds all N" copy) stays open and is unaffected.

=== 3. M5 / GG-4 retirement hygiene — NEW `frontend/src/pages/__tests__/chapterEditorRetirementHygiene.test.ts` ===
Match an IMPORT STATEMENT, never the token: `/(?:^|\n)\s*import\s[^;\n]*?from\s*['"][^'"]*ChapterEditorPage['"]/` plus dynamic `import\(\s*['"][^'"]*ChapterEditorPage['"]\s*\)` and the `require(...)` form. Scan `frontend/src` only (so specs 16/36 are out of scope by construction) and EXCLUDE `pages/ChapterEditorPage.tsx` itself (so the deprecation banner cannot self-trip; the import-regex could not match a comment anyway — belt and braces).
🔴 ASSERT `App.tsx` IS THE SOLE IMPORTER — `expect(importers).toEqual(['App.tsx'])` — NOT "zero importers". "Nothing imports ChapterEditorPage" CONTRADICTS a sealed decision: OQ-2 ("Keep for now"), spec 16 Phase 4b ("kept indefinitely, not deleted") and the file's own banner ("kept alive ONLY as a fallback route reachable by direct URL"). The single import at `App.tsx:27` (route at `:134`) is CORRECT and stays; rewrite the spec-36 §10 test name from `it('nothing imports ChapterEditorPage')` to `it('App.tsx is the ONLY importer of the deprecated ChapterEditorPage')`.

DEFAULT the PO may veto: I did NOT weaken GG-4 to "zero importers" because that would delete a route the PO explicitly voted to keep (OQ-2 stays open, untouched by this).

### Q-36-DECOMPOSE-EFFECT-ON-JOB-COMPLETION
CONFIRMED, and the code makes it STRICTER than the spec states: today the JOB'S COMPLETION also writes nothing to the outline. `decompose_preview`/`plan_pipeline` returns a PLAN and persists nothing (`operations.py:79-110` `run_decompose` → `dataclasses.asdict(result)`); the only outline write is `commit_decomposed_tree` inside `POST /outline/decompose/commit` (plan.py:730). So "invalidate outline on job completion" as literally written would ALSO be a no-op refresh — one level deeper than the concern spotted. Build it as FOUR mechanical steps:

(1) BE-20 — make the job's completion a REAL write, or the handler has nothing to refresh. `_execute_decompose` enqueues `operation="decompose_preview"` with `input.auto_commit=true`, `input.replace=<tool arg>`, `input.arc_title=<template.name>`. Extract plan.py's commit body (plan.py:660-760: IDOR check → EMPTY_DECOMPOSE_PLAN guard → cast validation → story_order stride → `commit_decomposed_tree` → motif ledger) into a shared `_commit_decomposed(...)` helper called by BOTH `decompose_commit` and `run_decompose` (when `input.get("auto_commit")`). The job's terminal `result` becomes `{plan, committed: true, arc_id, scene_ids}`; `EMPTY_DECOMPOSE_PLAN` / `CHAPTER_ALREADY_PLANNED` become the job's failed-result error so the agent renders a real reason (M4b's DoD demands exactly those two). GROUNDING that this is what BE-20 already means: `replace` is a **CommitRequest** field (plan.py:128), NOT a DecomposeRequest field (plan.py:70-87) — yet BE-20 lists `replace?` as a TOOL arg. And there is no MCP commit tool, so a preview-only agent path spends LLM tokens and writes nothing: the repo's own `silent-success-is-a-bug` class. Default is safe: `replace` defaults false ⇒ 409 CHAPTER_ALREADY_PLANNED, and the whole thing is Tier-W confirm-gated with a cost estimate.

(2) FE `compositionEffects.ts` — register NO handler on `/^composition_decompose$/` and NONE on `confirm_action`. `composition_decompose` returns `{confirm_token, descriptor, estimate}` (mirrors actions.py:3172-3187) = nothing happened; `confirm_action` returns `{outcome:"action_accepted", descriptor:"composition.decompose", job_id, poll}` (actions.py:738-741) = only ENQUEUED, still nothing happened.

(3) FE — register the effect on the POLL tool, gated twice:
```ts
registerEffectHandler(/^composition_get_mine_job$/, decomposeJobEffect);

export function decomposeJobEffect(ctx: EffectContext): void {
  const job = unwrapToolResult(ctx.result) as
    { status?: string; operation?: string; project_id?: string } | null;
  if (!job || job.status !== 'completed') return;              // pending/running/failed ⇒ NO effect
  if (job.operation !== 'decompose_preview' && job.operation !== 'plan_pipeline') return;
  // ^ the SAME poll tool serves motif_mine / arc_import / conformance_run — without this
  //   guard a completed conformance run would blow away the outline cache.
  ctx.queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['composition', 'outline'] });                    // bookEffects.ts:49's key
  ctx.queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['composition', 'decompose', job.project_id] });  // useArcMaterialize.ts:16 precedent
  ctx.queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['plan-hub'] });                                  // usePlanNodeWrites.ts:51 precedent
}
```
`unwrapToolResult` (resultEnvelope.ts) is MANDATORY — the live stream nests the domain payload inside the `{ok,result}` envelope, and reading it bare returns undefined while unit tests stay green (bookEffects.ts:19-28 documents that exact bug). `composition_get_mine_job` returns `job.model_dump(mode="json")` (server.py:3207-3222), so `status`/`operation`/`project_id` are all present on the wire (models.py:361-380).

(4) The HUMAN plan-hub Decompose dialog is untouched by Lane-B — it polls its own job inside `compositionApi.decomposePreview` (api.ts:273-289) and commits via `commitDecompose` (api.ts:291); that mutation's own `onSuccess` owns its invalidation. No chat tool call ⇒ the reconciler never sees it ⇒ no double-refresh.

TESTS (this is what makes the concern non-regressible — `frontend/src/features/studio/agent/handlers/__tests__/compositionEffects.test.ts`): feed the reconciler one message whose tool_calls are `[composition_decompose {confirm_token}, confirm_action {outcome:'action_accepted',descriptor:'composition.decompose',job_id}, composition_get_mine_job {status:'running'}]` → assert `invalidateQueries` called **0 times**. Then a 4th call `composition_get_mine_job {status:'completed', operation:'decompose_preview', project_id}` → assert the 3 keys above. Negative: `{status:'completed', operation:'motif_mine'}` → **0 times**.

PO VETO POINT (noted so it can be overridden without a checkpoint): if the PO would rather the agent's decompose stay preview-only (human must accept the tree), then step (1) is dropped AND step (3) must NOT invalidate outline/plan-hub at all — because nothing changed — and BE-20 must drop `replace?` from its arg list. I chose auto-commit because a confirm-gated, cost-estimated, replace=false-by-default job that writes nothing is a paid no-op, which is the exact defect class this run's policy calls CRITICAL.

*Evidence:* services/composition-service/app/worker/operations.py:79-110 (`run_decompose` returns the plan, writes NOTHING) · services/composition-service/app/routers/plan.py:730 (`commit_decomposed_tree` — the ONLY outline write) · plan.py:121-133 (`replace` is a CommitRequest field, not a DecomposeRequest field — yet BE-20 lists it as a tool arg) · plan.py:580-624 (decompose enqueues `operation="decompose_preview"`) · services/composition-service/app/routers/actions.py:738-741 (Tier-W confirm returns `action_accepted`+`job_id` — enqueued, not done) · services/composition-service/app/mcp/server.py:3193-3222 (`composition_get_mine_job` returns `job.model_dump()` → status/operation/project_id; the SAME poll tool serves mine/import/conformance) · services/composition-service/app/db/models.py:361-380 (GenerationJob fields) · frontend/src/features/studio/agent/useStudioEffectReconciler.ts:41-66 (Lane-B fires per SUCCEEDED chat tool call — its only trigger) · frontend/src/features/studio/agent/handlers/bookEffects.ts:19-28,47-52 (envelope-unwrap law + the `['composition','outline']` key) · frontend/src/features/plan-hub/hooks/usePlanNodeWrites.ts:51 (`['plan-hub']` prefix-invalidate precedent) · frontend/src/features/composition/api.ts:273-291 (the human path polls + commits itself — no Lane-B)

### Q-36-F-EC5A-BEATS-FACET-MISSING
BUILD the Beats facet — confirmed ZERO backend work — but with ONE correction to the question's spec: do NOT dead-end on `active_template_id` + deep-link to book-settings. Nothing in this repo ever WRITES `active_template_id` (BE accepts it at routers/works.py:60 + repositories/works.py:42, but FE `patchWork`'s param type is `{settings?, status?}` at composition/api.ts:443 and all 3 callers pass only `settings`), so it is NULL for every real book — the facet would show the empty state 100% of the time. And `book-settings` (studio/panels/BookSettingsPanel.tsx:25) is the BOOK-service tab (title/cover/genre/world); it has no structure control and does not own the composition work, so that deep-link would do nothing (PH7 dead-link/lie class, the exact thing PlanDrawer.tsx:9-12 exists to prevent). THE BEATS FACET ITSELF IS THE SURFACE THAT SETS active_template_id. Build it as:

(1) frontend/src/features/composition/api.ts:443 — widen `patchWork`'s patch type to `{ settings?; status?; active_template_id?: string | null }`. Type-only change; the route already accepts it.

(2) NEW frontend/src/features/plan-hub/hooks/useBeatsFacet.ts (controller; no JSX) — compose two EXISTING hooks: `useWorkResolution(bookId, token)` (composition/hooks/useWork.ts:7 → GET /books/{id}/work, carries project_id + active_template_id) and `useStructureTemplates(token)` (composition/hooks/usePlanner.ts:9 → GET /v1/composition/templates). Resolve `activeTemplate = templates.find(t => t.id === work.active_template_id) ?? null`. Expose `setActiveTemplate(templateId)` = useMutation → `compositionApi.patchWork(work.project_id, { active_template_id: templateId })` → invalidate ['composition','work',bookId]. Return { templates, activeTemplate, setActiveTemplate, saving, error }.

(3) frontend/src/features/plan-hub/components/PlanDrawer.tsx — call `useBeatsFacet(bookId)` in the PlanDrawer body BEFORE the `if (!selectedId) return null` guard (Rules of Hooks; same shape as usePlanNode at :411-412) and thread the result into ChapterSceneFacets. DELETE the read-only `<Field label="Beat role" ...>` at :236 and add `<Section title="Beats" testid="plan-drawer-section-beats">` immediately AFTER Overview (PH16 order):
  • activeTemplate === null → an in-place template `<select>` (reuse BeatSheetView.tsx:104's pattern), options = templates by name, placeholder "— choose a story structure —", copy: "No story structure chosen for this book — pick one to enable beats." onChange → setActiveTemplate. NO deep-link.
  • activeTemplate present → a CLOSED-SET beat `<select>` (never free-text): options = activeTemplate.beats sorted by `order`, value=beat.key / text=beat.label, plus a "— no beat —" option (value '' → null). When node.beat_role is set but NOT in this template's key set, render an extra `<option value={node.beat_role}>{node.beat_role} (not in this structure)</option>` as the selected value — mirroring the unknown-status pattern at PlanDrawerEdit.tsx:151 and BeatSheetView's unmapped semantics at BeatSheetView.tsx:40 — so a template switch never silently rewrites the row. Render the selected beat's `purpose` (migrate.py:1629 carries it) as helper text.
  • onChange → `writes.edit(node.id, node.version, { beat_role: v || null })`. NO new write plumbing: NodeEdit.beat_role exists (plan-hub/api.ts:118), patchNode already sends If-Match (plan-hub/api.ts:139), and usePlanNodeWrites.ts:57-63 already renders 412 as "That node changed elsewhere — the drawer reloaded. Make the edit again." via writes.error (PlanDrawer.tsx:224) — the exact behavior the question asks for, already built.
  • `writes` absent (no EDIT grant) → render the beat's label as a plain read-only `<Field>`, no control (PlanDrawer.tsx:47-48 convention: never render a control that would 403).
  • The setActiveTemplate error gets its own line inside the Beats section.
Keep the shipped Cast & Setting / Craft / Open-threads facets — they are strictly more than spec 24 PH16 lists and are REST-writable; only ADD Beats.

(4) frontend/src/features/composition/components/BeatSheetView.tsx:69 — seed its local `templateId` state from `work.active_template_id` (keep the local override). Today it persists nothing, so the drawer and the Beat Sheet would disagree on which structure the book uses — one concept under two names (DA-10, cited in PlanDrawer.tsx:43-45).

TESTS (frontend/src/features/plan-hub/components/__tests__/PlanDrawer.test.tsx): (a) active template + beat_role='midpoint' → select shows "Midpoint", options == template beats + "— no beat —", and NO text input in the section; (b) change → writes.edit called with (node.id, node.version, {beat_role:'catalyst'}); (c) "— no beat —" → {beat_role: null}; (d) beat_role not in the active template → "(not in this structure)" option is selected and NO write fires; (e) active_template_id null → picker + "No story structure chosen for this book", and picking one calls patchWork with {active_template_id}; (f) no `writes` prop → read-only label, no <select>.

PO NOTE (veto-able default): I chose "the Beats facet sets the book's structure in place" over "send the user elsewhere to choose one", because the elsewhere does not exist. If you'd rather the structure picker live on a dedicated book-level surface, that is a separate (larger) work item — but the Beats facet still cannot ship gated on a field nothing writes.
