### Q-36-DEFERRED-BE13-DIVERGENCE-SPEC-EDIT
**BUILD BE-13 in M3. Do NOT defer it. Delete the D-DIVERGENCE-SPEC-EDIT row and flip EC-3a from read-only to editable.** The spec's premise ("UNBUILDABLE on today's backend — needs new write semantics", 36_editor_craft_ports.md:704) is FALSE: the tables, columns, unique index, repo write-pattern and EDIT gate all already exist, and the packer re-reads overrides fresh on EVERY pack (pack.py:153-157: "an edited override takes effect on the next pack") — so there is no cache, no projection and no snapshot to invalidate. "New write semantics" means, literally, an UPDATE statement. It clears NO defer gate: no migration (columns exist), no refactor (fresh reads self-sync), no cross-service contract (composition-service owns both tables; the panel ships in the same M3 wave). **Re-size M -> S.**

WHY IT MATTERS (not just cheapness): `POST /derive` mints a FRESH knowledge project (works.py:371). A user who mistypes their POV anchor or wants to drop a bad override today CANNOT fix it — they must abandon the derivative and re-derive, losing every drafted chapter. And EC-3a's proposed inline note literally tells the user "editing needs BE-13" — a UI that confesses a missing feature, the inverse of the PO's own SEALED GG-1 honesty axis ("every backend capability a user owns must have a human surface"). Divergence-spec editing today has NO surface at all — not GUI, not agent.

=== BUILDER RECIPE (no further thought required) ===

**1. `services/composition-service/app/db/repositories/derivatives.py`** — add 3 methods, mirroring the existing `create_spec`/`create_override` shape (conn-optional, `_SPEC_COLS`/`_OVERRIDE_COLS` RETURNING):
- `update_spec(work_id, fields: dict) -> DivergenceSpec | None` — build the SET clause DYNAMICALLY from the keys present in `fields`. Do NOT use COALESCE: `pov_anchor=None` is a LEGITIMATE value (clear the anchor), and COALESCE cannot distinguish "clear it" from "don't touch it". `UPDATE divergence_spec SET <present keys> WHERE work_id=$1 RETURNING {_SPEC_COLS}`. Return None if no row.
- `upsert_override(override: EntityOverride) -> EntityOverride` — `INSERT INTO entity_override (...) SELECT ..., w.book_id, ... FROM composition_work w WHERE w.id=$3 ON CONFLICT (work_id, target_entity_id) DO UPDATE SET overridden_fields = EXCLUDED.overridden_fields RETURNING {_OVERRIDE_COLS}`. The ON CONFLICT target MUST match `uq_entity_override_work_target` exactly (migrate.py:175-176). Reuse `_row_to_override`.
- `delete_override(work_id, target_entity_id) -> bool` — `DELETE FROM entity_override WHERE work_id=$1 AND target_entity_id=$2`; return whether a row was removed (parse the `DELETE n` tag).

**2. `services/composition-service/app/routers/works.py`** — add 2 routes (place them after `get_derivative_context`, ~line 480). BOTH must, in this order: (a) `work = await works.get(project_id)`; 404 `NOT_ACCESSIBLE_MESSAGE` if None; (b) `await _gate_book(grant, work.book_id, user_id, GrantLevel.EDIT)` — gate on the LOADED ROW's book_id, never a client-supplied one (copy works.py:353); (c) 409 `{"code":"NOT_A_DERIVATIVE"}` if `work.source_work_id is None`; (d) 409 `{"code":"WORK_NOT_BACKED"}` if `work.id is None` (the pending/lazy-work trap already guarded at works.py:354).
- `PATCH /works/{project_id}/divergence-spec` — body `DivergenceSpecPatchBody(taxonomy: DivergenceTaxonomy | None, pov_anchor: UUID | None, canon_rule: list[str] | None)`; pass `body.model_dump(exclude_unset=True)` to `update_spec` so an EXPLICIT `pov_anchor: null` clears it while an OMITTED key leaves it alone. 404 if `update_spec` returns None. Return the updated spec.
- `PUT /works/{project_id}/overrides/{target_entity_id}` + `DELETE /works/{project_id}/overrides/{target_entity_id}`. **DEVIATION FROM THE SPEC TEXT (flagged for veto):** the spec proposed `POST|PATCH|DELETE /overrides`; use a single idempotent **PUT keyed on `target_entity_id`** instead — the UNIQUE index means one override per entity, so POST-vs-PATCH is a distinction the data model does not have, and PUT collapses them (one name for one concept). DELETE returns 404 when 0 rows matched (NOT a silent 204 no-op — repo lesson `silent-success-is-a-bug`); PUT returns the row.

**3. Do NOT add an MCP tool.** This is deterministic GUI CRUD, no LLM decides anything — the MCP-first invariant does not bite, and REST is consistent with the sibling `/derive` + `/derivative-context` routes.

**4. `D-DECOMP-KEY-COLLIDES-ON-SPEC-BRANCH` STAYS DORMANT** — none of these routes touch `outline_node`. Explicit instruction: **do not copy `outline_node` rows into the derivative partition.** That, and only that, is what fires it (plan 30 §10).

**5. TESTS (the third one is load-bearing — it is the whole point):**
- `tests/unit/test_routers.py`: PATCH updates taxonomy/pov/canon_rule; explicit-null `pov_anchor` CLEARS it while an omitted key preserves it; `canon_rule: []` clears the array; non-derivative -> 409; no-grant -> 404.
- `tests/integration/db/test_repositories.py`: `update_spec`; `upsert_override` on BOTH paths (fresh insert AND the ON-CONFLICT update); `delete_override` returns False for an absent row.
- **`tests/unit/test_pack_override.py` (EXTEND):** PUT an override -> run the pack path -> assert the NEW value reaches `present`. Then DELETE it -> re-pack -> assert the base value is restored. This proves the new writer actually flows through `build_derivative_context`'s fresh read (pack.py:153) end-to-end — a green repo test alone would NOT prove the edit reaches the prompt window.

**6. SPEC EDITS to land with the code:** `36_editor_craft_ports.md` — rewrite EC-3a (:269) to "spec + overrides are EDITABLE (BE-13)" and DELETE the "editing needs BE-13" inline note from the panel table (:374); flip the BE-13 row (:439) from "DEFERRED to v2" to "MUST-BUILD (M3), size S"; DELETE the defer row (:704) -> move to "Recently cleared". `30_TOOL_GUI_GAP_AUDIT_AND_PLAN.md`:307 — re-size BE-13 M -> S. Add BE-13 to the M3 DoD line (:570) next to BE-13a. Per PO policy, `/review-impl` runs at wave close.

**VETO PATH (the default I picked, stated so the PO can overrule):** I chose BUILD over the spec's read-only default because the blocker cited was technical, not a taste call, and the code falsifies it. ### Q-36-REFERENCE-DELETE-NO-UNDO
CONFIRMED by code, and it is a build instruction for M2 (not an open question). Build it exactly like this:

(1) DELETE MUST GO THROUGH THE SHARED ConfirmDialog (DOCK-9 — do NOT hand-roll a `fixed inset-0` overlay; `dockablePanelHygiene.test.ts` scans for that). In `frontend/src/features/studio/panels/ReferenceShelfPanel.tsx`:
  - `const [pendingDelete, setPendingDelete] = useState<ReferenceSource | null>(null)`.
  - The library row's ✕ button (`data-testid={`references-delete-${r.id}`}`) calls `setPendingDelete(r)` — it MUST NOT call `refs.remove.mutate(...)` (that is exactly ReferencesPanel.tsx:132 today, which deletes with no confirm at all).
  - Also `disabled={refs.remove.isPending}` on every ✕ so two deletes cannot be in flight.
  - Render `<ConfirmDialog>` from `@/components/shared` (`frontend/src/components/shared/ConfirmDialog.tsx:36`) with: `open={!!pendingDelete}`, `onOpenChange={(o) => { if (!o) setPendingDelete(null) }}`, `variant="destructive"`, `loading={refs.remove.isPending}`, `confirmLabel` = i18n `panels.reference-shelf.deleteConfirm.confirm` ("Delete permanently"), `onConfirm={() => refs.remove.mutate(pendingDelete.id, { onSettled: () => setPendingDelete(null) })}`.
  - NO `confirmationPhrase`. The typed-phrase escalation in ConfirmDialog (`:26-31`) is reserved for mass destruction (a KG rebuild deleting thousands). One row + an honest cost sentence is the right ceiling. (Default chosen; PO may veto to typed-phrase if they want a harder gate.)

(2) THE COPY — and this is the adjudication that matters: the cost of deleting ONE reference is ONE paid embed call to restore it, NOT "re-embed all N". The "changing the model re-embeds all N" sentence belongs ONLY to the read-only embed-model header (EC-2a, spec 36 :334/:396). Writing it into the delete dialog would be false. Add to `frontend/src/i18n/locales/{en,vi,ja,zh-TW}/studio.json`:
  - `panels.reference-shelf.deleteConfirm.title` = "Delete this reference permanently?"
  - `panels.reference-shelf.deleteConfirm.body` = "“{{label}}” and its embedding are deleted immediately. There is no undo and no trash. To get it back you must paste the passage again — and that costs one paid embedding call ({{model}}, the model this book is locked to)."
  - `{{label}}` = `r.title || r.content.slice(0,60)`; `{{model}}` = the Work's `reference_embed_model_ref` from the header row (fall back to the literal "your embedding model" when the LIST does not carry it — BE-17 is deferred to v2, so the FE renders the model it already knows from the add-time selection/`embed_model_set` header, never a fabricated name).

(3) ADD IS A PAID EMBED CALL — PORT THE EXISTING GUARD, DO NOT DROP IT. `ReferencesPanel.tsx:82` already has `disabled={!canAdd || refs.add.isPending}` and `:86` already swaps the label to "Adding…". Carry both into `ReferenceShelfPanel.tsx` verbatim, plus a first-line `if (refs.add.isPending) return;` in `submit()` (kills Enter-key/double-fire). One add at a time; no second POST until the first settles. There is no queue and no batch add in v1.

(4) TESTS (new `frontend/src/features/studio/panels/__tests__/ReferenceShelfPanel.test.tsx`, all four are required for M2's DoD):
  a. click ✕ → `compositionApi.deleteReference` called ZERO times, dialog is open, its text contains "no undo" and the model name;
  b. click Confirm → `deleteReference` called exactly once with that row's id, dialog closes;
  c. click Cancel → `deleteReference` called ZERO times;
  d. while the add mutation is pending → `references-add-submit` is `disabled` and reads "Adding…"; a second click issues no second `addReference`.

(5) The BE needs NO change. `DELETE /references/{rid}` already derives scope from the row (`routers/references.py:160-165`) and returns `{id, deleted:true}`. This is a pure FE slice — do not open a soft-delete/undo BE track (that is a schema change and is out of M2's scope; if the PO ever wants real undo it is a `deleted_at` column + a restore route, a v2 defer, not this wave).

*Evidence:* services/composition-service/app/db/repositories/references.py:116-125 (`delete()` = hard `DELETE FROM reference_source`; docstring :9-12 "no soft-archive" → row + embedding vector are gone, no undo) · services/composition-service/app/routers/references.py:145-168 (DELETE route, scope from the row, returns `deleted:true`) · frontend/src/features/composition/components/ReferencesPanel.tsx:129-132 (✕ → `refs.remove.mutate(r.id)` with NO confirm — the defect that must not be ported) · ReferencesPanel.tsx:82,86 (add already `disabled={!canAdd || refs.add.isPending}` + "Adding…" — preserve) · services/composition-service/app/routers/references.py:100-140 (POST = a real provider embed call → add is paid) · frontend/src/components/shared/ConfirmDialog.tsx:36-51 (shared dialog API: variant/loading/confirmationPhrase) · docs/specs/2026-07-01-writing-studio/36_editor_craft_ports.md:267 (EC-2a) and :569 (M2 DoD already says "the delete confirm names the re-embed cost")

### Q-36-DEFERRED-REFERENCES-MCP
**KILL the defer row — build the reference MCP tools IN Wave 6, as `BE-10b`, shipped with M2 (`reference-shelf`).** It does not clear any defer gate: gate #3 ("naturally-next-phase") is false — every prerequisite exists at HEAD, and this wave is ALREADY building six MCP tools of exactly this shape (BE-10, style/voice, plan 30 §BE-10 / spec 36 line 304) in the same file, for the same reason (plan 30 **GG-2**, line 44: "a GUI whose domain has no agent tools is also a defect"). Shipping the reference GUI while consciously leaving its inverse half open, in the one wave whose job is closing tool↔GUI gaps, is the defect the plan exists to kill. CLAUDE.md: "if fixing is cheaper than writing + carrying its defer row, just fix it" — this is ~120 LOC against routes that already work.

**BE-10b — `composition_reference_{list,add,delete,search}` · Tier-A · size S · file `services/composition-service/app/mcp/server.py`, mirroring the `composition_canon_rule_*` block at `:1079-1198` verbatim (gate → project-scope → repo → `_meta.undo_hint`):**

1. `composition_reference_list(ctx, project_id)` — `_book_or_deny(works, tc, pid, GrantLevel.VIEW)`; `ReferencesRepo(get_pool()).list(pid)`; return `{"references":[…], "embed_model_set": reference_embed_model(work.settings) is not None}` — mirrors `routers/references.py:79-93`. Read ⇒ no undo_hint.
2. `composition_reference_add(ctx, args{project_id, content, title?, author?, source_url?})` — **deliberately NO `model_ref`/`model_source` args (PO-vetoable default):** the reference embed model is set on first add and is thereafter immutable (`references.py:54-57,134-137`, EC-2a's one-way door). An agent must not silently pick the vector space for the whole Work. So: EDIT gate; if `reference_embed_model(work.settings) is None` → return `{"success": False, "error": "reference_embed_model_unset", "message": "Add the first reference from the reference-shelf panel — the first add permanently fixes this Work's embedding model."}` (a structured refusal, never a raise). Else embed via `get_embedding_client()` (`deps.py:228` — the ONLY embedding path, provider-gateway invariant); on `EmbeddingError` return `{"success": False, "error": "embed_failed", "retryable": exc.retryable}`; then `refs.create(...)`. `_meta.undo_hint = _undo("composition_reference_delete", project_id=…, reference_id=str(ref.id))`.
3. `composition_reference_delete(ctx, project_id, reference_id)` — EDIT gate; **project-scope BEFORE mutating** (`refs.get(pid, rid)` is None ⇒ `uniform_not_accessible()`), then `refs.delete(pid, rid)`; `undo_hint = None`, honestly (re-adding re-embeds and mints a new id — the `canon_rule_delete` precedent at `:1195-1197`).
4. `composition_reference_search(ctx, project_id, node_id, q?, limit=8)` — VIEW gate; **do NOT re-implement the query-seed + degrade logic**: lift the body of `search_references` (`references.py:194-224`) into one shared helper (e.g. `app/services/reference_search.py::retrieve_for_scene`) called by BOTH the router and the tool (`css-var-duplicated-across-two-consumers-drifts`). Keep the neutral-empty degrade (`{"hits":[], "embed_model_set":…, "unavailable": true}`) — never raise on a provider outage — and the pin/exclude annotation from `GroundingPinsRepo.list_for_scene`.

**Cost:** add/search embed one passage/query — the single cheap provider call spec 36 §Cost gates already blesses as a **direct, non-Tier-W** call. No confirm spine, no new convention (AN-8).

**Registration:** the 3-schema-source FastMCP caveat applies exactly as for BE-10 (memory `knowledge-mcp-three-schema-sources-fastmcp-strips`) — update all three sources. **Lane-B (X-4):** in `frontend/src/features/studio/agent/handlers/compositionEffects.ts` (Wave 1 creates it; EXTEND) add `registerEffectHandler(/^composition_reference_/, …)` — a **RegExp, not a string** (`effectRegistry.ts:41` does `tool === p || startsWith(p)`) — invalidating `['composition','references',pid]` and `['composition','references','search',pid]`, the exact keys `frontend/src/features/composition/hooks/useReferences.ts:16-17` uses. **Discovery scent:** one clause in `stream_service.py`'s `book_context_note`, sequenced after Track C lands, same constraint BE-10 already carries.

### Q-36-SWITCH-TO-CROSS-PANEL-EFFECT
BUILD IT AS **BUS + A PERSISTENCE TIER** — the concern is half-right: the bus is the live cross-panel channel, but a bus-ONLY implementation fails the M3 DoD ("Switch to survives a reload"), because the bus is in-memory. So: the durable home of the active Work is a **per-user server preference**; the bus is what panels read; `useActiveWork(bookId)` is the ONLY resolver any panel calls. This is exactly spec 36 EC-3d (36_editor_craft_ports.md:272) — it does not contradict it, it makes it buildable. Four slices, no ambiguity:

**M3-EC3d-A · the bus gains an active-Work concept** — `frontend/src/features/studio/host/types.ts`:
1. `StudioBusEvent` (currently ends at `planFocusNode`, :67) — add `| { type: 'workSwitch'; workId: string; projectId: string; bookId: string }`.
2. `StudioBusSnapshot` (:69-90) — add `activeWorkId?: string; activeWorkProjectId?: string;`.
3. `applyBusEvent` (:92) — add `case 'workSwitch': return { ...base, activeWorkId: e.workId, activeWorkProjectId: e.projectId, activeSceneId: undefined };` — **clear `activeSceneId`**: scene ids are `outline_node` ids scoped to a *project* (`useSceneInspector.ts:26-32` fetches the node by `projectId`), so a scene carried across a Work switch 404s/edits the wrong Work. Keep `activeChapterId` (book-scoped, still valid).
4. `StudioContextSlice` (:35) — add `activeWorkProjectId?: string` so the agent rack sees which Work the user is in.

**M3-EC3d-B · new `frontend/src/features/composition/hooks/useActiveWork.ts`** — signature `useActiveWork(bookId: string | null): { workId: string|null; projectId: string|null; isDerivative: boolean; switchTo(w: Work): Promise<void> }`.
- Resolve: `activeWorkProjectId` from `useStudioBusSelector` ?? `selectCanonicalWork(candidates).project_id` (EC-3c's helper is the FALLBACK, never a panel's direct call).
- **Hydrate on mount** (this is the slice that passes the reload DoD): `loadPrefFromServer<{work_id:string;project_id:string}>(\`lw_active_work.${bookId}\`, token)` — the helper already exists at `frontend/src/lib/syncPrefs.ts:37-48`. **Validate the loaded id against the live candidate list**; if the Work is gone/archived, fall back to canon and clear the pref. Then `publish({type:'workSwitch',…})` exactly once.
- `switchTo(w)`: **persist THEN publish** — `await savePrefToServer(\`lw_active_work.${bookId}\`, {work_id:w.id, project_id:w.project_id}, token)` (`syncPrefs.ts:22-34`, the awaitable variant) and only then `publish`. A fire-and-forget publish that outruns a failed PATCH is the false-fresh bug class.
- **Key shape is load-bearing:** flat dotted key `lw_active_work.<book_id>`, NOT a nested `lw_active_work: { <bookId>: … }` object. `PATCH /v1/me/preferences` is a **top-level** JSON merge (`prefs || $2` — `syncPrefs.ts:5`), so a nested object would be REPLACED wholesale and switching Book B would wipe Book A's active Work.
- Home = the caller's own `/v1/me/preferences`, **not** `work.settings` (that blob is per-book and shared — one user switching would move every collaborator's Editor: the `entity_kinds` tenancy bug re-shipped).

**M3-EC3d-C · every consumer reads the bus, nobody re-derives** — all 7 studio sites (Editor/`DerivativeBanner`, navigator, scene-inspector, quality panels, divergence panel, plan hub, agent rack) call `useActiveWork(bookId)` and NOTHING calls `selectCanonicalWork` or `candidates[0]` directly. Fix the live violation at `frontend/src/features/studio/panels/useSceneInspector.ts:31` (`d.candidates[0]?.project_id`). Ship the hygiene test from the M3 DoD: `candidates[0]` appears nowhere in `frontend/src` or `services/` outside tests.

**M3-EC3d-D · the banner is derived, never a singleton** — `DerivativeBanner` renders iff `useActiveWork().isDerivative`, and `useDerivativeContext` is called with the ACTIVE `projectId`. No module-level "current work" singleton, no local `useState` in the divergence panel.

**The DoD test that proves it** (`frontend/src/features/composition/hooks/__tests__/useActiveWork.test.tsx`): mock `loadPrefFromServer` → `{work_id:'w-d1',project_id:'proj-d1'}`, **fresh mount, never call `switchTo`** (a mount IS a reload), then assert the bus snapshot carries `activeWorkProjectId==='proj-d1'` AND that the Editor banner renders AND `useSceneInspector`'s `projectId==='proj-d1'` — while the candidate list still sorts canon first. A bus-only implementation fails this test at the first assertion.

*Evidence:* frontend/src/features/studio/host/types.ts:41-67 (StudioBusEvent — chapter/scene/selection/qualityIssue/panels/notificationsUnread/startGuidedTour/planFocusNode; NO work event) and :69-90 (StudioBusSnapshot — no activeWorkId/activeWorkProjectId) — confirms "the bus has no active-Work concept today". frontend/src/lib/syncPrefs.ts:5 (PATCH /v1/me/preferences is a TOP-LEVEL JSON merge), :22-34 (savePrefToServer — awaitable), :37-48 (loadPrefFromServer) — the persistence tier already exists, nothing to build server-side. frontend/src/features/studio/panels/useSceneInspector.ts:26-32 — the live `candidates[0]?.project_id` re-resolution that would silently drag the scene-inspector back to canon. docs/specs/2026-07-01-writing-studio/36_editor_craft_ports.md:272 (EC-3d) + :570 (M3 DoD: "Switch to survives a reload … the one a bus-only implementation fails").

### Q-36-DECOMPOSE-REPLACE-AND-EMPTY-PLAN
DECIDED — and the spec's own prose is WRONG on one fact the builder must not copy: the already-planned refusal is a **409 `CHAPTER_ALREADY_PLANNED`**, not a 400 (plan.py:734-739). Fix that line in spec 36 while building. The full working pattern ALREADY EXISTS on the legacy page — M4b PORTS it (GG-3), it does not invent it. Four concrete changes:

**(1) Already-planned = 409, handled BOTH proactively and reactively (port `usePlanner`).**
- REACTIVE (the authoritative one — the guard runs INSIDE `commit_decomposed_tree`'s Tx to close a TOCTOU race, so it can fire even when the tree looked unplanned at dialog time): in the new plan-hub decompose hook (`frontend/src/features/plan-hub/hooks/useDecompose.ts`, new), copy `usePlanner.ts:38-48` (`asPlannerError` — reads `err.body.detail.code` + `.chapter_ids`) and `usePlanner.ts:115-133` (`doCommit(replace)` → `onError`: `if (pe.status === 409 && pe.code === 'CHAPTER_ALREADY_PLANNED') setNeedsReplace(pe.chapterIds)` else `setError(pe)`), exposing `commit: () => doCommit(false)` / `confirmReplace: () => doCommit(true)` / `cancelReplace`. Render the confirm block as `PlannerView.tsx:105-114` does: title `plan.replace_title`, body `plan.replace_prompt` ({{count}} = `needsReplace.length`), buttons `plan.replace_confirm` / `plan.cancel`. i18n keys ALREADY EXIST at `frontend/src/i18n/locales/en/composition.json:416-419` — reuse them, do not mint new ones.
- PROACTIVE (this is the "explicit checkbox" the CONCERN asks for): the plan-hub tree already knows whether the target chapter node has scene children, so the `FormDialog` (structure ▾ · premise · model) carries a **`Replace the existing N scenes` checkbox, default UNCHECKED, rendered ONLY when the chapter node has ≥1 scene child**, wired to `replace` on the commit payload. It is a convenience, NOT the gate — the 409 handler above stays, because the checkbox cannot see a concurrent write.

**(2) `EMPTY_DECOMPOSE_PLAN` today renders as the literal string `EMPTY_DECOMPOSE_PLAN` — that is the "something went wrong" bug, and it is REAL at HEAD.** The BE puts its prose under `detail.**detail**` (plan.py:682-687: `{"code": …, "detail": "the plan has no scenes for any chapter — the planner likely degraded…"}`), but `frontend/src/api.ts:152` picks `o.message ?? o.code` — `.detail` is never read, so the thrown Error's message is the bare code. And `PlannerView.tsx:26-32`'s `errorText` maps only NO_CHAPTERS / TOO_MANY_CHAPTERS / BAD_ENTITY / BAD_CHAPTER — `EMPTY_DECOMPOSE_PLAN`, `BAD_REFERENCE`, `CONSTRAINT` all fall through. Two fixes, both required:
  - `frontend/src/api.ts:152` → `const picked = o.message ?? o.detail ?? o.code;` (widen the FastAPI `{code, detail}` picker — fixes the whole class, one line; add a unit test asserting a `{detail:{code,detail}}` 400 throws with the prose, not the code).
  - Port `errorText` into `frontend/src/features/plan-hub/components/` and ADD the missing arms: `EMPTY_DECOMPOSE_PLAN → t('plan.err_empty_plan')`, `BAD_REFERENCE → t('plan.err_bad_reference')`, `CONSTRAINT → e.message`. New en key: `"err_empty_plan": "The planner produced no scenes for any chapter — it likely degraded. Nothing was committed. Try again, or pick a different model."` (+ the 12 sibling locales via `scripts/i18n_translate.py`).

**(3) Also PREVENT the empty commit, don't just report it.** `EMPTY_DECOMPOSE_PLAN` is raised at COMMIT, so an all-empty preview tree can still be submitted today (`PlannerView.tsx:122` disables Commit only on `committing || needsReplace`). In the plan-hub port: disable Commit when `totalScenes === 0` and show the same `plan.err_empty_plan` prose inline under the preview tree (each chapter's `warning` from the preview says WHY). Keep the 400 handler as the backstop.

**(4) The 202 path must NOT reuse the legacy self-poller (PO-3 conflict).** `frontend/src/features/composition/api.ts:273-288` (`decomposePreview`) swallows the job by polling internally and throws the opaque literal `'decompose failed'` — that is exactly the banned "something went wrong". For M4b add a NEW `decomposeStart(projectId, body, token): Promise<{job_id: string}>` in the plan-hub api that returns the 202 envelope **without polling**; the drawer hands `job_id` to `ui_watch_job` → `job-detail` (PO-3), which renders the real failure reason. Leave the legacy `decomposePreview` untouched (legacy page still uses it). On job `completed`, `job.result` IS the `DecomposePreview` → render the preview tree → user accepts → `POST /works/{pid}/outline/decompose/commit` with `{replace, idempotency_key}`.

**Tests (Definition of Done for M4b):** vitest on the new hook — (a) 409 `CHAPTER_ALREADY_PLANNED` → `needsReplace = ['ch1']`, `confirmReplace()` re-POSTs with `replace: true` (mirror `usePlanner.test.tsx:91-98`); (b) 400 `EMPTY_DECOMPOSE_PLAN` → the rendered alert contains the human sentence and NOT the string `EMPTY_DECOMPOSE_PLAN`; (c) preview with 0 scenes → Commit is `disabled`; (d) api.ts unit test for the `.detail` picker. Plus `/review-impl` at wave close.

*Evidence:* services/composition-service/app/routers/plan.py:682-687 (400 EMPTY_DECOMPOSE_PLAN, prose under detail.detail) · plan.py:734-739 (**409** CHAPTER_ALREADY_PLANNED + chapter_ids — NOT a 400, spec 36 line ~415 is wrong) · plan.py:707-710 (guard runs inside the commit Tx → TOCTOU-closed, so a checkbox alone cannot gate it) · frontend/src/api.ts:152 `const picked = o.message ?? o.code;` (never reads `.detail` → the bare code leaks to the user) · frontend/src/features/composition/hooks/usePlanner.ts:38-48 + 115-133 (the 409→needsReplace→confirmReplace pattern to PORT) · frontend/src/features/composition/components/PlannerView.tsx:26-32 (`errorText` maps 4 codes, MISSES EMPTY_DECOMPOSE_PLAN) + :105-114 (replace prompt UI) + :122 (Commit not disabled on an empty tree) · frontend/src/i18n/locales/en/composition.json:416-419 (replace_* keys already exist) · frontend/src/features/composition/api.ts:273-288 (legacy self-poller throws 'decompose failed' — must NOT be reused; PO-3 requires ui_watch_job → job-detail) · target files: frontend/src/features/plan-hub/{hooks/useDecompose.ts (new), components/PlanDrawer.tsx, api.ts}

### Q-36-DEFERRED-MODEL-ROLES-DEFAULT-REF
DELETE the defer row D-WORK-MODEL-ROLES-DEFAULT-REF. Its premise is false on two counts, and the real residual work is 4 frontend lines that land INSIDE M4a — deferring them ships the exact F-EC4b write-only bug the plan congratulates itself for catching, only on the FE side.

FACT 1 — "8 scripts/eval_*.py still read the legacy scalar" is FALSE. No file named `scripts/eval_*.py` exists, and NOTHING under `scripts/` reads `settings.default_model_ref`. `grep -rn "default_model" scripts/` returns 6 hits, all of them the string `user_default_models` — a provider-registry TABLE, an unrelated concept (scripts/eval/tool_liveness/config.py:32, .../user_fixture.py:44, scripts/eval/run_discoverability_scenario.py:58, scripts/eval/discoverability_scenarios/README.md:107). OQ-8's author conflated `user_default_models` with `default_model_ref`. There is no eval-script blast radius. Gate #2 ("wider blast radius") therefore has nothing under it and the row is not defer-eligible.

FACT 2 — the backend has ZERO stale `default_model_ref` readers. Full non-test census across services/, scripts/, frontend/src/, contracts/: the ONLY backend hit is `internal_model_settings.py:59` — which IS the dual-read shim (legacy scalar → role `chat`), i.e. already the intended one-home fallback. The compose engine never reads it (it takes `model_ref` per call). So unlike `critic_model_ref` (7 engine sites → BE-21), the chat/composer scalar needs NO backend re-point at all.

WHAT IS ACTUALLY LEFT — 4 FRONTEND sites, and it is a HARD PREREQUISITE of EC-4, not a later slice. EC-4 (plan 30 line 390) replaces the "Default drafter model" select with a ModelPicker writing `settings.model_roles.composer`, and stops writing `default_model_ref` (SET-8: one writer). But three FE compose sites still key on the scalar and will read `undefined` → the book's drafter default silently vanishes on the M4a deploy for EVERY existing book. Fold this into M4a as slice FE-21b, run alongside BE-21:

1. NEW `frontend/src/features/composition/lib/modelRoles.ts` — one home for the FE dual-read, mirroring `_model_roles_from_settings` (internal_model_settings.py:46-65) exactly; do NOT re-write the fallback at each call site:
   `export function resolveModelRole(settings: Record<string, unknown> | undefined, role: 'chat'|'composer'|'planner'|'critic'): string | null`
   Precedence: `settings.model_roles[role].model_ref` → (for `composer` only) `settings.model_roles.chat.model_ref` → the legacy scalar (`default_model_ref` for chat|composer, `critic_model_ref` for critic) → null.
   The composer→chat hop is LOAD-BEARING: the BE shim maps the legacy scalar to role `chat` (internal_model_settings.py:61) while EC-4 writes `composer` — without the hop, every pre-M4a book loses its drafter default.

2. Re-point the 3 readers at it (role `composer`), preserving each site's existing downstream logic verbatim:
   - `frontend/src/features/composition/components/CompositionPanel.tsx:310` → `const defaultModelRef = resolveModelRole(work.settings, 'composer') ?? '';` (keep the `defaultIsAvailable` stale-model guard and the `inheritedChatModel` / `guided.soleModelId` cascade at :317-321 untouched)
   - `frontend/src/features/studio/panels/EditorPanel.tsx:199` → `const persistedDefaultModel = resolveModelRole(composeWork?.settings, 'composer');`
   - `frontend/src/pages/ChapterEditorPage.tsx:243` → identical change.

3. `frontend/src/features/composition/components/CompositionSettingsView.tsx:30,47` — EC-4's own work: the `default_model_ref` select becomes the ModelPicker writing `model_roles.composer`. After EC-4 there must be ZERO writers of `default_model_ref` in frontend/src (grep is the check).

4. ONE-LINE BE companion in `_model_roles_from_settings` (internal_model_settings.py:59-61): have the legacy `default_model_ref` fill BOTH `chat` and `composer` when the map sets neither. The user's "Default drafter model" IS the book's composer; today book-tier `composer` is always empty, so chat-service (settings_resolution.ModelRole.COMPOSER) falls through to account tier and the book setting is invisible to it. Additive, back-compat-safe.

TESTS (M4a DoD):

### Q-36-DERIVE-503-PROJECT-CREATE
BUILD IT AS SPEC'D, and fix the FE trap that would otherwise make "surface it verbatim" impossible. No backend change — every code already exists.

(1) THE TRAP (this is why the concern is real). `apiJson` at frontend/src/api.ts:159-163 throws `Object.assign(new Error(msg), { status, code: err?.code, body })` where `err?.code` is the **top-level** body `code`. FastAPI/composition never sends that — it raises `detail={"code": "..."}`. So `err.code` is `undefined` for EVERY composition error. The code lives at `err.body.detail.code`; `err.message` only happens to equal the raw token because of the `o.message ?? o.code` pick at api.ts:150-154. **Builder MUST read `err.body?.detail?.code`, with `err.status` as fallback discriminator. Never `err.code`.**

(2) NEW FILE `frontend/src/features/composition/hooks/deriveError.ts`: export `deriveErrorCode(e: unknown): string | undefined` => `(e as {body?:{detail?:{code?:string}}})?.body?.detail?.code`, and `deriveErrorMessage(e, t): string` switching on it. Map ALL FOUR derive failures (works.py:355/359/373/375), not just the 503 — same fix, same file, and a bare `PROJECT_CREATE_FAILED` string is just as user-hostile:
  - `PROJECT_CREATE_UNAVAILABLE` (503) -> "Couldn't create the dị bản: the knowledge service returned no project (PROJECT_CREATE_UNAVAILABLE). Nothing was created — try again in a moment."
  - `PROJECT_CREATE_FAILED` (502) -> "Couldn't create the dị bản: the knowledge service rejected the request (PROJECT_CREATE_FAILED). Nothing was created."
  - `BOOK_SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE` (502) -> "Couldn't reach the book service (BOOK_SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE). Nothing was created."
  - `SOURCE_WORK_NOT_BACKED` (409) -> "This Work has no knowledge project yet (SOURCE_WORK_NOT_BACKED) — open it once to finish setup, then derive."
  - fallback -> the existing generic message.
"Verbatim" = the literal code token appears in the rendered sentence (so a bug report is greppable), wrapped in a human sentence. Copy lives in `frontend/src/i18n/locales/en/studio.json` under a new `divergence.error.*` block.

(3) WIRE IT: in `useDivergenceWizard.ts`, replace the `error:` field's `(derive.error as Error)?.message ?? 'derive failed'` with `derive.isError ? deriveErrorMessage(derive.error, t) : null`. The wizard's Step-4 view renders it inline; `isSubmitting` already exists.

(4) ARCHIVE = SOFT DELETE, and the copy is VERIFIED TRUE (do not soften it, do not imply destruction). `status` is a plain column and `resolve_by_book` filters `WHERE book_id=$1 AND status='active'` (db/repositories/works.py:268) — chapters and the knowledge project_id are untouched. ConfirmDialog body verbatim per spec 36 line 375: "Archive this dị bản? Its chapters and knowledge partition are kept; it disappears from this list." Confirm button label "Archive" — the word "Delete"/"Remove"/"Permanently" must not appear.

(5) ARCHIVE 412: call it as `patchWork(pid, { status: 'archived' }, token, { ifMatch: String(work.version) })` — the optional 4th arg added by EC-4b/BE-18 at frontend/src/features/composition/api.ts:443 (per-call-site If-Match; do NOT put it on the shared writer — useWorldMap would self-412 mid-drag). On `err.status === 412`: refetch the works list, re-seed `version` from the response, and set the error to `t('sceneRail.stale')` — **reuse the EXISTING key** `sceneRail.stale` at frontend/src/i18n/locales/en/studio.json:488 ("changed elsewhere — reloaded"), the same key SceneRail.tsx:63 renders. Do NOT re-type the literal string into a new key: a duplicated shared string drifts (memory: css-var-duplicated-across-two-consumers-drifts).

(6) TESTS (all in M3's wave; /review-impl at wave close):
  a. `useDivergenceWizard.test.tsx`: mock `deriveWork` rejecting with `Object.assign(new Error('x'), { status: 503, body: { detail: { code: 'PROJECT_CREATE_UNAVAILABLE' } } })`; assert `result.current.error` matches /PROJECT_CREATE_UNAVAILABLE/ **and** does not equal 'derive failed'. This test is the one that would have caught the `err.code === undefined` trap. Repeat for the 502/409 codes.
  b. Divergence-panel test: archive confirm text matches /chapters and knowledge partition are kept/ and does NOT match /delete|permanently|destroy/i.
  c. Archive-412 test: `patchWork` rejects with `{status:412, body:{detail:{code:'WORK_VERSION_CONFLICT', current:{...version: 2}}}}` -> rendered error is exactly the `sceneRail.stale` value, the list is refetched, and a retry sends `If-Match: 2`.

DEFAULT THE PO CAN VETO: I kept the machine code token inside the user-facing sentence (that is what "surface verbatim" buys — an actionable bug report). If the PO prefers a code-free sentence, drop the parenthetical; everything else stands.

*Evidence:* services/composition-service/app/routers/works.py:375 (`raise HTTPException(status_code=503, detail={"code": "PROJECT_CREATE_UNAVAILABLE"})`; siblings at :355 SOURCE_WORK_NOT_BACKED, :359 BOOK_SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE, :373 PROJECT_CREATE_FAILED) · works.py:603-607 (412 `{"code":"WORK_VERSION_CONFLICT","current":…}`) · frontend/src/api.ts:159-163 (`code: err?.code` reads the TOP-LEVEL body key — undefined for FastAPI's `detail:{code}`; the code is at `err.body.detail.code`, message picked at api.ts:150-154) · frontend/src/features/composition/hooks/useDivergenceWizard.ts `error:` field (`(derive.error as Error)?.message ?? 'derive failed'`) · services/composition-service/app/db/repositories/works.py:268 (`WHERE book_id = $1 AND status = 'active'` — proves archive is soft) · frontend/src/i18n/locales/en/studio.json:488 (`"stale": "changed elsewhere — reloaded"`) + frontend/src/features/studio/manuscript/SceneRail.tsx:63 (412 -> `t('sceneRail.stale')`) · frontend/src/features/composition/api.ts:443 (`patchWork(projectId, patch, token)` — needs the EC-4b optional `{ ifMatch }` 4th arg) · spec 36 lines 375-378 (the verbatim copy).

### Q-36-DEFERRED-DIVERGENCE-MCP

Nothing structural is missing; this is CLAUDE.md's "missing infrastructure is unbuilt work, not a blocker" case.

1.    - `composition_list_derivatives(book_id)` → `_gate(tc, book_id, GrantLevel.VIEW)` then `WorksRepo.resolve_by_book(book_id)` (`app/db/repositories/works.py:250`); split canonical (`source_work_id IS NULL`) vs derivatives; per derivative attach `DerivativesRepo.get_spec_for_work` (taxonomy/pov_anchor/canon_rule) + `len(list_overrides_for_work)` as `override_count`. This is the LIST plan 30 BE-13 called absent — the repo method exists; only the projection is new. Synonyms: ["list dị bản","what-if versions","alternate universes","derivatives of this book"].
   - `composition_derivative_context(project_id)` → mirror `GET /works/{project_id}/derivative-context` (`works.py:443-470`): `works.get` → `_gate_book(..., VIEW)` → `build_derivative_context` + `get_spec_for_work`. Return `{is_derivative:false}` for a greenfield Work, exactly as the route does.

3. ONE WRITE TOOL, Tier W, mirroring `composition_motif_adopt` (`server.py:2896-2955`) — copy that function's shape, do not invent one:
   - `composition_derive_work(source_project_id, branch_point?, taxonomy, pov_anchor?, canon_rule[], entity_overrides[])`, args as `ForbidExtra`; `taxonomy` MUST be a `Literal[...]` closed set matching `DivergenceSpecBody` (Frontend-Tool-Contract IN-rule).

Return `{confirm_token, descriptor, title:"Create a dị bản (derivative work)", domain:"composition", preview:{source_title, branch_point, taxonomy, canon_rule_count, override_count, forks_knowledge_partition:true, reversible:"archive only — a derivative has no delete"}}`. NO `_precheck_or_402`: derive makes zero LLM calls (`works.py:310-406`), so it is an irreversibility gate, not a spend gate — say so in the tool description.
   - REGISTER the descriptor `composition.derive_work` in BOTH descriptor blocks (`app/mcp/server.py:104-127` and `app/routers/actions.py:64-100`) and add it to `_ALL_DESCRIPTORS` (`actions.py:96`) — a descriptor missing from `_ALL_DESCRIPTORS` is a silent 400.
   - CONFIRM branch in `actions.py::confirm_action`, inserted next to the `_MOTIF_ADOPT_DESCRIPTOR` branch (`actions.py:259`), because derive is BOOK-scoped like adopt, not Work-scoped: re-resolve the source, `authorize_book(grant, source.book_id, envelope_user, GrantLevel.EDIT)` (a grant revoked between propose and confirm stops the fork), `await _claim_or_replay(token, claims)` (the replay ledger — WITHOUT it a double-confirm mints TWO knowledge partitions), then `derive_work_core(..., bearer=mint_service_bearer(envelope_user, settings.jwt_secret))` — the same seam `server.py:583` already uses to reach knowledge-service. Return `{"outcome":"action_done","project_id":…,"work":…}`.

4. SPEC EDIT (the "confirm design" the row asked for is ONE TABLE ROW, not a spine): add to the AN-8 edit-discipline table in `docs/specs/2026-07-01-writing-studio/28_agent_native_studio.md:466` a row — object class **Work (derivative)** · channel `composition_derive_work` · tier **W (propose→confirm, no spend)** · undo **archive (`PATCH /works {status:'archived'}`) — there is no delete; the confirm preview must say so**. Cite this adjudication.

5. TESTS (`services/composition-service/tests/test_mcp_divergence_tools.py`, `pytestmark = pytest.mark.xdist_group("pg")`):
   a. propose returns a token + descriptor `composition.derive_work` and creates **no** Work row and **no** knowledge project (assert the `create_project` client is never called) — the "nothing until confirm" law;
   b. confirm creates a derivative whose `project_id != source.project_id` and persists spec + overrides;
   c. **replay**: confirming the same token twice returns the ledger result and calls `knowledge.create_project` exactly ONCE (this is the bug the row was afraid of; the ledger is the answer);
   d. EDIT grant revoked between propose and confirm → 403, no row;
   e. knowledge outage at confirm → 503 `PROJECT_CREATE_UNAVAILABLE`, no Work row (txn);
   f. `composition_list_derivatives` / `composition_derivative_context` return the same shape as their REST siblings; a non-grantee gets the uniform not-accessible (no oracle).
   Run: `python -m pytest tests -q -n auto --dist loadgroup`. Wave DoD includes `/review-impl` per the run policy.

### Q-36-COMPOSITION-SECTION-OWN-SAVE-PATH
AFFIRMED as stated — the spec's constraint is correct in all four clauses and is confirmed by code. Build it exactly so:

(1) PLACEMENT — port `features/composition/components/CompositionSettingsView.tsx` (99 LOC) into a new `frontend/src/features/composition/components/CompositionSettingsSection.tsx` exporting `<CompositionSettingsSection bookId: string />`. Mount it in `frontend/src/pages/book-tabs/SettingsTab.tsx` immediately AFTER the `<BookWorldSection/>` block (currently SettingsTab.tsx:356-361) and BEFORE the final `<Divider/>` + save bar, preceded by its own `<Divider/>` + `<SectionHeader>{t('settings.composition')}</SectionHeader>`. Do NOT add it to StudioDock/catalog.ts and do NOT touch the panel-id enum: `book-settings` is ALREADY registered (catalog.ts:224) and already in the BE closed set (frontend_tools.py:402), and `BookSettingsPanel` is a pure pass-through wrapper (BookSettingsPanel.tsx:47-54), so mounting in SettingsTab gives the CLASSIC book page and the Studio panel simultaneously — the +3 panel-ids stay style-voice / reference-shelf / divergence only.

(2) OWN SAVE PATH — the section keeps CompositionSettingsView's existing per-control instant commit through `useSetWorkSettings` (hooks/useWork.ts:131) → `compositionApi.patchWork` → `PATCH /v1/composition/works/{projectId}`. Do NOT add its fields to SettingsTab's `isDirty` (SettingsTab.tsx:88-93) and do NOT add them to `handleSave` (SettingsTab.tsx:229-243) — those are book-service fields going to `booksApi.patchBook`. Two resources, two services, two saves; this is the exact shape `BookWorldSection` already uses (self-saving section, `onChanged` callback, absent from the dirty bar).

(3) SELF-CONTAINMENT (the gap the spec text leaves implicit) — the section takes only `bookId`, so it resolves everything else itself: `projectId` via `useWorkResolution(bookId, token)` (hooks/useWork.ts:7) and the model list via `useUserModels({ capability: 'chat' })` (pattern at CompositionPanel.tsx:180). If `useWorkResolution` returns no Work (greenfield book), render the section's controls DISABLED with a one-line "Set up the co-writer on this book to configure composition" hint — do NOT implicitly `useCreateWork`; minting a Work is a user action, not a side effect of opening Settings.

(4) SERIALIZE THE WRITES (falls directly out of "its own save path") — `patchWork` REPLACES the whole settings blob (api.ts:441-443) and sends NO `If-Match`, while the controls instant-commit. Two rapid toggles both merge from the same stale cached `settings` and the second silently drops the first (this repo's known instant-commit-over-a-replace-blob bug class). Chain the mutations: hold a promise ref and `await` the in-flight patch before building the next merge from the freshly-invalidated `settings` (or disable all controls while `setSettings.isPending`, which CompositionSettingsView already does per-control — extend it to the whole section).

TESTS: (a) extend `frontend/src/pages/book-tabs/__tests__/` with a SettingsTab test asserting the composition controls render AND that toggling one does NOT set the book form dirty (save bar stays disabled) — that is the "two saves" invariant made mechanical; (b) a CompositionSettingsSection test asserting two rapid toggles produce two patches where the SECOND body contains BOTH keys (the serialization regression); (c) a BookSettingsPanel test asserting the section appears through the wrapper (proves the GG-1 both-surfaces claim). Leave `CompositionSettingsView.tsx` in place for the legacy CompositionPanel (GG-4: the legacy page is not deleted this wave) — or have it delegate to the new section to avoid a fork.

DEFAULT I AM PICKING (veto-able): the greenfield no-Work state is a disabled section, not an auto-create.

*Evidence:* frontend/src/features/studio/panels/catalog.ts:224 (`book-settings` already a registered panel) · services/chat-service/app/services/frontend_tools.py:402 (`book-settings` already in the panel-id enum → not part of the +3) · frontend/src/features/studio/panels/BookSettingsPanel.tsx:47-54 (thin DOCK-2 wrapper: renders `<SettingsTab bookId book onReload onOpenWorld/>` and nothing else) · frontend/src/pages/book-tabs/SettingsTab.tsx:356-361 (`BookWorldSection` = the existing self-saving-section precedent) vs SettingsTab.tsx:88-93 (`isDirty` covers book fields only) and SettingsTab.tsx:229-243 (`handleSave` → `booksApi.patchBook` only) · frontend/src/features/composition/api.ts:441-443 (`patchWork` → `PATCH /v1/composition/works/{projectId}`, server REPLACES the settings blob, no If-Match) · frontend/src/features/composition/hooks/useWork.ts:131-139 (`useSetWorkSettings` merge-patch, the section's own save path) and useWork.ts:7-13 (`useWorkResolution(bookId)` → the projectId the section needs) · frontend/src/features/composition/components/CompositionSettingsView.tsx:1-99 (the 99-LOC component being ported; already instant-commit, no dirty bar) · docs/specs/2026-07-01-writing-studio/36_editor_craft_ports.md:48 (the port row) and :6 (Composition is a SECTION in the existing `book-settings` panel, not a new panel)

NOT a design question — a mechanical work item, and the code confirms every named command works as the spec states. Bake this exact 5-step recipe into each of M1/M2/M3's Definition of Done (panel ids: `style-voice`, `reference-shelf`, `divergence`):

2) **17 locales — run the script, NO `--force`:**
   `python scripts/i18n_translate.py --ns studio`
   It is **gap-fill** (`i18n_translate.py:341-357`): it carries every existing valid translation and translates ONLY the new keys. Do **not** pass `--force` (that re-translates the whole studio namespace × 17 locales and clobbers prior hand-fixes) and do **not** pass `--langs` (all 17 is the default). Never hand-write a locale value.

Write defer row **D-36-I18N-LOCALES** (gate 4, blocked-on-external: needs a local model process) and keep going; drain it in one batched `--ns studio` run at the end of the wave. Check any residual `frontend/src/i18n/locales/<lang>/_FAILED.json` before closing the wave.

   `WRITE_FRONTEND_CONTRACT=1 python -m pytest tests/test_frontend_tools_contract.py` (this **skips** by design — it writes the file, `test_frontend_tools_contract.py:135-140`), then **re-run it WITHOUT the env var** and require green — that second run is the only proof `contracts/frontend-tools.contract.json` matches the live schemas.

5) **One commit.** `contracts/frontend-tools.contract.json` + `frontend_tools.py` + `catalog.ts` + `en/studio.json` (+ the 17 locale files if step 2 ran) land in the SAME commit — a split commit leaves `panelCatalogContract.test.ts` red on the intermediate HEAD.

Do this once in M1; M2/M3 then get it for free. Per the repo's "checklist ⇒ test the effect" rule, that converts step 1 from a checklist item into a machine-checked one.

  scene:   'bg-indigo-50 text-indigo-700 border-indigo-200'   // mirrors `session`
  chapter: 'bg-violet-50 text-violet-700 border-violet-200'   // mirrors `book`
  work:    'bg-teal-50 text-teal-700 border-teal-200'         // mirrors `account`
  neutral: 'bg-muted text-muted-foreground border-border'     // mirrors `no_model_configured`

  scene: 'this scene' · chapter: 'this chapter' · work: 'this work' · neutral: 'unset'

TITLE:
  scene:   'Set on this scene — overrides the chapter and work profiles.'
  chapter: "Inherited from this chapter's profile."
  work:    "Inherited from the work's profile."
  neutral: 'No row at any scope — the packer adds no density/pace directive.'

No shared-ui extraction is warranted for a 2nd consumer.

Belt-and-braces: assert `Object.keys(CLS) === Object.keys(LABEL) === Object.keys(TITLE)` (three-way key equality) so the next tier added to one map cannot silently skip the other two. Put the test with the style-voice panel; `features/chat/components/__tests__/SessionSettingsPanel.tiers.test.tsx` is the existing sibling pattern to copy.

- **Q-36-PREFERENCES-ARBITRARY-KEY** — Already answered by the code: `/v1/me/preferences` is an OPEN key/value JSONB store with NO schema/enum — arbitrary namespaced keys are accepted today. There is NO unenumerated BE prerequisite for M3; do not add a BE slice.

Proof chain: `user_preferences` is `(user_id UUID PK, prefs JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '{}')` with no key constraint (services/auth-service/internal/migrate/migrate.go:63-67). `patchPreferences` decodes ONLY `{"prefs": json.RawMessage}` — zero key validation — and merges `prefs = user_preferences.prefs || $2` (services/auth-service/internal/api/handlers.go:847-864). The FE helpers already take an arbitrary string key (frontend/src/lib/syncPrefs.ts:8,23,41), and a dotted namespaced key is ALREADY shipped in production: `modelPicker.recents.${capability}` (frontend/src/components/model-picker/recents.ts:13-14). Gateway routing exists (services/api-gateway-bff/src/gateway-setup.ts:69,578).

BUILDER INSTRUCTION (M3, FE-only):
1. Use a FLAT TOP-LEVEL key — the literal string `lw_active_work.${bookId}` — exactly as EC-3d/OQ-7 spell it. Persist with `savePrefToServer(\`lw_active_work.${bookId}\`, { work_id, updated_at }, token)`; restore on Studio mount with `loadPrefFromServer<{work_id: string; updated_at: string}>(\`lw_active_work.${bookId}\`, token)` (both from `frontend/src/lib/syncPrefs.ts`). Use the awaitable `savePrefToServer` (not fire-and-forget `syncPrefsToServer`) so the 'survives a reload' DoD can order the reload after the durable write.
2. DO NOT nest as `{"lw_active_work": {"<book_id>": ...}}`. The PATCH merge is Postgres `||` — a SHALLOW top-level merge — so a nested shape means a PATCH for book B REPLACES the whole `lw_active_work` object and silently drops book A's entry. This is the only real hazard in this item and it is invisible to a single-book test.
3. DoD test must assert the flat-key shape, not just single-book survival: switch work on book A -> switch work on book B -> reload -> assert BOTH `lw_active_work.<A>` and `lw_active_work.<B>` are present and correct. (A single-book reload test passes under the buggy nested shape.)
4. Per-device-only fallback stays localStorage-cached but server is SSOT (CLAUDE.md Data Persistence Rules); mirror the read-through/write-through pattern in `frontend/src/components/model-picker/recents.ts` — including its `cacheKey` user-id scoping so user A's cached active-work never leaks into user B's session on a shared browser.

Sane default noted for PO veto: keys accumulate one per book with no GC. That is a few bytes per book in a JSONB blob — deliberately NOT pruning in v1.
- **Q-36-AN8-TABLE-TWO-NEW-CLASSES** — WORK ITEM, already decided — no open question. Spec 36 states the instruction verbatim and PO-1 sets the precedent (amend spec 28 in place, do not fork). The two classes follow the existing Tier-A convention exactly, so this is an ADDITION, not an amendment: no PO sign-off needed, no new confirmation convention.

BUILDER INSTRUCTION (do this IN THE SAME COMMIT as BE-10, per spec 36:504):

1. EDIT `docs/specs/2026-07-01-writing-studio/28_agent_native_studio.md`. In the AN-8 edit-discipline table (§"Edit discipline — the safety contract", table at :472-484), insert TWO rows IMMEDIATELY AFTER the **Steering rules** row (:479) and BEFORE the **Lockfile** row (:480). The Steering row is the template — same Tier, same grant, same undo shape:

| **Style profile** (`style_profile` — density/pace, scoped work\|chapter\|scene) | `composition_style_upsert` / `_delete` (36 BE-10) | A (EDIT grant) | `undo_hint` carries the prior row (re-upsert) — or `composition_style_delete` when the upsert CREATED the row. No version column ⇒ no OCC; last-writer-wins by design |
| **Voice profile** (`voice_profile` — per-character voice tags) | `composition_voice_upsert` / `_delete` (36 BE-10) | A (EDIT grant) | `undo_hint` carries the prior/deleted row (re-upsert) — or `composition_voice_delete` when the upsert CREATED the row. No version column ⇒ no OCC |

2. Do NOT touch the invariant sentence below the table ("no tool in this spec's gap layer introduces a new row") — it is scoped to spec 28's OWN gap layer, and these rows come from spec 36. Leave it as-is.

3. The load-bearing consequence for BE-10's CODE (not just the doc): because neither table has a version column, `composition_style_upsert` / `composition_voice_upsert` MUST read-before-write to build an honest `_meta.undo_hint` via `_undo(...)` (mcp/server.py:181-183):
   - prior row EXISTS → `_undo("composition_style_upsert", project_id=…, scope_type=…, scope_id=…, density=<OLD>, pace=<OLD>)` (voice: `entity_id`, `entity_name`, `tags=<OLD>`)
   - prior row ABSENT → `_undo("composition_style_delete", project_id=…, scope_type=…, scope_id=…)` (voice: `.../voice-profiles/{entity_id}`)
   - `_delete` on a row that existed → `_undo("composition_*_upsert", …deleted row's values…)`; on a no-op delete (`removed: false`) → `_meta.undo_hint = None` (honest null, per plan 30 §8.1: "honestly `None` where no faithful inverse exists").
   An upsert that emits a blanket re-upsert hint WITHOUT reading the prior row would resurrect a row the user never had — a fake inverse, which is the AN-8 defect class.

4. TEST (make the doc row testable, per the checklist⇒test-the-effect law): in composition-service MCP tests, assert BOTH branches — upsert-over-existing returns an undo_hint whose tool is `composition_style_upsert` and whose args carry the OLD density/pace; upsert-creating-new returns an undo_hint whose tool is `composition_style_delete`. Same pair for voice. Round-trip: applying the undo_hint restores the pre-call `list` output byte-for-byte.

DEFAULT I PICKED (veto-able): TWO rows, not one merged "Style/voice profiles" row — spec 36 says "gains TWO object classes" and they have different keys (scope_type+scope_id vs entity_id) and different delete routes, so one row would hide a real difference.
- **Q-36-WORK-SETTINGS-MCP-WONTFIX** — Already answered by the code + the sealed AN-8 contract, and already recorded in spec 36 itself (line 496). The won't-fix STANDS and needs no new defer row. Builder instruction for Wave 6:

1) DO NOT create `composition_update_work` — or any MCP tool that writes `composition_work.settings` — now or later. The agent's only work-settings channel stays Tier-R `composition_get_work` (server.py:284). Verified in code: `composition_create_work` (server.py:647) takes ONLY `(book_id, project_id)` — no `settings` param — so there is currently ZERO agent write path to settings, and grepping `critic_model_ref|reference_embed_model_ref|capture_correction_prose` across every service's `app/mcp/` returns zero hits. The won't-fix is not aspirational; it is the code's actual state, and the job is to keep it that way.

2) Rationale that binds a future builder: the blob holds BYOK MODEL REFS (`critic_model_ref`, `reference_embed_model_ref`) — spend-causing, user-owned choices. AN-8 (28_agent_native_studio.md:466-490) enumerates every agent-touchable object class (prose, spec objects, steering, lockfile, registry, glossary, KG, generation, reads); settings is deliberately NOT a row. Adding a settings write tool would mint a new write class, which AN-8 explicitly says "a reviewer finding a new confirmation convention here has found a defect."

3) The write path is the GUI, per GG-1 (the human surface is the door): F-EC4's Composition section in the existing `book-settings` panel, exposing all 7 keys with effective value + source tier (SET-1..8). This does NOT violate GG-2 (the inverse law) — GG-2 fires only when a domain has NO agent tools; `composition_get_work` gives the agent read access, so it can advise on settings while the user makes the change.

4) ANTI-RESURFACING (the one concrete edit this item earns — do it in the Wave 6 slice that touches work settings): add a comment block immediately after the `composition_get_work` handler in `services/composition-service/app/mcp/server.py` (~line 302, at the point of temptation where the next agent would add the sibling write tool), reading: "# NO composition_update_work — CONSCIOUS WON'T-FIX (spec 36 F-EC4; AN-8 gives settings no agent channel). The settings blob holds BYOK model refs (critic_model_ref, reference_embed_model_ref) = the user's own spend choices. Writes go through the book-settings GUI only. If an agent channel is ever wanted, it must be Tier-W propose->confirm (an FE card), never a direct tool." A future agent reads server.py, not the spec — this is what actually stops it re-surfacing.

5) OUT OF SCOPE HERE: the full-blob REPLACE at the REST layer is a REAL bug but is already tracked as BE-18 — do not fold it into this item. NOTE FOR THE BUILDER: BE-18's cited path is wrong. The file is `services/composition-service/app/db/repositories/works.py:311-313` (`set_clauses.append(f"settings = ${len(params)}::jsonb")`), NOT `app/repositories/works.py`. Today nothing is lost only because every FE caller hand-merges (`frontend/src/features/composition/hooks/useWork.ts:135` spreads `...v.currentSettings`).

DEFAULT THE PO MAY VETO: if they ever DO want an agent to change settings, the sanctioned shape is a Tier-W propose->confirm FE card (human clicks Apply), not a direct write tool. Not v1.

- **Q-36-DO-NOT-TOUCH-LIST** — The fence is CORRECT as written — the code confirms every clause, so there is nothing to decide. Builder instruction, verbatim:

1. **DO NOT edit these 6 files in Wave 6 (spec 36):** `frontend/src/features/studio/components/StudioDock.tsx`, `.../components/StudioFrame.tsx`, `.../palette/useStudioCommands.ts`, `.../panels/UserGuidePanel.tsx`, `.../agent/studioUiNav.ts`, `.../agent/useStudioUiToolExecutor.ts`. The first four are pure consumers of `panels/catalog.ts` (verified imports at StudioDock.tsx:9, StudioFrame.tsx:17, useStudioCommands.ts:4, UserGuidePanel.tsx:10) — adding the 3 catalog rows (`style-voice`, `reference-shelf`, `divergence`) + their i18n `titleKey`/`descKey`/`guideBodyKey` in the `studio` locale namespace makes all four pick the panels up for free (dock mount, palette command, user-guide row). The last two are panel-id-agnostic. If you find yourself editing one of these six, STOP: you have introduced a per-panel special case where the catalog was supposed to be the only registry (that is a DOCK-1 violation, and `/review-impl` should flag it).

2. **Registration step 7 (`host/studioLinks.ts`): SKIP — do not add rows.** No external URL resolves to these panels: `PATH_PANELS` (studioLinks.ts:46) maps bare app paths only, and `App.tsx:109-136` gives chapters exactly five routes (`/read`, `/edit`, `/compare`, `/translations`, `/review/:versionId`) — the composition sub-tabs have never been URL-addressable, and `/edit` is already absorbed by `CHAPTER_RE` → `host.focusManuscriptUnit`. (Default I am setting, so the builder does not stall on it: IF a later wave introduces a notification `metadata.link` that must land on one of these panels, that is an additive one-line `PATH_PANELS` row at that time — not Wave 6 work.)

3. **Registration step 9 (tours): SKIP.** `frontend/src/features/studio/onboarding/` contains zero references to the three new panel ids; none of them is a role-tour step in v1.

4. **Registration step 10 (`host/types.ts`) IS in scope — the single exception, and only in M3 (EC-3d).** Today the bus has no active-Work concept: `StudioContextSlice` carries only `activeChapterId`/`activeSceneId` (types.ts:36-37), the reducer state the same (types.ts:73-74), and `StudioBusEvent` has no `work` variant. M3 adds `activeWorkProjectId` to the slice + state, a `{ type: 'work'; projectId: string }` bus event + its reducer arm, and hydrates it on mount from `/v1/me/preferences` key `lw_active_work.<book_id>` (OQ-7 answer — never `work.settings`, which is per-book/shared). Change this file ONCE, in M3, and make all 7 consumer sites read `useActiveWork(bookId)`.

5. **Make the fence mechanical, not a promise (add this literal step to every wave's Definition of Done, since the PO policy says "an item is DONE only when a test asserts its effect"):** run
   `git diff --name-only main...HEAD -- frontend/src/features/studio/components/StudioDock.tsx frontend/src/features/studio/components/StudioFrame.tsx frontend/src/features/studio/palette/useStudioCommands.ts frontend/src/features/studio/panels/UserGuidePanel.tsx frontend/src/features/studio/agent/studioUiNav.ts frontend/src/features/studio/agent/useStudioUiToolExecutor.ts frontend/src/features/studio/host/studioLinks.ts`
   and require EMPTY output. Non-empty = the wave is not done; either revert the edit and push the change into `catalog.ts`, or (if the edit is genuinely necessary) it is a spec-36 scope breach that must be raised, not absorbed. `host/types.ts` is deliberately absent from that list — it is the sanctioned M3 exception.
